ĪPrVV_1,1.0	nirābhāsāt pūrṇāt aham iti purā bhāsayati yat dvi śākhām āśāste tadanu ca vibhaṅktum nija kalām sva rūpāt unmeṣa prasaraṇa nimeṣa sthiti juṣaḥ tad advaitam vande parama śiva śakti ātma nikhilam śrotraiyambaka sat vaṃśa madhya mukta āmaya sthiteḥ śrosoma ānanda nāthasya vijñāna pratibimbakam anuttara ānanya sākṣi pum artha upāyam abhyadhāt īśvara pratyabhijñā ākhyam yaḥ śāstram yat su nirmalam tad praśiṣyaḥ karomi etām tad sūtra vivṛtim laghum buddhvā abhinavaguptaḥ aham śrīmat lakṣmaṇa guptataḥ vṛttyā tātparyam ṭīkayā tad vicāraḥ sūtreṣu eteṣu granthakāreṇa dṛbdham tasmāt sūtra artham manda buddhīn pratīttham samyak vyākhyāsye pratyabhijñā viviktyai sarvatra alpa matau yat vā kutra api su mahā dhiyi na vā anyatra api tu sva ātmani eṣā syāt upakāriṇī 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^1	 granthakāraḥ aparokṣam ātma dṛṣṭa śaktikām parameśvara tanmaya tām paratra saṃcikramayiṣuḥ sva tādātmya samarpaṇa pūrvam avighnena tad sampattim manyamānaḥ parameśvara utkarṣa prahvata aparāmarśa śeṣa tayā parameśvara tādātmya yogya tā āpādana buddhyā prayojanam āsūtrayati kathaṃcid āsādya maheśvarasya dāsyam janasya api upakāram icchan samasta saṃpad samavāpti hetum tad pratyabhijñām upapādayāmi iha prameśvaram prati yā iyam kāya vāc manasām tad eka viṣaya tā niyojanā lakṣaṇā prahvatā sā namaskārasya arthaḥ sā ca tathā kartum ucitā prāmāṇikasya bhavati yadi sarvatas namaskaraṇīyasya utkarṣam paśyet anyathā yuktim aparāmṛśataḥ aparama arthe api namaskāra udyatasya sāṃsārika jana madhya pāti tvam eva yathā uktam na vindanti param devam vidyā rāgeṇa rañjitāḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^2	 tāvati hi māyīyā śuddha vidyā rāga kalā saṃcāryamāṇasya paśu tvam eva itara apekṣayā tu katipaya adhva uttīrṇa tayā samutkarṣaḥ api syāt tat uktam kasya nāma karaṇaiḥ akṛtrimaiḥ paśyataḥ tava vibhūtimakṣatām vibhramāt avarataḥ api jāyate tvām vyudasya vara da stuti spṛhā iti śrīmat vidyā adhipatinā etaḥ ca āgama kāṇḍe nirūpayiṣyāmaḥ tasmāt nikhila utkarṣa parāmarśanam api tatra svīkāryam yadi api āyāta dṛḍha īśvara śaktipātasya svayam eva iyam iyatī paramaśiva bhūmiḥ abhyeti hṛdaya gocaram na tu atra svātmīyaḥ puruṣakāraḥ kaḥ api nirvahati sarvasya tasya māyā maya tvena andhatamasa prakhyasya āmāyī iyam śuddha prakāśam sva pratidvandvinam prati upāyat anupapatteḥ vajigamiṣayā niḥśeṣa utkarṣa viśeṣa abhidhīyijayati ādi śabda anuvedhena parāmarśanīyam iti namaskāre ākṣepyaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^3	 jaya pada udīraṇe api tādṛśa samutkarṣa atiśaya śālini sva ātmānam aprahvīkurvāṇasya taṭasthasya paramanātma upakāri tvam iti samutkarṣa viśeṣa ākṣiptaḥ eva namaskāraḥ avaśyam abhyantarī kāryaḥ iti anayā yuktyā jaya namaskāra ekatara prakrame anyatarasya artha ākṣipta tā avaśyam aṅgīkartavyā vandana na mana smaraṇa pradhyāna prabhṛtīnām api namaskāra jayati artha mātra parama artha tvāt iyam eva vartanī atra ayam punar grantha kṛtā tādṛś prakramaḥ āśritaḥ yatra dvayam api idam sva śabda parāmṛṣṭam eva etat ca padārtha vyākhyāna avasaraḥ eva prakaṭībhaviṣyati sva śabda parāmarśaḥ ca sarva jana hita tvāt yukti yuktaḥ sa hi sarvasya eva jhaṭiti hṛdayaṃgamaḥ artha ākṣiptaḥ tu katicid eva prati sva pratibhodita vāc tattva avamarśa asaṃbhavāt vāc tattva avamarśa śūnyasya ca prakāśasya aprakāśa kalpa tvāt etat ca sphuṭībhaviṣyati 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^4	 abhiprāyeṇa prasiddha jaya namaḥ prabhṛti śabda śaṭyāna āśleṣeṇa imām saraṇim anusarasi sma granthakāraḥ iha yat yat kiṃcana sphurati tad tad vakṣyamāṇa īśvara rūpa sva ātma prathā mātram tatra tu upāya upeya bhāva prabhṛtiḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ api yathāprakāśam parama artha bhūtaḥ eva prakāśasya anapahnavanīya tvāt yat āha bhaṭṭativākara vat saḥ viveka añjane prakāśaśva eva bhāvānām ityādi na śāpa uktyā vilīyate iti antam tatra tu kārya kāraṇa bhāve api kvacid paripūrṇa svātantrya lakṣaṇa māheśvarī ana antarīya ka tā kroḍīkṛta ananta śakti cakra cumbita bhāva bhāvita prathā antara vyacadhānam cakāsti sa tu māyīya tvena sthāpayiṣyate jaḍa cetana ādyava antara bheda śata saṃbhinnaḥ ca asau tad kṛtaḥ ca sarvaḥ ayam niṣpādya niṣpādaka bhāva jñāpyajñāpaka bhāva aṃvabhāsaḥ loka vyavahāra rūpaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^5	 yatra tu śuddha sva ātma rūpa prathā ātmaka anuttara śakti śāli nirargalasva ātma prakāśaḥ eva māyīya prathā antara vyavadhāna vandhyaḥ nibandhanam tatra tasya eva bhagavataḥ kāraṇa tvam eṣa ca anugraha lakṣaṇaḥ antyaḥ pañcamaḥ pārameśvaraḥ kṛtya viśeṣaḥ para puruṣa artha prāpakaḥ tad nibandhana tvāt parama artha mokṣasya anyatratyaḥ hi apavargaḥ kutaścid muktiḥ na sarvatas iti niḥśreyasa ābhāsaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ sa ca ayam dvitīyaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ laukika anvaya vyatireka siddha prasiddha kārya kāraṇa bhāva vilakṣaṇa tvāt sphuṭena rūpeṇa asaṃcetyamānaḥ kādācid ka vastu sadbhāva unneya parama arthaḥ ati durghaṭa kāri tva lakṣaṇa aiśvarya vijṛmbhā bhāvita adbhuta bhāvaḥ prathama koṭi saṃbhāvanā śūnya kālika ākāra sva prakāśa āvaraṇa nirākaraṇa manoratha śata duṣprāpa iti evaṃprakāraḥ kathamā dyotaka nipāta sahitena nirūpitaḥ akathaṃcit a iti kenacid ca prakāreṇa parameśvara abhinna guru caraṇa samārādhanena parameśvara ghaṭitena eva 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^6	 yathā uktam saṃbandhaḥ atīva durghaṭaḥ iti aāsādya a iti ā samantāt paripūrṇa rūpa tayā sādayitvā sva ātma upabhoga yogya tām nirargalām gamayitvā iyatā vidita vedya tvena para arthe śāstra karaṇe adhikāraḥ darśitaḥ anyathā pratāraka tā mātram eva syāt paurvakālyena sāmanantaryam atra vivakṣitam anyathā tu āsādana tāratamya prāptau māyīya mala kalāpa saṃskāra prakṣaye katham para upadeśaḥ śakya kriyaḥ saṃbhavanti hi māyā garbha adhikāriṇaḥ viṣṇu viriṃca ādyāḥ tad uttīrṇāḥ api mahā māyā adhikṛtāḥ śuddha aśuddhāḥ mantra tad īśa tat maheśa ātmānaḥ śuddhāḥ api śrī sadāśiva prabhṛtayaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^7	 te tu yadīya aiśvarya vipruḍbhiḥ īśvarībhūtāḥ sa bhagavān anavacchinna prakāśa ānanda rūpa svātantrya parama arthaḥ maheśvaraḥ tasya adāsyam a iti anena tad pratyabhijña upapādanasya mahā phala tvam āsūtrayati dīyate asmai svāminā sarvam yathā abhilaṣitam iti dāsaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ iti anena parameśvara rūpa svātantrya pātra tā uktāḥ ajanasya a iti yaḥ kaścid jāyamānaḥ tasya iti anena adhikāri viṣayaḥ na atra kaścid niyamaḥ iti darśayati yasya yasya hi idam svarūpa prathanam tasya tasya mahā phalam prathanasya eva parama artha phala tvāt tasya ca pratibandhaka saṃmataiḥ apratibandhanīya tvāt na hi prathitam aprathitam iti nyāyāt tat uktam na iha abhikrama nāśaḥ asti pratyavāyaḥ na vidyate su alpam api asya darmasya trāyte mahataḥ bhayāt iti parama guru pādaiḥ api śiva dṛṣṭau eka vāram pramāṇena śāstrāt vā guru vākyataḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^8	 jñāte śiva tve sarva sthe pratipattyā dṛḍha ātmanā karaṇena na asti kṛtyam kvāpi bhāvanayā api vā sakṛt jhāte suvarṇe kim satya tā karaṇa ādinā sarvadā pitṛ mātra ādi tulya dārḍyena satya tā iti janasya anavarata janana maraṇa pīḍitasya iti anena kṛpā āspadatayā upakaraṇīya tvam āha api śabdaḥ sva ātmanaḥ tad abhinnatām āviṣkurvan pūrṇa tvena sva ātmani para artha saṃpatti atirikta prayojana antara avakāśam parākaroti para arthaḥ ca prayojanam bhavati eva tad lakṣaṇa tvāt na hi ayam daiva śāpaḥ sva arthaḥ eva prayojanam na para arthaḥ iti tasya api atad lakṣaṇa tve sati aprayojana tvāt saṃpādya tvena abhisaṃhitam yat mukhya tayā tatas eva kriyāsu prayojakam tad prayojanam atas eva bheda āde api īśvarasya sṛṣṭi ādi karaṇe para arthaḥ eva prayojanam iti darśayitum nyāya nirmāṇa vedhasā nirūpitam yam artham adhikṛtya puruṣaḥ pravartate tat prayojanam iti 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^9	 icchan iti icchā viṣayīkṛtasya phalasya pravṛttaḥ hetu tvam śatrā darśayati icchā śaktiḥ ca uttarottaram ucchūna svabhāva tayā kriyāśakti paryantībhavati iti darśayiṣyāmaḥ upaśabdaḥ samīpa arthaḥ tena janasya parameśvara dharma samīpa tā karaṇam atra phalam atas eva āha samastaḥ iti parameśvara tāla ābhe hi samastāḥ saṃpadaḥ tad niḥṣyanda mayyaḥ saṃpannāḥ eva rohaṇa lābhe ratna saṃpadaḥ iva pramuṣitasva ātma parama arthasya hi kim anyena labdhena labdha tad parama arthasya api tat anyat na asti yat vāñchanīyam yat uktam grantha kṛtā evaḥ bhakti lakṣmī samṛddhānām kim anyat upayācitam enayā vā daridrāṇām kim anyat upayācitam iti evam ṣaṣṭhī samāsena prayojanam uktam bahubrīhiṇā tu upāyaḥ sūcyate 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^10	 samastasya bhāva abhāva rūpasya bāhya abhyantarasya nīla sukha ādeḥ yā saṃpad saṃpattiḥ siddhiḥ tathātva prakāśaḥ tasyāḥ samyak avāptiḥ vimarśa rūḍhiḥ sā eva hetuḥ yasyām tat pratyabhijñāyām tathā hi sphuṭatara bhāsa samāna nīla sukha ādi pramā anu eṣaṇa dvāreṇa eva pāramārthika pramātṛ lābhaḥ iha upadiśyate yat āha anyatraḥ idam iti asya vicchinna vimarśasya kṛtārtha tā yā sva svarūpe viśrāntiḥ vimarśaḥ saḥ aham iti ayam iti tathā tatra eva prakāśasya ātma viśrāntiḥ ahaṃbhāvaḥ hi kīrtitaḥ uktā ca sā eva viśrāntiḥ sarva apekṣā nirodhataḥ svātantryam atha kartṛ tvam mukhyam īśvara tā api ca iti iyatā ca upāye ati durghaṭa tva āśaṅkā parākṛtāḥ yat ante nirūpayiṣyati sughaṭaḥ eṣa mārgaḥ navaḥ iti tamya maheśvarasya pratyabhijñā pratīpam ātma ābhimukhyena jñānam prakāśaḥ pratyabhijñā pratīpam iti sva ātma avabhāsaḥ hi na ananubhūta pūrvaḥ avicchinna prakāśa tvāt tasya sa tu tat śaktyā eva vicchinnaḥ iva vikalpitaḥ iva lakṣyate iti vakṣyate 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^11	 pratyabhijñā ca bhāta bhāsamāna rūpa anusaṃdhāna ātmikā saḥ eva ayam caitra iti pratisaṃdhānena abhimukhībhūte vastuni jñānam loke api etad putraḥ evaṃguṇaḥ evaṃrūpakaḥ iti evam vā antataḥ api sāmānya ātmanā vā jñātasya punar abhimukhībhāva avasare pratisaṃdhi prāṇitam eva jñānam pratyabhijñā iti vyavahriyate nṛpam prati pratyabhijñāpitaḥ ayam ityādau iha api prasiddha purāṇa siddhānta āgama anumāna ādi vidita pūrṇa śakti svabhāve īśvare sati sva ātmani abhimukhībhūte tad pratisaṃdhānena jñānam udeti nūnam saḥ eva īśvaraḥ aham iti tām enām upapādayāmi iti upapattiḥ saṃbhavaḥ tām saṃbhavantīm tat samartha ācaraṇena prayojaka vyāpāreṇa saṃpādayāmi tathā hi saṃbhavati tāvat asau avicchinna prakāśa tvāt nirodhaka abhimata māyā śakti samapasāraṇa mātram eva tu tatra upapādanam 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^12	 pratyabhijñā upapattau sva para vibhāga abhāve tad apekṣam kartṛ abhiprāya ādi asaṃbhāvyam iti para smaipada prayogaḥ ittham ca atra śloke yojanā  maheśvarasya dāsyam samasta saṃpad lābha hetum kathaṃcid āsādya janasya api kathaṃcid tad pratyabhijñām āsādya prāpayya upakāram samasta saṃpad lābha hetu bhūtam maheśvara dāsya ātmakam icchan tām eva samasta saṃpad samavāpti hetukām tad pratyabhijñām upapādayāmi āsādya iti āvṛtti yojane dvau ṇicau iyati ca vyākhyāne vṛtti kṛtā bharaḥ na kṛtaḥ tātparyavyākhyānāt yat uktam saṃvṛta sautra nirdeśa vivṛti mātra vyāpārāyām iti ṭīkākāreṇa api vṛtti mātram vyākhyātum udyatena na idam spṛṣṭam asmākam tu sūtra vyākhyānaḥ eva udyamaḥ iti vibhajya vyākhyātam 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^13	 evam sarvatra evam anena ślokena abhidheyam prayojanam tad prayojanam tad prayojanam adhikāri nirūpaṇam guru parva kramaḥ saṃbandha iti darśitam tathā hi samasta saṃpad lakṣaṇaḥ vyākhyātaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ pūrvam puṇya pāpa ādau saṃsāra mūla kāraṇe hetuḥ saḥ eva pratyabhijñāyate anayā iti karaṇa vyutpattyā upāyaḥ iha lokottara mārgam prati nirṇītaḥ iti ati durghaṭa kāri tva lakṣaṇam aiśvaryam mārgaḥ navaḥ iti śākhā ante nirūpayiṣyamāṇam sūcayatā upāyaḥ darśitaḥ abhidheya tvena atas eva tathā hi jaḍa bhūtānām iti upakrama pūrvakam śloka antaram bhaviṣyati prayojanam ca pratyabhijñā upāya jñānam tasya prayojanam pratyabhijñānam tasya api prayojanam samasta saṃpad lakṣaṇa pāramaiśvarya eka rūpa rathanam tatas param na asti eva tasya sarva paryanta phala tvāt aṃśa aṃśikayā api 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^14	 yat uktam mayā eva stotre phalam kriyāṇām athavā vidhīnām paryantataḥ tvad maya tā eva deva pahla īpsavaḥ ye punar atra teṣām mūḍhā sthitiḥ syāt anavasthayā eva iti etat vakṣyati tat atra nidadhat padam iti pāda dvayena janasya iti anena adhikārī darśitaḥ yat nigamayiṣyati aniśam āviśan iti kathaṃcid iti anena guru parva kramaḥ vakṣyati mahā gurubhiḥ ucyate sma śiva dṛṣṭi śāstre yathā iti evam pratyabhijñātavya samasta vastu saṃgrahaṇena idam vākyam uddeśa rūpam pratijñā piṇḍa ātmakam ca madhya granthaḥ tu hetu ādi nirūpakaḥ iti prakaṭitaḥ mayā iti ca antyaślokaḥ nigamana granthaḥ iti evam pañca avayava ātmakam idam śāstram para vyutpatti phalam 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^15	 naiyāyika kramasya eva māyā pade pāramārthika tvam iti granthakāra abhiprāyaḥ kriyā saṃbandha sāmānyaḥ ityādiṣu uddeśeṣu prakaṭībhaviṣyati iti tāvat granthasya tātparyam su janaḥ ca laukikeśvara paricitaḥ īśvara viṣaye janam anujīvi guṇa saṃpannam prakāśayati jana viṣaye ca abhigāmika ādi guṇa saṃpannam īśvaram prakāśayati itiiyā an arthaḥ sāmānyena ṣaṣṭhosamāsena darśitaḥ tasya pratyabhijñāḥ iti etat śloka ākarṇana samaye ca śiṣyāṇām etad artha saṃkramaṇa krameṇa parameśvara tādātmyam eva upajāyate tāvat tathā hi janasya iti ākarṇanāt vayam te janana maraṇa pīḍitāḥ aparyupasta vṛttayaḥ ca asmāka mayam upakāram icchan maheśvarasya dāsyam āsādya samasta saṃpad samavāpti hetum tad pratyabhijñām upapādayati tatas ca tad pratyabhijñām evaṃbhūtām vayam prāptāḥ eva iti ittham eva hi adhikāriṇi śāstra arthasya bimba pratibimba vat saṃkrāntiḥ loḍliṅā ādīnām viṣayībhavati prathama puruṣa arthaḥ uttama puruṣa arthe paryasyati na tu tāṭasthyena adhikārī anadhi kāriṇoḥ pratipattau viśeṣa abhāva prasaṅgāt 
ĪPrVV_1,1.1^16	 ārogya kāmāḥ śivām sevantām sevadhvam iti vā vākya arthasya sevām ahai iti evaṃrūpeṇa adhikāriṇi dvitīyā kakṣyā saṃkrāntau tṛṭīya kakṣyām eva bhāvi koṭi patitām api puruṣa artha saṃpattim akāla kalita svarūpa anupraveśena sva ātmīkṛtām abhimanyamāne tatas eva vitata saṃvid sundara parāmarśaḥ pūrṇa tā abhimāna pratilambhāt anyasya tu anevaṃrūpa tvena eva anadhikāritā tāṭasthya prāṇāḥ iti tadā āstām avāntaram etat ati gahanam ca iti sthitam etat etena ślokena īśvara sāṃmukhyam vineyānām prayojana ādi pratipādanam ca kriyate iti ananta bhāva saṃbhāra bhāsane spandanam param upoddhātāyate yasya tam stumaḥ sarvadā śivam 
ĪPrVV_1,1.2^1	 nanu īśvarasya siddhiḥ eva kartavyā kā iyam siddhiḥ na tāvat utpattiḥ nitya tvāt na api īśvara siddhi kāra ādayaḥ tasya upapattim vidadhate jñaptiḥ siddhiḥ iti ced anavacchinna prakāśasya pramāṇa vyāpāra upādheya prakāśa ātmaka siddhi anupayogaḥ eva nanu anavacchinnaḥ tadīyaḥ prakāśa iti katham etat nīla sukha ādi prakāśe hi tad prakāśaḥ kutas tad aprakāśe api supta mūrchā ādau nitarām sva prakāśe api vai īśvare pramātḥṇām kim vṛttam yena teṣām pramāṇa vyāpāra anupayogaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha kartari jñātari sva ātmani ādi siddhe maheśvare ajaḍa ātmā niṣedham vā siddhim vā vidadhīta kaḥ iha kaḥ īśvare kīdṛśe kīdṛśena pramāṇena asti iti jñāna lakṣaṇām siddhim na asti iti jñāna lakṣaṇam vā niṣedham kuryāt pramātāḥ iti ced saḥ eva kaḥ deha ādiḥ jaḍaḥ uta tad anyaḥ vā kaścid ātma ādi śabda vācyaḥ saḥ api sva prakāśa svabhāvaḥ vā na vā deha ādiḥ jaḍaḥ iti ced saḥ eva sva ātmani asiddhaḥ paratra kām siddhim kuryāt ātmā api asvaprakāśaḥ jaḍaḥ eva tad tulya yogakṣemaḥ sva prakāśa svabhāvaḥ iti ced kīdṛśena svena rūpeṇa bhāti 
ĪPrVV_1,1.2^2	 yadi pariniṣṭhita saṃvid mātra rūpeṇa tadā saṃvidām bhedanam bheditānām ca antaranusaṃdhānena abhedanam na syāt tena svatantra sva prakāśa ātma tayā tāvat sa bhāsate bheditānām ca antaranusaṃdhānena abhedanam na syāt tena svatantra sva prakāśa ātma tayā tāvat sa bhāsate tathā abhāsamānaḥ ca kīdṛśam īśvaram sādhayet niṣedhet vā kartṛ jñātṛ svabhāvam iti ced nanu sa pramātā eva tathābhūtaḥ iti kaḥ anyaḥ saḥ nanu sarva kartṛ tva sarvajña tve pramātuḥ na staḥ na khalu sarva śabda arthaḥ jñātṛ kartṛ tvayoḥ svarūpam bhinatti bheda darśane api īśvara jñāna cikīrṣā yajña ādeḥ nityasya viṣayeṇa akāraṇa bhūtena anādheya atiśaya tvāt prakāśam ānatā ānayanam eva viṣaya tvam iti ced aprakāśa svabhāvasya tathā atvam anucitam iti vakṣyāmaḥ prakāśamāna svabhāva tve viṣayaḥ api sarva ātmanā prakāśaḥ eva nimagnaḥ iti prakāśaḥ prakāśate iti etāvat mātra parama artha tve kaḥ sarvajñā sarvajña vibhāgaḥ  pramāṇam api evam siddha tva asiddha tvābhyām paryanuyojyam evam siddhiḥ api 
ĪPrVV_1,1.2^3	 tasmāt viṣaya abhimatam vastu śarīra tayā gṛhītvā tāvat nirbhāsamānaḥ ātmā eva prakāśate viccheda śūnyaḥ suṣuptam api prati prakāśataḥ eva anyathā smṛtya yogāt prakāśasya ca nitya tvāt viccheda hetoḥ abhāvena anya pramātṛ apekṣayā ca prakāśamāna tvāt sva para pramātṛ vibhāgasya tat sṛṣṭasya māyīya tvena vakṣyamāṇa tvāt sa ca ayam svatantraḥ svātantryam ca asya abhede bhedanam bhedite ca antaranusaṃdhānena abhedanam iti bahu prakāram vakṣyāmaḥ etat eva asya pārameśvaryam mukhyam ānanda mayam rūpam iti pūrvam upāttam kartari iti 
ĪPrVV_1,1.2^4	 tat eva tu svātantryam vibhajya vaktum jñātari iti pañcāt nirdiṣṭam jñāna pallava svabhāvā eva hi kriyā iti vakṣyate tena sarva kriyā svatantre sarva śaktike iti yāvat uktam bhavet tāvat eva kartari jñātari iti iyam eva ca saṃvid svabhāva tā saṃvid iti tu ucyamānā vikalpya tvena prameya tām spṛśantaḥ sṛṣṭa tvāt na parama artha saṃvid iti vakṣyāmaḥ kartā jñātā ca maheśvara iti abhidhāne api saḥ eva prakāraḥ āpatet iti yathā yathā prameya bhūmikā pāda na nyakkāra kalaṅka parihāraḥ śakyaḥ tathā tathā yāvat gati yatitavyam iti bhūta vibhaktyā nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,1.2^5	 upadeśa avasare hi sarva ātmanā tāvat sā prameya tā asya parihartum aśakyā sva ātmani iti svasmin anapāyi rūpe svabhāve iti anena vaiśeṣika ādi abhimata jaḍa ātma vāda nirāsaḥ ādi siddhe iti avicchinna prakāśe iti arthaḥ maheśvare iti etat eva māheśvarya yat anavacchinna parkāśa tvena jñātṛ kartṛ tva dhārā upārohaḥ ajaḍa ātmā iti yasya tu vaiśeṣika ādeḥ jaḍaḥ ātmā sa siddhim karotu īśvara viṣayām anyaḥ tu sāṃkhya ādi niṣedham sāṃkhyaḥ api viṣaya avabhāsana rūpam jñānam buddhi dharmam icchan ātmānam vastutas jaḍam eva upaiti na ca jaḍa ātmā sva ātmani api durlabha prakāśa svātantrya leśaḥ kiṃcid sādhayitum niṣeddhum vā prabhaviṣṇuḥ pāṣāṇaḥ iva na ca ajaḍa ātmanaḥ api etat ucitam tathā hi sa sva ātmani siddhim ittham kuryāt yadi asya saḥ abhinava tvena bhāsamānaḥ pūrvam na bhāsate na bhāsanam ced jaḍa tā eva 
ĪPrVV_1,1.2^6	 niṣedham ca ittham vidadhyāt yadi sa na prakāśate tathā ca jaḍaḥ na ca jaḍasya etat yuktam iti uktam na api ajaḍasya tasmāt saṃvid prakāśaḥ eva ghaṭa ādi prakāśaḥ na tu asau svatantraḥ kaścid vāstavaḥ prakāśaḥ eva ca ātmāḥ tat na tatra kāraka vyāpāra vat pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ api nitya tva vat sva prakāśa tvasya api tatra bhāvāt 
ĪPrVV_1,1.3^1	 nanu kāraka vyāpāraḥ pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ ca yadi īśvare na saṃbhavati tarhi pratyabhijñāpayāmi iti yaḥ vyāpāraḥ uktaḥ sa katamaḥ vyāpāraḥ iti āśaṅkya āha kiṃtu moha vaśāt asmin dṛṣṭe api anupalakṣite śakti āviṣkaraṇena iyam pratyabhijñā upadarśyate saḥ īśvara svabhāvaḥ ātmā prakāśate tāvat tatra ca asya svātantryam iti na kenacid vapuṣā na prakāśate tatra aprakāśa ātmanā api prakāśate prakāśa ātmanā api tatra api prakāśa ātmani sarvathā prakāśa ātmanā prakāśaḥ bhāgaśas vā bhāgaśas prakāśane sarvasya vyatirekeṇa avyatirekeṇa vā katipayasya vyatirekeṇa avyatirekeṇa vā ukta prakāra pūrṇa tayā vā tat amī sapta prakārāḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,1.3^2	 tatra prathamaḥ prakāraḥ jaḍa ullāsaḥ antyaḥ parama śiva ātmā madhyamāḥ jīvāḥ bhāsāḥ sā eva bhagavataḥ māyā vimohinī nāma śaktiḥ tad vaśāt prakāśa ātma tayā satatam avabhāsamāne api ātmani bhāgena aprakāśana vaśāt anupalakṣite sarvathā hṛdayaṃgamībhāvam aprāpte atas eva pūrṇa tā avabhāsana sādhyām artha kriyām akurvati tad pūrṇa tā avabhāsana ātmaka abhimāna viśeṣa siddhayepratyabhijñā vyākhyāta pūrvā pradarśyate katham 
ĪPrVV_1,1.3^3	 śakteḥ īśvara niṣṭha tvena prasiddhāyāḥ dṛkkriyā ātmikāyāḥ āviṣkaraṇena pradarśanena abhimāna sādhya artha kriyāṇām tad abhimāna siddhyā vinā asiddheḥ tathā ca dṛṣṭāntam darśayati taiḥ taiḥ api upayācitaiḥ iti etat uktam bhavati na kāraka vyāpāraḥ bhagavati na api jñāpakavya apāraḥ ayam api tu moha apasāraṇa mātram etat vyavahāra sādhanānām pramāṇānām tāvatī eva viśrānteḥ ghaṭaḥ ayam agra gaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt iti anena hi ghaṭaḥ na jñāpyate pratyakṣeṇa eva prakāśamāna tvāt anyathā pakṣe hetu asiddheḥ kevalam moha mātram apasāryate yaḥ ca ayam mohaḥ tad apasāraṇam ca yat tat ubhayam api bhagavataḥ eva vijṛmbhā mātram na tu adhikam kiṃcid iti uktam vakṣyate ca 
ĪPrVV_1,1.4^1	 nanu paridṛśyamāne bhāva rāśau kimīyā śaktiḥ āviṣkriyate kam ca prati iti jaḍānām tāvat na jñāna ātmikā śaktiḥ asti kriyā ātmikā api svātantrya prāṃā svātantrya vyapagamāt asaṃbhāvanā bhūmiḥ eva tathā ca rathaḥ gacchati ityādau upacāram kecana pratipannāḥ na ca jaḍān prati vyavahāra sādhanam ucitam atha ajaḍa jīvat janata adhikāreṇa ubhayam api tarhi sarvasya sva ātmā maheśvaraḥ iti dūrataram viprakarṣitā pratyāśā tat etat āśṅkya nirūpayati tathā hi jaḍa bhūtānām pratiṣṭhā jīvat āśrayā jñānam kriyā ca bhūtānām jīvatām jīvanam matam tathā hi iti yukti upakramam dyotayati dṛśyatām kila iti arthaḥ tathā iti anena sādhyam sūcyate hinā hetuḥ iti anye prakṛtam sādhyam hetu siddhi āyat tam upakramyate iti arthaḥ tena iti buddhi vartinā tatas eva smaryamāṇena granthena varṇayiṣyamāṇena prakāreṇa yasmāt sarvam etat yuktam iti tathā hi iti śabdasya vā arthaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,1.4^2	 iha tāvat bhāva rāśiḥ yathā vimṛśyate tathā asti astitvasya prakāśam śaraṇīkurvataḥ prakāśa prāṇita deśīyam āśritya samunmevāt avimṛṣṭam hi yadi vastu tat na nīlam na pītam na sat na asat iti kutas iti paryanuyoge kim uttaram syāt tena yat yathā yāvat avādhitam vimṛśyate tat tathā tāvat asti tat eva deśa kāla ākāra vitata ātmānaḥ api dravya kriyā saṃbandha ādayaḥ ekatvena paramārtha santaḥ iti vakṣyatekriyā saṃbandha sāmānyaḥ ityādinā tatas ca vitatam api idam viśvam saṃkṣepa vimarśa daśa adhirohe jaḍam jīvat ca iti etāvatā dvaya rūpeṇa asti tatra jaḍāḥ vimṛśyamānāḥ na svatantrāḥ bhavanti vimṛśyamāna tā hi teṣām na sva śarīra viśrāntaḥ kaḥ api dharmaḥ jaḍa tva abhāva prasaṃgāt mama nīlam bhāti mayā nīlam jñāyate iti teṣām jaḍa bhūtānām cit maya tve api māyā ākhyayā īśvara śaktyā jāḍyam prāpitānām jīvantam pramātāram āśritya pratiṣṭhā tad pramātra abhimukhyena avasthānam tatas jaḍāḥ nāma na pṛthak santi 
ĪPrVV_1,1.4^3	 yathā uktam grantha kṛtā evaḥ evam ātmani asat kalpāḥ prakāśasya eva santi amī jaḍāḥ prakāśaḥ eva ekaḥ sva ātmanaḥ sva para ātmabhiḥ iti saḥ eva hi sva ātmanā san vaktavyaḥ yasya anyān upahitam rūpam cakāsti na ca bhā rūpān upahitam jaḍam nāma kiñcid tena jaḍānām hi śaktiḥ āviṣkriyate jaḍān prati iti etat tāvat nirutthānam eva ye tu anye jaḍebhyaḥ jīvanta iti nāma prasiddhāḥ teṣām api śarīra prāṇa puryaṣṭaka śūnya ākārāḥ tāvat jaḍāḥ eva iti teṣām api kim ucyate atas eva ghaṭa śarīra prāṇa sukha tadbh avarūpam yat lagnam bhāti tat eva jīva rūpa bhūtam satyam tasya ca āpāte yadi api bahu tvam bhāti tathā api tat jaḍa ātmaka vedya śarīra ādi upādheḥ tatas tat apārabha arthikam anyonya āśrayāt jīvāḥ hi jaḍa bhedāt bheda bhāginaḥ jaḍāḥ ca jīva bhedāt etat dehaḥ ayam etat vedyaḥ ayam iti bhedam upeyuḥ nīla pīta ādi bhāva bhedāḥ tu pramātṛ saṃlagna tayā bheda bhūmim eva paramadhirūḍhāḥ iti kim tena 
ĪPrVV_1,1.4^4	 tat ayam jīvānām abhedaḥ eva saṃpannaḥ iti jīvan pramātā iti jātam jīvanam ca jīvana kartṛ tvam tat ca jñāna kriyā ātmakam yaḥ hi jānāti ca karoti ca sa jīvati iti ucyate tat ayam pramātā jñāna kriyā śakti yogāt īśvara iti vyavaharta vayaḥ purāṇa āgama ādi prasiddha īśvara vat tad prasiddhau= api sarva viṣaya jñāna kriyā śaktimat tva svabhāvam eva aiśvaryam tanmātra anubandhi tvāt eva siddham tat api ca kalpita īśvare rāja ādau tathā vyāpti grahaṇāt yaḥ yāvati jñātā kartā ca sa tāvati īśvarp rājā iva anīśvarasya jñātṛ tva kartṛ tve svabhāva viruddhe yatas ātmā ca viśvatra jñātā kartā ca iti siddhā pratyabhijñā jñāna kriyā śaktaḥ eva svābhāvikyau aprarūḍha bheda unmeṣe sadāśiva īśvarau bhedasya sāmānyatas prarohe vidyā kale viśoṣataḥ prarohe buddhi karma indriya gaṇaḥ iva bhaviṣyati jaḍāḥ iti ajīvantaḥ anye ca jīvanta iti āpāte tāvat bhāti na tu saṃvid āpāte bhāti iti jīvatām iti jaṅgamāḥ eva amī ittham nirdiṣṭāḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,1.5^1	 nanu jñāna kriye eva katham siddhe yatas aiśvarya vyavahāraḥ prasādhyate iti śaṅkām śamayitum āha tatra jñānam svatas siddham kriyā kāya āśritā satī paraiḥ api upalakṣyeta tayā anya jñānam ūhyate aham jānāmi mayā jñātam jñāsyate ca iti evam sva prakāśa ahaṃparāmarśa pariniṣṭhitam eva idam jñānam nāma kim tatra anyat vicāryate tad aprakāśe hi viśvam andhatamasam syāt tat api vā na syāt bālaḥ api hi prakāśa viśrāntim eva saṃvedayate tat uktam vijñāta āram are kena bojānīyāt iti tad nihnave hi kaḥ praśnaḥ kim uttaram ca syāt iti tatra ca jānāmi iti antar saṃrambha yogaḥ api bhāti yena śukla ādeḥ guṇāt atyanta jaḍāt jānāmi iti vapuḥ cit svabhāva tām abhyetiḥ sa ca saṃrambhaḥ vimarśaḥ kriyāśaktiḥ bhavati 
ĪPrVV_1,1.5^2	 yat uktam asmad parameṣṭhi śraḥ sroma ānanda pādaiḥ ghaṭa ādi graha kāle api ghaṭam jānāti sā kriyā iti tena āntarī kriyāśaktiḥ jñāna vat eva svatas siddhā sva prakāśāḥ sā eva tu sva śaktyā prāṇa puryaṣṭaka krameṇa śarīram api saṃcaramāṇā spandana rūpā satī vyāpāra ātmikāḥ māthā pade api pramāṇasya pratyakṣa ādeḥ viṣayaḥ sā ca para śarīra ādi sāhityena avagatā svam svabhāvam jña ātmakam avagamayati na ca jñānam idan tathā bhāti idantā hi ajñāna tvam na ca anyat vastu anyena vapuṣā bhātam bhātam bhavet tat jñānam bhāti ā iva param bhāti ca yat tat eva aham iti asya vapuḥ iti para jñānam api sva ātmā evaḥ para tvam kevalam upādheḥ deha ādeḥ sa ca api vicāritaḥ yāvat na anyaḥ iti viśvaḥ pramātṛ vargaḥ paramārthataḥ ekaḥ pramātā saḥ eva ca asti 
ĪPrVV_1,1.5^3	 tat uktam  prakāśaḥ eva asti sva ātmanaḥ sva para ātmabhiḥ iti tatas ca bhagavān sadāśivaḥ jānāti iti atas prabhṛti krimiḥ api jānāti iti antam ekaḥ eva pramātāḥ iti phalatas sarvajña tvam pramātuḥ evam kartṛ tve api vācyam yat uktam asmad parameṣṭhibhiḥ śiva dṛṣṭau ghaṭaḥ mad ātmanā vetti vedmi aham ca ghaṭa ātmanā sadāśiva ātmanā vedmi sa vā vetti mad ātmanā nānā bhāvaiḥ svam ātmānam jānan= āste svayam śivaḥ ityādi ūhyate iti anena jñānena jñānasya prameya tvam na nirvahati iti darśayati anyathā hi anumīyate iti brūyāt 
ĪPrVV_1,1.5^4	 tat evam yeṣām tārkika pravāda pāṃsu pāta dhūsarībhāvaḥ na vṛttaḥ asmin saṃvedana pathe te iyatā eva ātmānam īśvaram vidvāṃsaḥ ghaṭa śarīra prāṇa sukha tad abhāvān tatra eva nimajjayante īśvara samāviṣṭāḥ eva bhavanti tatas ayam upoddhātaḥ upa iti ātmanaḥ samīpe ṭaṅka vat īśvara pratyabhijñāna lakṣaṇaḥ utkarṣaḥ hanyate viśrāmyate yena etāvat eva ca asya granthasya tātparyam iti tatas api ayam upoddhātaḥ upāṃśu avitatam kṛtvā uditi śāstrasya ūrdhvaḥ eva hanyate apasāryate prameya viṣayaḥ vyāmohaḥ yena iti gati artha tvāt vā hanteḥ jñānam arthaḥ jñāyate prameyam yena iti kecid tu gatim striyam gacchati iti etat viṣayam eva hanti artham āhuḥ evam śloka catuṣṭaya artha bhāvanā dārḍhi adeva labhyate parama śivaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,2.0^1	 pūrva pakṣa tayā yena viśvam ābhāsya bhedataḥ abheda uttara pakṣa antam nīyate tam stumaḥ śivaḥ iha yat parama artha rūpam āśaṅkyamāna pratipakṣa pratikṣepeṇa nirūpayiṣyamāṇam suṣṭhutamām spaṣṭokṛtam bhavati yat āha bhaṭṭa nārāyaṇaḥ namaḥ te bhava saṃbhrānta bhrāntim udbhāvya bhindate jñāna ānandam ca nirdvandvam deva vṛtvā vivṛṇvate tatra iha anātmāni īśvara vādinām bhrānti bhedana pūrvakam parama artham vivarīṣyan tad udbhāvanam tāvat ekādaśabhiḥ ślokaiḥ karoti nanu sva lakṣaṇa ābhāsam ityādibhiḥ tena kartā api kalpitaḥ iti antaiḥ tatra śloka dvayena ātmanaḥ dhruvasya dṛśya anupalabdhyā abhāvaḥ uktaḥ pratyakṣa ātma vādinaḥ prati 
ĪPrVV_1,2.0^2	 tatra śloka trayeṇa smṛti anusaṃdhānam saṃskārāt siddham iti anya bāsiddha tvāt ātma anumānāya na paryāptam iti proktam anumeya ātma vādinaḥ prati tatra ślokena jñāna ādi guṇaiḥ guṇini pratipattiḥ iti anumānam nirastam evam ātmānam nirākṛtya tatas jñāna kriyā śakti saṃbandha rūpam aiśvarya nirākartum jñānasya svarūpam eva vyatiriktam vādi antara mate sāṃkhya mate ca ayujyamānam iti nirūpitam śloka dvayena tatas ekena kriyā nāma na kācid kvacid api asti iti kathitam tatra sādhakam pratikṣipya bādhakam ca upanyasyati tatas saṃbandhasya ślokena nāstitvam pratipāditam pramāṇa abhāvam vadatā ślokena eva tatra bādhakam pramāṇam uktvā na ātmā sthiraḥ na api jñātṛ tva kartṛ tva lakṣaṇam asya aiśvaryam iti sva pakṣe upasaṃhṛtaḥ iti pūrva pakṣasya piṇḍa arthaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,2.1–2^1	 atha grantha arthaḥ vyākhyāyate nanu sva lakṣaṇa ābhāsam jñānam ekam param punar sa abhilāpam vikalpa ākhyam bahudhā na api tat dvayam nityasya kasyacid draṣṭuḥ tasya atra anavabhāsataḥ ahaṃpratītiḥ api eṣā śarīra ādi avasāyinī nanu iti ākṣepe iha ātmā saṃvid svabhāvaḥ sthiraḥ iti tāvat ayuktam sthirasya api sva prakāśasya aprakāśanāt tathā hi ghaṭaprakāśaḥ ghaṭavikalpaḥ ghaṭa pratyabhijñā ghaṭa smṛtiḥ ghaṭa utprekṣā ityādi rūpeṇa jñānāni eva prakāśante bhinna kāntāni bhinna viṣayāṇi bhinna kārāṇi ca tatra nīlasya prakāśaḥ sva lakṣaṇa ābhāsam jñānam svam anyān anuyāyi svarūpa saṃkoca bhāji lakṣaṇam deśa kāla ākāra rūpam yasya ābhāsaḥ prakāśanam antarmukham yasmin bahis mukhīna svarūpa dhāriṇi jñāne tat avikalpakam viṣaya bhede api eka jātīyam svarūpa vaicitrye api kāraṇa abhāvāt 
ĪPrVV_1,2.1–2^2	 vikalpe hi vaicitrya kāraṇam abhilāpaḥ sa ca atas na asti na hi abhilāpaḥ nīlasya dharmaḥ na ca cakṣuḥ grāhyaḥ tatas asau prācyaḥ smartavyaḥ aprabuddhe ca saṃskāre na smṛtiḥ tad prabodhaḥ ca vastu darśana utthitaḥ iti vastu darśana samaye abhilāpa smṛtiḥ na asti tatas param vikalpakam jñānam sarvasya vikalpasya sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā nirvikalpaka mūla tvāt param iti ca anya rūpam sāmānya lakṣaṇam tasya viṣayaḥ sva lakṣaṇe ati saṃkocini vitata vikalpa sādhyasya vrḍdhavyāvahārikasya aupadeśikasya vā saṃketasya kartum aśakya tvāt kṛtasya api vaiyarthyāt tena hi ananuyāyinā na punar vyavahāraḥ tat ca bahu bhedam yatas tat abhilāpena saṃjalpa ātmanā śabda rūpeṇa saha vartate śabdanam ca idam iti tat iti tat idam iti bhavet idam iti idam vai idam ityādi bahudhā bhidyate 
ĪPrVV_1,2.1–2^3	 tat ca na viṣaya pakṣaḥ vartate api tu tasya vikalpasya svarūpam eva vicitra ukurvat pratibhāti iti vikalpaḥ bahu bhedaḥ evam anubhava vikalpa paramparā tāvat sva prakāśa tvena bhāti syāt etat yat lagnā asau paramparā saḥ api ābhāti iti tatra yatas dvayam api etat avikalpa itara rūpam na anyasya kasyacid etat atiriktasya draṣṭuḥ anubhavituḥ saṃbandhi dṛśyasya tu bhavatu bāhya artha vāde atra hetuḥ yatas tasya draṣṭuḥ atas eva saṃvid svabhāvatā upagamāt sva prakāśa tā yogya tvāt āpanna upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteḥ atra etat bodha dvaya madhye na asti avabhāsaḥ nanu asti eva avabhāsaḥ iti asiddhā dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ tathā hi aham vedmi niścinomi smarāmi idam iti vidādi prakṛti artha rūpāt jñāna smṛti ādeḥ idam iti ca karma rūpāt viṣayāt atiriktam eva aham iti anuyāyini prakāśe anuyāyi rūpam bhāti kaḥ evam āha bhāti iti 
ĪPrVV_1,2.1–2^4	 bhānam hi avikalpakam aham iti śabda anuviddhaḥ vikalpa pratyayaḥ nanu tathā api kim anena vikalpyate śarīra santānaḥ vā kṛśaḥ aham ityādi pratyayāt jñāna santānaḥ vā sukhī aham iti pratīteḥ matu arthīyaḥ ca santānam eva spṛśati na atiriktam tat etat uktam ahaṃpratītiḥ api śarīram ādi grahaṇāt jñānam avasyati saṃtāna rūpa tayā vikalpayati avaśyam sadṛśa apara bhāva bheda grahaṇa sāmarthya vāsanā āviṣṭa tvāt iti eṣā iti na asmābhiḥ nihnutā sa abhilāpam vikalpa ākhyam iti anena saṃgṛhīta tvāt etat uktam bhavati ahaṃpratītiḥ eva tāvat na ātmā tasyāḥ api vikalpa rūpa tvāt asthaiḥ yāt ca etat pratīti pratyayaḥ api na asti anyaḥ śarīra ādeḥ bhavan= api vā vedya pakṣa patitaḥ syāt iti tathā api saṃvid saṃvedya vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ na siddhiḥ iti etat api śabdena dyotitam evam na asti ātmā saṃvid saṃvedya tri atiriktaḥ dṛśyasya tasya anupalabdheḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,2.3^1	 atra ātma vādi anumānam utthāpayati atha anubhava vidhvaṃse smṛtiḥ tad anurodhinī katham bhavet na nityaḥ syāt ātmā yadi anubhāvakaḥ iha smṛti kāle su smūrṣitaḥ arthaḥ bhavatu dhvaṃsatām vā iti kintena anubhavaḥ tāvat dhvastaḥ iti atra sarvasya avivādaḥ tam eva ca anurundhānā smṛtiḥ jāyate tathā hi smṛtau na arthasya prakāśaḥ na adhyavasāyaḥ na api anubhavasya arthasya ca aṅguli dvaya vat na api anubhava viśiṣṭasya arthasya daṇḍi vat sarvatra ayam iti pratyaya prasaṅgāt kiṃtu anubhava prakāśaḥ eva smṛtau pradhānam anubhavasya tu artha prakāśa ātmaka tvāt anubhava prakāśana antarīyakaḥ artha avabhāsaḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,2.3^2	 sarvathā yadi anubhavaḥ dhvastaḥ tadā tad prakāśa rūpā katham smṛtiḥ tad dvāreṇa artha viṣayā syāt tayā ca sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ kriyamāṇaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti asau svarūpeṇa anapahnavanīyā satī anubhavasya nāśe kiṃcid avinaṣṭam āvedayati tat eva ca anubhava kartṛ anubhavitṛ rūpam ātmā anubhāvakaḥ nityaḥ iti iyat eva ca ātma siddheḥ jīvitam tat tu na adhikam iha eva unmīlitam ācāryeṇa vaktavya śeṣa vivakṣayā pūrva pakṣaḥ mā tāvat samāpad iti āśayena katham bhavet iti arhtaḥ tāvat tasyām akiṃcitkaraḥ anubhavaḥ ca dhvastaḥ iti na kenacid prakāreṇa smṛtiḥ syāt tad abhāve ca saṃketa śabda smṛti āyattāḥ api astaṅga tāḥ sarve vikalpāḥ nirvikalpam ca andha badhira mūka prāyam iti hanta nirākrandam avasīdet viśvam iti 
ĪPrVV_1,2.4	 iha kārya atirekeṇa tādṛś kalpanīyam yat kārya siddhaye paryāpnoti na ca evam ātmā arthaḥ hi tāvat smaryate sa ca anubhava prakāśa mukhena anubhavaḥ ca dhvastaḥ iti uktam yadi ātmā kaścid asti kim tena etat api hi vaktavyam ākāśam api asti iti atha ucyate na kevalena ātmanā etat siddhyati api tu anubhava saṃskāraḥ api atra upayogī iti tarhi saḥ eva astu kim anena  tat etat darśayati satya api ātmani dṛś nāśāt tad dvārāḥ dṛṣṭa vastuṣu smṛtiḥ kena atha yatra eva anubhavaḥ tad padā eva sā dṛṣṭeṣu anubhūteṣu vastuṣu yā smṛtiḥ tasyām anubhavaḥ dṛś ātmā dvāram artha āśa sparśe sa ca sati api ātmani naṣṭaḥ anubhavaḥ tasya hi anāśe idam iti eṣaḥ eva atruṭitaḥ prakāśaḥ iti kā smṛtiḥ tad anubhavitā kim smṛteḥ kuryāt iti yatra eva viṣaye anubhavaḥ vṛttaḥ tat eva tasyāḥ smṛteḥ padam smaryamāṇam tad padā iti bahuvrīhiḥ sā iti smṛtiḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,2.5	 nanu jñāna antarasya viṣayeṇa katham tasyāḥ viṣayitvā abhimānaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha yatas hi pūrva anubhava saṃskārāt smṛti saṃbhavaḥ yadi evam antar gaḍunā kaḥ arthaḥ syāt sthāyinā ātmanā anubhavena hi saṃskāraḥ janyate sva ucitaḥ saṃskāraḥ ca prātana rūpām sthitim sthāpayati ākṛṣṭa śākhādeḥ cira saṃvartitasya vivartyamānasya bhūrja ādeḥ tena atra api saṃskāraḥ tām smṛtim pūrva anubhava anukāriṇīm karoti iti tad viṣayaḥ eva smṛteḥ viṣayaḥ evam tarhi antargaḍuḥ yathā āyāsāya param tadvat ātmā sthiraḥ kalpana āyāsa mātra phalaḥ iti kim tena sarvam hi saṃskāreṇa jagat vyavahāra kuṭumbakam kṛta kara avalambam iti 
ĪPrVV_1,2.6^1	 nanu tasma eva saṃskārasya āśrayaḥ vaktavyaḥ sa hi guṇa tvāt āśrayam apekṣate yaḥ āśrayaḥ saḥ ātmā syāt iti āśaṅkya āha tatas bhinneṣu dharmeṣu tad svarūpa aviśeṣatah saṃskārāt smṛiti siddhau syāt smartā draṣṭā iva kalpitaḥ iha saṃskāre jāyamāne yadi ātmanaḥ viśeṣaḥ sa tarhi avyatiriktaḥ iti na nityaḥ syāt atha na kaścid asya viśeṣaḥ tena tarhi kim atha saṃskāraḥ eva asya viśeṣaḥ tarhi na vyatiriktaḥ asau iti punar api anitye jñāne saṃskāraḥ iti āyātam anubhavāt viśiṣṭam viśiṣṭa smrṭi ākhya kārya kāri jñānam paramparayā jāyate iti iyān a iva saṃskāra arthaḥ atha saṃskāra ātmā vyatiriktaḥ viśeṣaḥ tasya tarhi kim asau saṃbandhaḥ ca vyatiriktaḥ nirākariṣyate 
ĪPrVV_1,2.6^2	 evam jñāna sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharmāḥ api vikalpanīyāḥ etat āha tatas iti ātmanaḥ bhinneṣu dharmeṣu aṅgīkriyamāṇeṣu teṣu satsu api ātmanaḥ svarūpe viśeṣa abhāvāt sa tāvat ātmā smrṭau na vyāpriyeta asmatṛ rūpa asaṃskṛta rūpa ādi prācya rūbh anapāyāt iti saṃskārāt eva smṛteḥ siddhiḥ iti aham smarāmi iti yaḥ smartā saḥ api śarīra saṃtānaḥ jñāna saṃtānaḥ ca adhyāvasīyate yathā draṣṭā pūrvam hi uktam ahaṃpratītiḥ api eṣā śarīra ādi avasāyinī iti evam ātmani sādhakam pramāṇam pratyakṣam anumānam ca parākṛtam bādhakam ca sūcitam dharma yoge nityatā ahāni anyathā kim tena tat uktam carma upamaḥ ced saḥ anityaḥ sva tukyaḥ ced asat samaḥ varṣa ātapābhyām kim vyomnaḥ carmaṇi asti hi tad phalam iti 
ĪPrVV_1,2.7^1	 ittham ātmānam nirākṛtya tasya aiśvaryam api nirākartum jñāna śaktim eva parīkṣitum āha jñānam ca cit svarūpam ced tat anityam kim ātma vat atha api jaḍam etasya katham artha prakāśa tā para abhyupagamena prasaṅga āpādanam etat pūrva pakṣa vādī karoti prasaṅga viparyaya lābhaḥ me bhaviṣyati iti tatra ātma vādī nitya tvam ātmanaḥ ittham brūte iha kālaḥ nāma idaṃbhāva viśiṣṭasya viśeṣaṇa tām avalambamānaḥ tam viśiṣṭīkurvan tad saṃkocāt anityam saṃpādayati ātmanaḥ ca cit svabhāva tvāt idam iti prathana abhāvena viśeṣya tvam na asti viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ hi yojaka āyattaḥ na ca sva prakāśe yojaka antaram asti 
ĪPrVV_1,2.7^2	 saḥ ittham bruvāṇaḥ paryanuyujyate jñānam api tarhi sva prakāśam iti tatra api eṣā eva vārtā iti tat api kasmāt na nityam na ca dvayoḥ nityayoḥ kaścid saṃbandhaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ hi asau na anyaḥ tatas ātmanaḥ jñānam śaktiḥ iti avasannam adaḥ atha na sva prakāśam jñānam tarhi parasya api adaḥ na prakāśaḥ sva prakāśa rūpa āveśanam hi asau parasya vidadhat bodhaḥ prakāśaḥ bhavati parasya api tatas sva prakāśa tā śūnyaḥ na asau arthasya prakāśaḥ syāt bhāva antara vat 
ĪPrVV_1,2.8^1	 jaḍaḥ api asau ittham arthasya prakāśaḥ bhaviṣyati iti sāṃkhya matam āśaṅkate atha arthasya yathā rūpam dhatte buddhiḥ tathā ātmanaḥ caitanyam iha tāvat artham jānāmi iti asti vyavahāraḥ tatra arthasya prakāśaḥ iti etāvān eva parama arthaḥ tat na arthasya svam rūpam sarvam prati tathā tva prasaṅgāt na kaṃcid prati vā iti sarvajñam ajñam vā jagat syāt na api arthe anyatas etat rūpam upanipatitam eṣaḥ eva hi doṣaḥ syāt tat nūnam anyatra eva ayam dharmaḥ tattva antare tatra api katham arthasya prakāśaḥ syāt iti nūnam tatra tattva antare saḥ arthaḥ pratibimba tvena upasaṃkrāmati tat tattva antaram sattva prādhānyāt pratibimba graha yogyam tamasā aacchādita tvāt sakala pratibimba nataḥ vyāvartitam bhāge rajasā tamasaḥ apasāraṇāt kiṃcid eva pratibimbakam gṛhyāti tat eva buddhi tattvam ucyate 
ĪPrVV_1,2.8^2	 artha pratibimba grahaḥ ca jñānam asya vṛtti rūpam pūrva vyapadeśa tirodhāyaka dadhi ādi pariṇāma vilakṣaṇa pariṇati viśeṣa ātmakam evam arthasya tāvat rūpam buddhiḥ dhārayati iyaḥ ca sattva ādīnām sukha duḥkha moha rūpa tayām bhogya tvāt jaḍam iti darpakṣa vat aprakāśam na ca bhogyasya aprakāśasya tad viruddha bhoktṛtā rūpa prakāśa ātmaka svabhāva saṃbhavaḥ yukti anupātī iti tad vilakṣaṇena bhoktrā bhavitavyam sa ca prakāśaḥ iti etāvat svabhāvaḥ svabhāva antaram hi aprakāśa rūpam bhogyam katham bhoktuḥ svabhāvatayā saṃbhāvyeta sa ca prakāśa mātra svabhāva tvena eva yadi viśvasya prakāśaḥ tarhi yugapad eva prakāśeta ghaṭa prakāśaḥ api paṭa prakāśaḥ syāt iti viśvam saṃkīryeta sa ca arthāt artha pratibimbāt tad ādhārāt ca buddhi tattvāt anyaḥ katham arthasya prakāśaḥ syāt asaṃbandhāt tasmāt buddhiḥ eva svaccha tvāt prakāśa pratibimbam api gṛhṇāti 
ĪPrVV_1,2.8^3	 tatas prakāśa pratibimba parigraha mahima upanata prakāśa āveśa buddhi tattva āveśita pratibimbaka nīlā ādi artha paryanta saṃkrānteḥ prakāśa āveśasya arthaḥ prakāśate iti siddhaḥ vyavahāraḥ tat evam jñānam jaḍa buddhi tattva avyatirekāt jaḍam api cit pratibimba yogāt viṣayasya prakāśaḥ iti etat eva tāvat anucitam yat prakāśa ātmā pumān buddhau pratibimbam arpayati samāna guṇe bimbaka apekṣayā ca vimale pratibimba saṃkrānti darśanāt rūpavati ādarśe ghaṭa rūpa pratibimba vat ātma buddhyoḥ ca ati vailakṣaṇyam ātma apekṣayā ca na buddhiḥ vimalā tat bahvatu tāvat etat iti atha śabdena sūcayati kiṃtu pratibimba vādena api na kiṃcid pratisamāhitam bhavet iti darśayati  ajaḍā sā evam jāḍye na artha prakāsa tā caitanya pratibimba yoge yadi tāvat tad pratibimbakam api mukhyam prakāśa rūpam eva na bhavati tena api na kiṃcid kṛtam syāt na hi pratibimba ta vahni puñjaḥ ādarśaḥ dāhyam dahet 
ĪPrVV_1,2.8^4	 atha mukhya prakāśa rūpam eva tad pratibimbakam tat tarhi buddheḥ avyatiriktam iti mukhya prakāśa rūpā eva buddhiḥ jātāḥ iti yatas viruddha dharma adhyāsāt bhīrubhiḥ etat kalpitam saḥ eva punar jājvalyamānam nijam ojaḥ jṛmbhayati tatas ca sā buddhiḥ eva cit mayī syāt kim puruṣeṇa evam artha pratibimba ka dvāreṇa artha mayī iti api āyātaḥ vijñāna vādaḥ kutas etasyāḥ tad rūpa tvam iti pūrva kāraṇa paramparātaḥ iti utaram vācyam evam sā eva ced cit rūpā prāgvat nitya tā prasaṅgaḥ na ceta cit rūpasya api nitya tā tarhi ātmā na nityaḥ kaścid asti yasya jñānam nāma śaktiḥ syāt iti jñāna mātram eva asti yaḥ artha prakāśa rūpaḥ bodhaḥ yaḥ ca vikalpa smṛti ādi rūpaḥ tāvatā artha vyavahāra siddheḥ iti prasaṅga viparyaya lābhaḥ jñānam ca cit svarūpam ced iti ādeḥ śloka dvayasya tātparyam 
ĪPrVV_1,2.9^1	 evam jñānam parīkṣya kriyām parīkṣate kriyā api arthasya kāya ādeḥ tad tad deśa ādi jāta tā na anya adṛṣṭeḥ iha parispanda rūpam tāvat gavcchati calati patati ityādi yat pratibhāsa gocaram tatra gṛhaseśa gata deva datta svarūpāt anantaram bāhya deśa varti deva datta svarūpam iti etāvat upalabhyate na tu tad svarūpa atiriktām kāṃcid anyām kriyām pratīmaḥ devadattaḥ dinam tiṣṭhati iti atra tu prabhāta kāla āviṣṭa devadatta svarūpam tatas prahara kāla āliṅgita tad svarūpam ityādi bhāti dugdham pariṇamate iti atra madhura vastu rūpam amla vastu rūpam drava rūpam kaṭhina rūpam ityādi evam sādṛśyāt ca tatra pratyabhijñā bhinne api kāya keśana sva ādau= iva deśa ākāra anya tve tu kāla anya tvam avaśyaṃbhāvi deśa kāla anya tve api svarūpasya eva deśa tvāt kāla bhede ca svarūpa bhedāt deśa kāla ākārāḥ ākāraḥ eva yadi api paryavasmanti tathā api sthūla dṛṣṭyā asti bhedaḥ iti te hi bhedena bauddhaiḥ ucyante iti tātparyam 
ĪPrVV_1,2.9^2	 evam pratyakṣeṇa na dṛśyate kacid kriyā tad bhāvāt na tad pūrvakeṇa anumānena kāryam ca prāma prāpti ādi uttara kṣaṇa rūpam tad deśa vastu rūpa ādi iti kārya anyatha anupapattyā api na sā kalpyāḥ evam pratyakṣa anumānābhyām tasyāḥ adṛṣṭiḥ iti sādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ uktaḥ bādhakam api āha  na sā api ekā kramikā ekasya ca ucitā tatra pūrva apara rūpa tā kṣaṇānām vikalpa budvya anusaṃdhānāt na tu sva ātmani kiṃcid pūrvam aparam vā vastu mātram hi tat 
ĪPrVV_1,2.9^3	 atas vikalpa prāṇitam pūrva aparībhūta tvam krama rūpa tā kriyāyāḥ kiṃcid kṣaṇam na vastu spṛśati te hi kṣaṇāḥ na anyonya svarūpa āviṣṭāḥ iti katham ekā kriyā kramaḥ hi bhedena vyāptaḥ abhiśne tad abhāvāt bhedasya viruddham ekyam iti katham kramikā ekā ca iti syāt atha ekatra āśraye avasthānāt ekā tatra api tad kṣaṇa atiriktaḥ na kaścid āśrayaḥ anubhūyate kṣaṇāḥ eva hi prabandha vṛttayaḥ bhānti kim ca tathābhūtaiḥ bhinna deśa kāla ākāraiḥ kriyā akṣaṇaiḥ āviṣṭaḥ āśrayaḥ katham ekaḥ syāt atas eva devadattaḥ ayam saḥ eva grāmam prāptaḥ iti sādṛśyāt bhavantī pratyabhijñā na aikyam vāstavam gamayitum alam 
ĪPrVV_1,2.10	 evam jñānam kriyām ca parīkṣya yasmin sati te saṃbaddhe sarvajña tva sarva kartṛ tā ru upa aiśvarya prasādhanāya prabhavataḥ tam saṃbandham dhvaṃsayitum tad viṣayam pramāṇa abhāvam tāvat āha tatra tatra sthite tat tat bhavati iti eva dṛśyate na anyat na anyaḥ asti saṃbandhaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvataḥ mṛtppiṇḍe sati stūpakaḥ tatra sati śivikaḥ yāvat ghaṭaḥ iti evam bhāva kṣaṇāḥ eva upalabhyante na adhikam kiṃcid pratyakṣeṇa avabhāsate na api anumānena iti kriyāyām iva vācyam sarvatra ādhāra ādheya bhāva ādau ayam eva panthāḥ pṛthagrūpa kuṇḍa vat arakṣaṇa anantaram nirantara ātmaka viśiṣṭa kuṇḍavat ara udayaḥ iti ayam eva ca bhāvaḥ bhāva antareṇa saha niyata pūrva aparatayā vikalpena vyavahiyamāṇaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti abhidhīyate na ca jñāna kriyābhyām saha ātmanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ātmanaḥ tad kārya tva abhāvāt jñānasya ca sva sām agrokārya tvāt kriyāyāḥ ca abhāvāt iti na jñāna kriyā saṃbandhaḥ yatas jñātṛ tva kartṛ tve syātām 
ĪPrVV_1,2.11	 evam pramāṇam parākṛtya saṃbandhe bādhakam sāmānya viśeṣa mukhena nirūpayati dviṣṭhasya aneka rūpa tvāt siddhasya anya anapekṣaṇāt pāratantrī a ādyayogāt ca tena kartā api kalpitaḥ saṃbandhaḥ tāvat paraspara prāpti rūpaḥ dvayoḥ prāpti bhājoḥ ekaḥ tiṣṭhati iti sāmānya lakṣaṇam tat ca katham na hi ekatra viśramita aśeṣa śarīra sāraḥ anyatra viśramitum alam svarūpa bheda prasaṅgāt etena saṃyoga samavāyau tad mūlāḥ ca anye api saṃbandhāḥ bādha vidhurām dhuram adhyāropitāḥ mantavyāḥ yaḥ api cetaneṣu tad kalpanayā ca acetaneṣu pāratantrī a ātmā saṃbandhaḥ vyavahiyate tatra siddhasya na pāratantryam asti siddha tvāt eva asiddhasya natarām niḥsvarūpasya tāddharmyā yogāt evam apekṣāyām api vācyam dve ca rūpe katham śliṣyataḥ dvayoḥ ekatva anupapatteḥ eka tve vā kaḥ śleṣaḥ tasmāt jñāna saṃbandhāt jñātāḥ iti yathā vikalpa kalpitaḥ arthaḥ na vastu tathā kriyā saṃbandhāt kartā iti api kalpanā mātram iti pūrva pakṣasya saṃkṣepaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,3.0	 vinā yena na kiṃcid syāt samastāḥ api dṛṣṭayaḥ anastamita saṃbodha svarūpam tam stumaḥ śivam etasmin pūrva pakṣe yat uktam smṛteḥ saṃskāra mātrāt eva siddhiḥ iti tat eva dūṣayituṃsatyam ityādi jñāna smṛti apohana śaktimān iti antam śloka saptakam kriyāyām saṃbandhe ca dūṣaṇa uddharaṇam dvitīye kriyā adhikāre bhaviṣyati yat tu pareṇa vyatiriktam jñānam kāśāt asāṃkhya ādi dṛṣṭau nirākṛtam tat abhimatam eva grantha kṛtaḥ iti tat dūṣaṇa antaram eva tatra śloka dvayena jñānasya sva saṃvedana rūpa tayā anubhavasya smṛtau aprakāśa tvam darśitam saṃskāra ja tve api tatas śloka dvayena smṛteḥ bhrānti tvam āśaṅkā pūrvakam parākṛtya tṛtīyena prasaṅgāt sarva adhyavasāyānām api bhrānti tva āśaṅkā śamitā tatas sati api saṃskāre smṛti anupapattau vyavahāra ucchedaḥ iti ślokena uktvā sva pakṣe tad upapattiḥ iti ślokena uktam iti tātparyam grantha arthaḥ tu nirūpyate 
ĪPrVV_1,3.1	 satyam kiṃtu smṛti jñānam pūrva anubhava saṃskṛteḥ jātam api ātma niṣṭham tat na adya anubhava vedakam pūrva pakṣa madhyāt mayā tāvat bahu aṅgīkartavyam iti satyam iti anena darśitam yat tu na aṅgīkartavyam tat dūṣyate iti etat uktam kiṃtu iti anena viśeṣa abhidhāyinā iha smṛtau viṣaya mātrasya prakāśaḥ na samarthanīyaḥ vartate yaḥ saṃskārāt eva siddhyet kiṃtu anubhava prakāśena vinā tat iti evaṃrūpā katham smṛtiḥ syāt katham ca tayā vinā abhilāṣeṇa vyavahāraḥ syāt anubhavena hi asya sukha sādhana tā niścitā tatas upādānam tatra pūrva anubhava janitāt saṃskārāt etāvat jātam yadi api tat jñānam viṣayeṇa na janitam tathā api tad viṣayam iti na ca etāvatā kiṃcid ātma niṣṭhe sva prakāśa jñāne viṣayasya iva anubhavasya prācyasya aprakāśāt 
ĪPrVV_1,3.2^1	 nanu saṃsś araja tvāt eva prācyam anubhavam api viṣayīkurutām smṛtiḥ iti āśaṅkya āha dṛś svābhāsa eva na anyena vedyāḥ rūpa dṛśā iva dṛś rase saṃskāra ja tvam tu tad tulya tvam na tad gatiḥ dṛś jñānam tat ca jaḍāt vibhidyate sva prakāśa eka rūpa tayā jaḍaḥ hi prakāśāt pṛthak bhūtaḥ vaktavyaḥ tena dṛś su ābhāsā ābhāsaḥ prakāśamānatā sā svam rūpam avyavhicāri yasyāḥ svasya ca ābhāsanam rūpam yasyāḥ sati api bāhye tad śarīra saṃkrāntam na prakāśanam jñānasya rūpam bhavitum arhati para prakāśana ātmaka nija rūpa prakāśanam eva hi sva prakāśa tvam jñānasya bhaṇyate nanu su ābhāsam eva sat tat anubhava jñānam smaraṇe bhāsiṣyate na iti āha na anyena vedyā paratra yadi dṛś bhāseta tarhi na sā su ābhāsā idam eva hi sva prakāśasya lakṣaṇam svayam hi yadi prakāśeta tadā pareṇa saha asaṃbandhāt saṃbandha prāṇā katham paratra iti saptamī saṃgacchatām tathā ca rūpa jñānena rase dṛś rasa viṣayam jñānam na vedyate evam hi cakṣuṣā eva rasaḥ phalatas gṛhītaḥ eva syāt 
ĪPrVV_1,3.2^2	 nanu yadi na ābhāti smaraṇe anubhavaḥ kim tarhi saṃskāreṇa kṛtam syāt rūpa jñānam na rasa jñāna jāt saṃskārāt jātam tat katham ayam prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt saṃskāraḥ eva bhavat saṃbhāvita doṣa bhaṅgāya prabhavet na etat yatas hi asau tad saṃskāra saṃskṛtāt samanantara pratyayāt utthitaḥ smṛti bodhaḥ tena tad sadṛśaḥ bhavatu śāsva asaṃniveśaḥ iva pūrva saṃniveśa tulyaḥ na tu yaḥ yad saṃskārāt jātaḥ sa tasya vedana svabhāvaḥ bhavati iti yuktam sadṛśa tvasya api gatiḥ avagamaḥ katham na hi anubhava jñānam sādṛśyam gamayati na api smṛti jñānam parasparam asaṃvedane dvaya niṣṭha sādṛśya adhyavasāya ayogāt abhyasya ca tad ubhaya vedana rūpasya abhāvāt iti saṃskārāt param sa viṣaya tā mātram smṛteḥ siddham na tu anubhava viṣaya tvam na api asya viṣayasya pūrva anubhava viṣayīkṛta tvam iti niścayaḥ eṣaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,3.3^1	 nanu yadi smṛti jñāne anubhavasya satyataḥ prakāśaḥ syāt tad mukhena ca tad viṣayasya tadā bhavet bhavat ukteḥ avakāśaḥ yāvatā smṛtiḥ vikalpa rūpa tvāt kevalam aparakāśa mānam eva anubhavam tat viṣayam ca adhyavasyati tat iyam bhrānti svabhāvāḥ tatra kaḥ ayam nirbandhaḥ tat etat darśayati śaṅkyamāna tvena atha ātat viṣaya tve api smṛteḥ tad avasāyataḥ dṛṣṭa ālamba natā bhrāntyā na tad darśanam na api tad viṣayaḥ smṛteḥ viṣayaḥ tathā api tu ubhayam adhyavasīyate bhrama rūpa tayā smṛteḥ etat nirākaroti  tat etat asamañjasam atra kārikayā upapattim āha smṛti tā eva katham tāvat bhrānteḥ ca artha sthitiḥ katham 
ĪPrVV_1,3.3^2	 pūrva anubhava saṃkāra apekṣā ca kim iti iṣyate anubhūtasya anubhava prakāśitasya viṣayasya apramoṣaḥ anapahāraḥ tathā eva prakāśanam yat etat smṛteḥ ātmīyam rūpam tat tathā aprakāśana abhāve vighaṭetamām kim ca bhrāntau asat vā ātma ākāraḥ vā prakhyāti na tu tayā arthaḥ svīkriyate tasya aprakāśanāt iti tayā arthaḥ na vyavasthāpitaḥ eva prakāśana ātmā hi vyavasthāpanāḥ tatas ca smaraṇāt abhilāṣeṇa katham artha viṣayaḥ vyavahāraḥ na ca tad aprakāśane saṃskāra ja tvena kiṃcid kṛtyam tat hi sādṛśyam labdhum avalambyate na ca anubhavena viṣaya prakāśana ātmanā smṛti abhidhānāyāḥ bhrānteḥ kicid api sādṛśyam asti sarvathā viṣayam aspṛśantyāḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,3.5^1	 nanu yaḥ anubhavaḥ yaḥ ca tad viṣayaḥ sa yatas tayā adhyavasīyate tatas aṃśāt sādṛśyam anubhavena smṛteḥ tad siddhaye ca saṃskāra parigrahaḥ adhyavasīyate iti kim ucyate prakāśyate iti ced na bhrānti tvam na prakāśyate iti ced punar api viṣayaḥ na spṛṣṭaḥ eva anayā iti sādṛśyam iti śabda gaḍu mātram tat etat darśayitum āha bhrānti tve ca avasāyasya na jaḍāt viṣaya sthitiḥ tatas ajāḍye nija ullekha niṣṭhā at na artha sthitiḥ tatas iha smṛteḥ anyasya vā bhrānti bodhasya sva saṃvedana aṃśe prakāśamāne na bhrāntitā tatra vaiparītya abhāvāt yaḥ tu tatra adhyavasīyate su a ākāraḥ sa viparīta tayā asvākāra tvena artha tayā iti tatra aṃśe bhrāntitā 
ĪPrVV_1,3.5^2	 sa ca aṃśaḥ artha lakṣaṇaḥ na smṛtyā anyayā vā bhrāntyā spṛśyate iti tatra asau tūṣṇīkāḥ iti balāt eva tatra aṃśe jaḍa tvam asyāḥ āyātam ghaṭa jñānasya iva paṭe na ca jaḍena viṣayasya kiṃcid kṛtyam tatas ca artha viṣayaḥ vyavahāraḥ vilupyeta atha tu tam avasāya rūpam sva saṃvedana aṃśam su a ākāram vā avalambya ajaḍa tvam asyāḥ evam api ajāḍye nijam sva saṃvedanam ullekhaḥ ca su ākāraḥ itīyati eṣā pariniṣṭhitā smṛtiḥ iti viṣayasya nāma api prahītum aśaknuvataḥ tatas smṛti adhyavasāyāt katham viṣayasya vyavasthāpanam vyavahārya tva saṃpādana sāmarthyam  
ĪPrVV_1,3.6^1	 saṃskāre sati api smṛtiḥ na kathaṃcana ghaṭate tatas ca paraspara saṅgati hīnāni sakalāni jñānāni iti yat uktam śloka pañcakena tat idānīm prakṛte yojayati evam anyonya bhinnānām aparaspara vedinām jñānānām anusaṃdhāna janmā naśyet jana sthitiḥ janasya lokasya yā kācana sthitiḥ vyavahāraḥ sā sarva jñānānām yat anusaṃdhānam eka viṣaya bhāva upapanna smṛti tā prāpti rūpam tatra āyattā tathā hi smaraṇa nibandhanāḥ sarve vyavahārāḥ prathamam api hi pratyakṣa jñānam aham iti pūrva apara rūpa anusaṃdhānena smaraṇa anuprāṇitena vinā na ghaṭate pramātari viśrānti abhāvāt apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt 
ĪPrVV_1,3.6^2	 evam sukha ādau mantavyam hāna ādāna preraṇa abhyupagamādavastu vyavahārāḥ smaraṇa mayāḥ eva evam jñānānām yat anusaṃdhānam tatas jāyamānā jana sthitiḥ evam iti para abhyupagame sati naśyet naśyati iti saṃbhāvyate kutas iti ced viśeṣaṇa dvāreṇa hetum āha anyonyam tāvat bhinnāni jñānāni anyat anubhava jñānam anyat idānīntanam jñānam vikalpa abhimatam anyat smaraṇa saṃmatam jñānam tat etāni sva viṣaya prakāśa mātra rūpāṇi para viṣaye jaḍa andhāna īḍamūka kalpāni na ca anyonyasya prakāśa rūpāṇi 
ĪPrVV_1,3.7^1	 evam na svarūpataḥ na vedyayaḥ vai ekībhāva rūpam anusaṃdhānam asti anyonyam ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ na asti na ca turyam jñāteya nibandhanam anusandhānādhāyi saṃbhāvyate iti dhvaṃseran vyavahārāḥ na ca dhvaṃsantām iti bhavat abhīṣṭa śāpa mātrāt te dhvaṃsante prakāśante yatas tatas etat āpadyate etat eva samarthayitum udyantavyam iti tat ca asmad abhimata prakāreṇa vinā vidheḥ api aśakya samarthanam iti darśayati na ced antar kṛta ananta viśva rūpaḥ maheśvaraḥ syāt ekaścit vapuḥ jñāna smṛti apohana śaktimān saṃvid tāvat prakāśate iti tāvat na kecid apahnuvate sā tu saṃvid yadi sva ātma mātra viśrāntāḥ arthasya sā katham prakāśaḥ sa hi artha dharmaḥ eva tathā syāt tatas ca artha prakāśaḥ tāvatī eva paryavasitaḥ iti galitaḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,3.7^2	 atas artha prakāśa rūpam saṃvidam icchatā balāt eva arthaḥ api tad rūpa antargataḥ eva aṅgīkratavyaḥ sa ca artha prakāśaḥ yadi anyaḥ ca anyaḥ ca tat na smaraṇam upapannam iti atas ekaḥ eva asau iti eka tvāt sarvaḥ vedya rāśiḥ tena kroḍīkṛtaḥ iti etat api anicchatā aṅgīkāryam evam api satatam eva unmagnena nimagnena vā viśvātmanā prakāśeta tathā svabhāva tvāt na ca evam atas svarūpa antar bruḍitam artha rāśim aparam api bhinna ākāram ātmani parigṛhya kaṃcid eva artham svarūpāt unmagnam ābhāsayati iti āpatitam sā eṣā jñānaśaktiḥ unmagna ābhāsa bhinnam ca cit svarūpam vahiḥ mukha tvāt tad chāyā anurāgāt navam navam jñānam uktam evam api nava nava ābhāsāḥ pratikṣaṇam udayavyaya bhājaḥ iti sā eva vyavahāra nivaha hāniḥ tena kvacid ābhāse gṛhīta pūrve yat saṃvedanam bahirmukham abhūt tasya yat antarmukham cit svarūpa tvam tat kāla antare api avasthā snu sva ātma gatam tad viṣaya viśeṣe bahirmukha tvam parāmṛśati iti eśā smṛti śaktiḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,3.7^3	 yat ca tat navam bhāsayati smarati vā tat vastutas saṃvidā viśva mayyā tādātmya vṛtti iti viśva mayam pūrṇam eva iti navam na kiṃcid ābhāsitam smṛtam vā syāt idam api pravāha patitam urīkāryam yat kila tat ābhāsyate tat saṃvidaḥ vicchiidyate saṃvid ca tatas saṃvid ca saṃvid antarāt saṃvedyam ca saṃvedya antaraāt na ca vicchedanam vastutas saṃbhavati iti vicchedanasya avabhāsa mātram ucyate na ca tat iyatā pāramārthikam nirmīyamāṇasya sarvasya ayam eva parama arthaḥ yatas eṣaḥ eva paritas chedanāt paricchedaḥ ucyate tad avabhāsana sāmarthyam apohana śaktiḥ anena śakti trayeṇa viśve vyavahārāḥ tat ca bhagavataḥ eva śakti trayam yat tathābhūta anubhavitṛ smartṛ vikalpayitṛ svabhāva caitra maitra ādi avabhāsanam 
ĪPrVV_1,3.7^4	 saḥ eva hi tena tena vapuṣā jānāti smarati vikalpayati ca yathā uktam ācāryeṇa eva yadi api artha sthitiḥ prāṇa puryaṣṭaka niyantrite jīve niruddhā tatra api paramātmani sā sthitā ityādi etāsām ca jñāna ādi śaktīnām asaṃkhya prakāraḥ vaicitrya vikalpaḥ iti tad sāmarthyam svātantryam apara adhīnam pūrṇam mahat aiśvaryam tad nirmita brahma viṣṇu rudra ādi aiśvarya apekṣayā ucyate tat evam cit vapuḥ iti ekam kṛtvā iyat āyātam viśva rūpaḥ iti tatas eva ca pariniṣṭhita eka rūpa jaḍa bhāva vailakṣaṇyāt jñāna ādi śakti yukta tāmāha īśvaryam upasaṃprāptaḥ etad anupagame na kiṃcid idam bhāseta iti prasaṅgaḥ bhāsate tu tasmāt etat avaśya aṅgīkartavyam iti prasaṅga viparyayaḥ naśyet jana sthitiḥ yadi evam na syāt iti prāktanena ślokena saha saṃbandhaḥ ced iti anena tad viparyayaḥ sūcitaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,4.0^1	 padārtha ratna nikaram nija hṛd gañja puñjitam grathnantam smṛti sūtra antar saṃtatyā eva stumaḥ śivam evam jñāna pūrvikā smṛtiḥ tad ubhaya anugrāhiṇī apohana śaktiḥ iti tāvat vastu saṃbhava krameṇa pradarśitam upakrama anusāreṇa smṛtiḥ eva sūcita prasaṅga viparyaya samarthana dṛśā vivecyāḥ satyam kiṃtu smṛti jñānam iti hi upakrāntam tatra saṃskāra mātrāt tāvat mā nāma udapādi smṛtiḥ idam tu vaktavyam tathābhūta bhavat abhyupagata bhagavat prabhāvaḥ api katham enām kuryāt iti śaṅkām śamayitum smṛti tattva nirūpaṇāyasa hi pūrva anubhūta artha upalabdhā ityādi arthau bhātaḥ pramātari iti antam śloka aṣṭakam tatra ślokena sva pakṣe smṛtiḥ upapannāḥ iti kathitam 
ĪPrVV_1,4.0^2	 dvitīyena smṛteḥ pūrva anubhava viṣayīkṛta sva lakṣaṇa prakāśana sāmarthyam uktam tṛtīyena anubhavena tad viṣayeṇa ca ekībhāva paryantaḥ āveśaḥ smaraṇasya uktaḥ turyeṇa anubhavasya na viṣaya tayā smṛtyā prakāśanam iti nirūpitam pañcamena yogi jñānam api anubhavam pṛthak bhāvena na viṣayīkaroti iti baḍatā turya śloka arthaḥ eva upodvalitaḥ ṣaṣṭhena āśaṅkyamānam anubhavasya smṛtyā pṛthak viṣayīkaraṇam kākpanikam iti avāstavīkṛtam saptamena smṛti prasaṅgāt vikalpe api pūrva anubhavena aikya ātma āveśaḥ darśitaḥ aṣṭamena smartavyasya smṛteḥ smartuḥ ca ekacit tattva viśrāntiḥ uktā prasaṅgāt ca dṛśyasya darśanasya draṣṭuḥ ca iti tātparya arthaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,4.1^1	 atha krameṇa śloka arthaḥ ucyate sa hi pūrva anubhūta artha upalabdhā paratas api san vimṛśan saḥ iti svairī smarati iti apadiśyate pūrvam anubhūtasya arthasya yaḥ upalandhāḥ antarmukhaḥ bodhaḥ sa tāvat adya api paratas smṛti kāle api asti eva saṃvid mātra svarūpasya kāla kṛta saṃkoca rūpa viśeṣa ātmaka avaccheda ayogāt anubhavasya ca antar arthaḥ api apṛthagbhāvena avasthitaḥ iti etat api ayatna siddham iyat tu cintyam akāla kalite saṃvedane tad antar vartini ca viśvatra bhāva jāte yadi tāvat cit mayatā parāmarśaḥ tat aham iti etāvatā eva pūrṇena vimarśena bhāvyam atha idamtayā pṛthak bhāva avabhāsanena tathā api tatra dvayī gatiḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,4.1^2	 aham iti aṃśe yadi viśrānyati idantā tadā aham idamiti sadāśiva ādi daśayā bhāvyam atha na rohati tat idam iti eva ābhāsanena bhavitavyam apūrva tā ābhāsanāt ca tat anubhavanam eva syāt na smaraṇam iti āśaṅgya āha svairī iti svam ātmīyam upakaraṇam īrayati sva kartavyeṣu avaśyam tad śīlaḥ ca svam ca ātmānam īrayati na punar sva kartavye prerakam apekṣate iti svairī svatantraḥ tena svatantra tvāt saḥ iti vimṛśati 
ĪPrVV_1,4.1^3	 saḥ iti vimarśanasya ca iyat rūpam yat sarvathā akāla kalita svarūpa parāmarśanam eva na na api atyantam bhedena vimarśanam eva api tu yaḥ bhāvaḥ pūrvam anubhava kāle tad deśa kāla pramātṛ antara sācivyena pṛthakkṛtaḥ na ca ahantāyām eva līnīkṛtaḥ sa tādṛś eva tamasā ivaḥ ācchādya avasthāpitaḥ saṃskāra śabda vācyaḥ tasya tam ācchādakam apahastayati tatra apahastite sa pūrvavat pṛthakkṛte eva avabhāti nanu ca idantayā avabhāset pūrvavat eva na evam tadānīntana avabhāsana pṛthak kṛta śarīra ādi saṃbandham anavadhūya eva hi tad prakāśaḥ tatas ca idānīntana avabhāsana smaraṇa kāla parāmarśaḥ api na nimīlati iti tad parāmarśa bhitti prādhānyena pūrva kāla parāmarśaḥ iti viruddha pūrva apara parāmarśa svabhāvaḥ eva saḥ iti parāmarśaḥ ucyate 
ĪPrVV_1,4.1^4	 evam ca saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ smarati etat eva hi tasya smartṛ tvam yat evaṃprakāra parāmarśa ucita kāla kalā ādi sparśa sahiṣṇu māyā pramātṛ bhāva parigrahaḥ iti māyā avidyā dvayā dvaya m ayam tatas eva sakala siddhi vitaraṇa catura cintāmaṇi prakhyam āgamikāḥ smaraṇam eva mantra ādi prāṇitam manyante tathā ca dhyāna ādi bhāvam smṛtiḥ eva labdhvā cintāmaṇiḥ tvad vibhavam vyanakti iti alam tāvat anena tṛnnanta samāsena yatnataḥ anubhavasya artha mukhena kāla sparśam artha viśrānta tām dvayoḥ api pramātari nirūḍhim bheda abhedābhyām darśayati vṛttaḥ eka arthībhāvāt tasya ca bheda abheda maya tvam iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,4.2^1	 etat eva smṛti tattvam upapādayitum śloka antarāṇi tatra yadi kaścid brūyāt iha smṛtiḥ vikalpaḥ na ca anena arthaḥ prakāśyate artha asaṃsparśinaḥ hi vikalpāḥ anubhavena ca yena saḥ arthaḥ prakāśa tām nītaḥ saḥ idānīm kīrti mātra mūrtiḥ jātaḥ na ca saḥ api smṛtyā prakāśyate jñānasya jñāna antareṇa asaṃvedya tvāt asattvāt ca iti arthasya prakāśana abhāvāt idam smarāmi iti jñānam bhrānti mātram eva iti punar api āpatitam iti tadā tam prati ucyate bhāsayet ca sva kāle arthāt pūrva ābhāsitam āmṛśan sva lakṣaṇam ghaṭa ābhāsa mātreṇa atha akhila ātmanā 
ĪPrVV_1,4.2^2	 iha smṛti vikalpe tāvat arthaḥ avasīyate anyathā supta mūrcchita kalpa tā āpatteḥ evam ca yāvat adhyavasāyaḥ arthasya tāvat arthāt iti sāmarthyāt iyat abhyupagantavyam yat saḥ arthaḥ prakāśate aprakāśamāne adhyavasātavye adhyavasāyaḥ andha prāyaḥ syāt prakāśanam ca na tad ānīntana kālasya tyāgena na api dvīkāreṇa idam iti eva avabhāsana prasaṅgāt tasmāt atīta anubhava kālaḥ pūrva anubhūta bhāva sva alakṣaṇyākṣepaka tvena apekṣaṇīyaḥ vedya bhāge prakāśa ātmaka avabhāsa abhiniveśitayā smartṛ deha prāṇa ādi avabhāsa kālaḥ ca avalambanīyaḥ vedaka bhāge vimarśa aṃśa abhiniveśi tvena 
ĪPrVV_1,4.2^3	 ābhāsa mātram hi bhāvasya sva rūpam pratyābhāsam pramāṇasya vyāpārāt tat eva ābhāsa antara vyāmiśraṇayā dipa sahasra prabhā saṃmūrcchana vat sphuṭībhavati ābhāsa antara vyāmiśraṇa abhāve api tu kāla ābhāsa saṃbhedena eva svālakṣaṇyam tasya ābhāsasya karoti kāla śakteḥ eva bhedaka tvāt iti vakṣyate evam tāvat sva lakṣaṇī bhāvaḥ prāktana deha ābhāsa sācivya abhyudita kāla ābhāsayā ghaṭa ābhāsasya iti tāvatī eva vā smṛtiḥ ābhāsā antaraiḥ api vyāmiśrāḥ ati sphuṭa iti atyanta sphuṭībhāve api tad ānīntana kālatā na truṭyati anya sādhāraṇya anavabhāvāt tathā avabhāse tu yoginaḥ tad nirmāṇam eva 
ĪPrVV_1,4.2^4	 brahma bhāṣita ādau tu navam eva avabhāsanam iti atra tu āgama ādi māna antara anubhūta brahma ādi svarūpa smaraṇa paramparā abhyupāyaḥ bhāsayet iti vidhi rūpeṇa niyogena niyamaḥ lakṣyate na bhāsayati iti etat na api tu bhāsayati eva iti sva kāle iti smaraṇa kāle āmṛśan iti vedaka bhāga niveśī vartamāna kāle uktaḥ pūrva ābhāsitam sva lakṣaṇam iti vedya aṃśa sparśī bhūtakālaḥ ghaṭa ābhāsasya api kevalasya svālakṣaṇya āpatti hetuḥ darśitaḥ iyat eva smṛteḥ avyavhi cāri vapuḥ arthita atiśayāt tu sphuṭa tvam iti atha śabdaḥ dyotayati tat eva āha asvila ātmanā iti sarva ābhāsa miśreṇa vapuṣā iti arthaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,4.3^1	 nanu evam sva lakṣaṇasya prakāśane bhedena bahis tad avabhāseta etat eva hi bahis avabhāsanam yat sva lakṣaṇa prakāśanam iti śaṅkā śamanāya nirūpayati na ca yuktam smṛteḥ bhede smaryamāṇasya bhāsanam tena aikyam bhinna kālānām saṃvidām vedita eṣa saḥ smaraṇa jñānāt bhinna tvena bahīrūpa tayā yadi saḥ arthaḥ bhāseta smaryamāṇasya ca yat bhāsanam tat eva na syāt smaryamāṇam eva tat na syāt anubhūyamānam eva tat bhavet iti yāvat nanu ca evam katham sva lakṣaṇasya prakāśanam uktam etat naḥ idāṇīm prakāśanam api tu pūrva kāle eva tadā ca asau bahis avabhāsate eva nanu ca idānīm tarhi kim vimarśanam iti brūmaḥ nanu prakāśana vimarśanayoḥ bhinna kāla tvam āpatitam tatas kim ubhayam api na kiṃcid syāt anyonya jīvita tvāt asya 
ĪPrVV_1,4.3^2	 mā evam yasya hi saṃvedanāni eva bhinnāni tattvam tasya idam apratisamādheyam eva asmad darśane tu bhinna kālāḥ api saṃvidaḥ tad kāla atyāgena eva ekatā avabhāsanena svatantraḥ pramātā yāvat antar mukha tayā tāvatī aṃśe vimṛśati tāvat prakāśasya tātkālika bahirbhāva ābhāsaḥ vimarśasya idānīntana antarmukhā sthitiḥ iti etat eva vedanā adhikam veditṛ tvam vedaneṣu saṃyojana viyojanayoḥ yathāruci karaṇam svātantryam kartṛ tvam ca etat eva ucyate ghaṭam aham anvabhūvam iti vā sa ghaṭaḥ iti vai aikyam anusaṃdhānam anusaṃdha ātura bhinnam iti darśayitum yat eva aikyam saḥ eva veditāḥ iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena darśitam eṣa saḥ iti ācchāditasya iva pramātṛ tattvasya sphuṭa avabhāsanam kṛtam idam iti vismaya garbhayā anayā uktyā pratyabhijñā eva sūcitā yat āha granthakāraḥ eva ittham sva saṃvittim apahnuvānaiḥ yat tat vadadbhiḥ kaluṣīkṛtam yat pramātṛ tattvam sphuṭa yuktibhiḥ tān mūkān vidhāya prakaṭīkṛtam tat iti 
ĪPrVV_1,4.4^1	 nanu ca prācyaḥ eva anubhavaḥ yadi smaryamāṇasya bahis avabhāsana rūpaḥ prakāśaḥ tarhi iyat ucyatām saḥ anubhavaḥ idānīm smaraṇena viṣayīkriyate iti aikyena tu alaukikena kaḥ arthaḥ iti vyāmoham vihantum āha na eva hi anubhavaḥ bhāti smṛtau pūrvaḥ arthavat pṛthak prāc anvabhūvam aham iti ātma ārohaṇa bhāsanāt pūrvaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ arthaḥ pṛthak iti idantayā bhāti sma na evam smaraṇa kāle smṛti jñānāt pṛthaktvena idam pūrvam anubhavanam iti bhāti yathā ca smṛti kāle tasmāt smṛti jñānāt saḥ arthaḥ prāk iti pūrva svabhāvaḥ na bhedena ābhāti smṛti kāle bahis avabhāsa abhāvāt evam tatas eva hetoḥ pūrvaḥ api anubhavaḥ na bhedena ābhāti katham tarhi ubhayam bhāti anvabhūvam iti evam 
ĪPrVV_1,4.4^2	 etat kim ucyate iti ced aham iti evaṃsvabhāvaḥ yaḥ ātmā pūrva apara saṃvid antarmukha svabhāvaḥ tatra yat ārohaṇam viśramaḥ tena hetunā pūrva saṃvid rūpa tāyāḥ sva prakāśāyāḥ bhāsanāt tat lonasya api ghaṭasya sva prakāśa deśīya tvena bhāsanam ātmani ca ārohaṇam viśramaṇā anubhavasya arthasya ca prakṛti pratyayau pratyaya artham saha brūtaḥ iti nyāyāt saṃkhyā ākṣipte tadvati vā kartṛ bhūte asmad arthe anubhavaḥ bruḍitaḥ tad dvāreṇa arthaḥ api ca na tu svātantryeṇa eva asau tad artham eva karma na nirdiṣṭam ghaṭa ādiḥ punar anubhava kāle na asmad artham ārohati hi yasmāt na eva bhāti pūrvaḥ anubhavaḥ pṛthak apara ardha uktāt hetoḥ tasmāt saṃvidāma aikyam iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ luṅā bhūtakālasya dyotita tvāt prāk iti bhinnakramaḥ uttama puruṣeṇa asmad arthasya aham iti api ārohaṇam iti ruhiḥ iti aṇijantaḥ ṇijanta upi 
ĪPrVV_1,4.5^1	 nanu kaḥ evam āha anubhavaḥ pṛthak na bhāti iti ghaṭa vat na bhāti iti ced kim tatas ghaṭaḥ api hi na anubhava sakhyaḥ bhāti iti kim na bhāti svabhāvena bhāti iti tu ubhayatra api samānam tathā hi atīta anāgata sūkṣma ādi yathā yogi jñāne viṣayībhavati iti abhyupagatam tathā para cittam api pratyayasya para citta jñānam ityādau tatra jñāna vṛtti pariṇatam eva sattvam citta śabdena uktam anyathā pratyayasya saṃyama viṣayī kārya tvam katham ucyeta ālambana yogaḥ ca katham śaṅkayeta na ca sa ālambanam iti 
ĪPrVV_1,4.5^2	 tasmāt parakīyam anubhavanam iva nijam api viṣayīkriyatām iti āśaṅkya dṛṣṭāntaḥ eva asiddhaḥ iti bhānti iti antena abhyupagamena vā siddha tve api prakṛte arthe viṣamaḥ iti śeṣeṇa darśayati yoginām api bhāsante na dṛśaḥ darśana antare sva saṃvid eka mānāḥ tāḥ bhānti meya pade api vā yoginām yat etat darśana antaram bhāvanā ādi udbhavaḥ para citta viṣayaḥ jñāna viśeṣaḥ tatra dṛśaḥ iti upalabdhayaḥ na bhānti tathā hi saugatānām tāvat sva prakāśa eka rūpam jñānam tat ced jñāna antareṇa vedyam tarhi yat asya nijam vapuḥ ananya vedya tayā prakāśanam nāma na tat prakāśitam syāt sāṃkhyānām api puruṣa= chāyā eva upalabdhiḥ puruṣaḥ ca asaṃvedya parvāḥ iti katham vedyā syāt 
ĪPrVV_1,4.5^3	 vaiśeṣikāṇām api ātmani abhedena samavāyi saṃvedanam para gatam manasā katham gṛhyeta antar śarīra vṛttinā tad śarīra antaranupraveśe tu tasya eva aham iti śarīrīkaraṇāt ahanta avabhāsita tvāt ātmanaḥ bhedaḥ vigalet nitya anumeya tvam tu naḥ ātmanaḥ upapadyate jñānasya ca jñāna antara vedya tve anavasthāna ādi uktam tasmāt yoginaḥ para citta vedanā avasare iyān prakāśaḥ etad deha prakāśa sahacārī ghaṭa sukha ādi prakāśaḥ iti tatra ghaṭa sukha ādi idantayā bhāti tad gataḥ tu prakāśaḥ aham iti eva sva prakāśa tayā prakāśate 
ĪPrVV_1,4.5^4	 pramātrīkṛta para deha prāṇa ādi samavabhāsa saṃskārāt tu tad niṣṭhām idantām eva prakāśa bhāge api manyamānaḥ idam para jñānam iti abhimanyate avigalita sva para vibhāgaḥ yogī prāpta prakarṣaḥ tu sarvam ātma tvena paśyan sva sṛṣṭam eva sva para vibhāgam manyate iti jñānasya na yogi jñānena prakāśyatā bhavatu vā tathā api prakṛtam naḥ etad samam tathā hi ayam anubhavati iti para niṣṭhaḥ eva asau anubhave yoginaḥ prakāśaḥ na tu aham anubhavāmi iti ātma āroheṇa vartamānaḥ iha tu anvabhūvam iti aham aṃśa viśrāntiḥ anālīḍha idaṃbhāva eva anubhavasya iti yuktam uktam yasmāt anubhavaḥ pṛthak na bhāti tasmāt aikyam bhinna kālānām saṃvidām veditāḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,4.6^1	 yadi ahaṃa bhāva viśrānti vaśāt anubhavaḥ smṛtau pṛthak na bhāti iti ucyate tadā parāmarśa antaram sākṣāt eva idantayā anubhavam parāmṛśat yadi vā idaṃbhāva ucita ghaṭa ādi viśrānta tām anubhavasya prathayat upalabdham iti tad anusāreṇa api kim na vyavahriyate iti para abhiprāyam pratikṣipati smaryate yat dṛś āsīt me sā evam iti api bhedataḥ tad vyākaraṇam eva asyāḥ mayā dṛṣṭam iti smṛteḥ lokasya tāvat evam na saṃvedanam sa hi na pṛthak bhūtām dṛśam kāṃcid manyate sā dṛś me āsīt iti evam evam api tu yat smaryate evaṃbhūtam api yat smaraṇam kasyacid vivecakaṃmanyasya tat smṛteḥ vyākaraṇam padasya iva prakṛti pratyaya artha nirūpaṃam kālpanikam vibhajya ākaraṇam paratra pratipādana mātram saḥ api yadi mūlaprati iti vedayate pūrva ukta krameṇa tadā anubhavam pṛthak bhūtam na veda yatas eva tat rāhoḥ śiraḥ iti vat kalpitam bhedam manyate anyathā sa ghaṭaḥ iti vat sā dṛś iti atra api prāktanam dṛś antaram apekṣaṇīyam syāt 
ĪPrVV_1,4.6^2	 tat iti anena hi ghaṭasya vā dṛśaḥ vā pūrva anubhava viṣaya āpattiḥ ucyate anyathā dṛś iti eva syāt tatas ca dṛś mayā dṛś antareṇa anubhūtāḥ iti āpatet tatra api tathātve anavasthā nanu smṛteḥ maulikam kim rūpam ucyate mayā dṛṣṭam iti nanu atra dayitā vadana nalina ādi viśrāntam darśanam uktam na tu ātma ārūḍham karmaṇi niṣṭhā utpatteḥ saḥ eṣa sva vācam eva na cetayati kartuḥ kriyayā hi āpyam karma iti dṛśi kriyāyāḥ kartṛ niṣṭhatā eva tathā ca kartṛ sthām eva dṛśikriyām āhuḥ darśayate bhṛtyān rājā ityādau jaiminīyaiḥ api jñāna rūpā dṛśiḥ bhāvanā ātmikā pramātṛ viśrāntā eva uktā kevalam prakaṭa tā viṣaya dharmaḥ dṛṣṭa tā ākhyā anyā saṃvid vā asvatantrāḥ iti anyat etat pramātṛ viśrānta tvam eva kathayitum mayā iti uktam tena anvabhūvam aham mayā anubhūtam iti śabda vaicitrya mātram idam na tu artha bhedaḥ anye tu bhinna krama tvena yojayanti dṛś āsīt sā me iti evam mayā dṛṣṭam iti ca yat smaraṇam tat vyākaraṇam asyāḥ iti anantara ukta anvabhūvam iti ucita parāmarśāyāḥ smṛteḥ iti apiḥ ca arthe 
ĪPrVV_1,4.7^1	 nanu dṛṣṭam api nirvikalpakena yāvat na parāmṛṣṭam vimarśa viśeṣa viśrāntyā tāvat na smaryate mārga dṛṣṭam iva tṛṇa parṇa ādi viśeṣeṇa rūpeṇa tat idam eva vicāraṇīyam samanantara bhāvi vikalpa kāle tad darśanam idantayā avabhāta pūrvam vā na vā iti tat etat āśaṅkya āha yā ca paśyāmi aham imam ghaṭaḥ ayam iti vā avasā manyate samavetam sā api avasātari darśanam iha darśanam yādṛśam nijena vapuṣā tādṛśena eva tena bhātavyam sarvadā tat ca sva kāle ananya prakāśam aham iti etāvatā svarūpeṇa ucita prakāśam tad vikalpa aṃśa vicāraḥ tāvat na kutracid aṅgam bhavatu vā aṅgam kim tu avasāyaḥ api evaṃbhūtaḥ iti api śabdena sūcayati tatra samanantara bhāvinā vikalpena vastu parāmṛśyamānam anubhava parāmarśa mukhena vā parāmṛśyate aham imam paśyāmi iti vartamāna tayā imam iti anena ca pratyakṣa vyāpāra tvam pratyakṣāyamāṇa tvena darśitam evam eva vā parāmṛśyate ghaṭaḥ ayam iti atra ayaṃśabdena pratyakṣāyamāṇa tvam uktam 
ĪPrVV_1,4.7^2	 tatra antye vikalpe darśanasya pṛthak parāmarśaḥ eva na asti iti kā tatra idantā śaṅkā tatas ca pāriśeṣyāt ahantayā tasya atra asti parāmarśaḥ tad abhāve vikalpasya nimīlita akṣe api bhāvāt svayam artha sparśe sati sphuṭam aviṣaya paryavasitaḥ katham adhyavasāyaḥ bhavet ādye tu darśanam parāmṛṣṭam api asmad arthe antarbhūtam ahaṃbhāva āspadam avasātari viśrāntam sva prakāśam eva parāmṛṣṭam iti vikalpaḥ api na bodha antara bodhyatām bodhayati bodhasya avasāyaḥ avasāḥ samavetam iti apṛthagbhāvam āha avasātari iti svatantre antarmukhe bodha ātmani ahanta āspade iti arthaḥ darśanam iti nirvikalpakam anubhavanam upalakṣaṇam ca etat vikalpa smṛti ādeḥ api jñānasya jñāna antareṇa parāmarśe hi ayam eva nyāyaḥ vikalpayāmi aham smarāmi aham vikalpitam mayā smṛtam mayā iti ahanta ārūḍhyā eva vikalpa ādeḥ avabhāsāt atas eva ātmanaḥ amī vikalpa ādyāḥ śakti viśeṣāḥ tad viśrānta śarīra tvāt iti darśitam jñāna smṛti apohana śaktimān iti atra 
ĪPrVV_1,4.8^1	 evam iyataḥ prameyasya yat phalam tat upasaṃhartum āha tat mayā dṛśyate dṛṣṭaḥ ayam saḥ iti āmṛśati api grāhya grāhaka tā bhinnau= arthau bhātaḥ pamātari tat iti tasmāt arthe pūrva uktasya prameyasya hetu bhāvena upajīvanam iha sūcayati yatas evam uktam anubhavasya arthasya iva smaraṇāt na bhedena avabhāsaḥ smrṭi śaktiḥ ca parameśvarasya eva tatas idam atra pariniṣṭhitam tattvam iti iha smṛtiḥ anubhavam kroḍīkaroti iti uktam 
ĪPrVV_1,4.8^2	 anubhavaḥ ca dvidhā  parāmarśa bhedāt kadācid sva ātma parāmarśa pūrvakam anubhāvyam parāmṛśati yatra asya abhisaṃdhi pradhāna tā mayā dṛśyate iti kadācid anubhavanīyam eva pradhāna tayā parāmṛśati yatra anabhisaṃdheḥ eva sahasā vastu upanipātaḥ artha kriyām prati āgraha viśeṣaḥ vai ayam iti tatra api ca prakāśa parāmarśaḥ asti eva anyathā prakāśa ayogāt evam ubhayathā anubhave pratyekam smṛtiḥ api dvaya parāmarśa mayī udeti iti catvāraḥ smaraṇa bhedāḥ dvau anubhava bhedau anusaṃdhānam pratyabhijñānam api etad ubhaya melana ātmakam atra eva antarbhūtam tat ca etad bhedāt aṣṭadhā pūrva apara viśrānti kṛtāt pratyekam dvidhā bhedāt ca ṣoḍaśadhā tat ete dvāviṃśatiḥ saṃvedana bhedāḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,4.8^3	 teṣu ca grāhyam tāvat prakāśāt abahiḥ bhūtam anyathā prakāśana ayogāt bahis bhūtam ca tat anyathārtha tva asaṃbhavāt na ca tatas eva tadā eva tat eva apṛthak bhūtam atra pṛthak bhūtam ca bhavati iti nūnam anyaḥ kalpita prakāśa ātmā kaścid atra arthaḥ asti yatas ayam artha rāśiḥ pṛthak bhavan anyonyam api pṛthaktām adhigacchet anyathā prakāśa abhinnānām parasparam api kathaṅkāram pṛthak bhāvaḥ bhavet saḥ ayam vedya eka deśaḥ eva vicchinnaḥ eva anujjhita vedya bhāvaḥ eva aham iti viccheda śūmya prakāśa ucitena parāmarśena parāmṛśyamānaḥ māyā pramātāḥ iti vakṣyate dehe buddhau iti atra sa ca grāhakaḥ iti ucyate evam samam eva sva ātmani nirmala m akura sthānīye yat yugalakam svasmāt prakāśa rūpāt avyatiriktam avabhāsayati parameśvaraḥ tat eva etat bhagavataḥ jñāna kartṛ tvam smaraṇa kartṛ tvam jñāna śakti smṛti śakti rūpam ucyate iti tātparya arthaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,4.8^4	 akṣara arthaḥ tu mayā dṛśyate iti ayam iti ca yat āmṛśati pramātā prakāśa rūpaḥ yena anubhavati iti ucyate tatas āmarśanāt etat lakṣyate grāhya rūpeṇa grāhaka rūpeṇa yojitau ghaṭa ādi deha ādi svabhāvau arthau vedyau pramātari viśuddha prakāśa rūpe bhātaḥ prakāśete evam dṛṣṭaḥ iti saḥ iti ca yat parāmṛśati prakāśa rūpaḥ pramātā yatas asau smarati iti vyapadeśyaḥ tatas api etat eva lakṣyate anubhava rūpa upajīvi tvam pūrva uktam draḍhayitum prasaṅgāt atra jñāna śakteḥ api unmīlanam kṛtam lakṣaṇe śatra ādeśaḥ api śabdaḥ ca arthe artha śabdaḥ vicchinna vedya vācī grāhakaḥ māyīyaḥ kalpitaḥ pramātāḥ aśuddha prakāśa svabhāvaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.0^1	 mahā guhā antar nirmagna bhāva jāta prakāśakaḥ jñāna śakti pradīpena yaḥ sadā tam stumaḥ śivam evam tāvat smṛti śakteḥ svarūpam pratipāditam adhunā tad upajīvanīya jñāna śakti parama artha nirṇayam vitatya vartamāna avabhāsñām iti ādikayā sa kramam pratibhāsate iti antayā śloka ekaviṃśatyā nirūpayati tatra ādya iva ślokena vastuni pratijñām karoti evaṃbhūtā jñānaśaktiḥ iti tatas śloka dvayena prakāśaḥ eva arthānām svarūpa iti āha tatas dvayena prakāśa bāhyānām arthānām sadbhāvam vijñāna vādi upagata vāsanā dūṣaṇena dṛḍhīkṛtam āśaṅkya tṛtīyena tad anabhyupagame api tāvat na kiñcid uparudhyate iti darśayati atha ślokena sva darśane artha tattvam upadarśayan bāhya artha sadbhāve pratyakṣam parākaroti pramāṇa tvena 
ĪPrVV_1,5.0^2	 tatas dvayena anumeya tām api bāhyasya nirasyati anantaram ślokena cit ātmani arthānām avaśyam sadbhāvaḥ parāmarśa ātmanā iti prakaṭayati tatas api prakāśasya pramātṛ rūpasya pratyavamarśaḥ eva jīvatam iti śloka catuṣṭayena anubhava āgama nyāya svarūpa nirūpaṇābhiḥ abhidhatte anantaram jñāna parāmarśaḥ eva jñeyam śuddham pramātṛ rūpa tā an ujjhitam ca prakṣayati iti tasya eva pradhāna tve nyāyam śloka trayeṇa āha prakāśa eka rūpa tve ca jñāna jñātra ādi bhinnam iti ślokena āha tatas jñātari iva viśuddhe jñāne api avikalpaka sa vikalpaka rūpe vimarśaḥ eva prāṇitam iti śloka dvayena āha tatas jñātuḥ jñānasya ca pūrva pakṣe dūṣi yat bhinna tvam tat upasaṃhāra diśā ślokena samarthayate iti tātparyam āhnikasya śloka arthaḥ tu nirūpyate 
ĪPrVV_1,5.1	 nanu smaraṇa vikalpa ādīnām anubhavaḥ eva jīvitam tatra yadi bhedena ābhāsa ante arthāḥ tat teṣu api tathā eva avabhāsaḥ ucitaḥ no ced anyathā tad anubhavaḥ eva tāvat jñāna śakti rūpaḥ vicāraṇīyaḥ iti āśayena āha vartamāna avabhāsānām bhāvānām avabhāsanam antar sthitavatām eva ghaṭate bahis ātmanā vartamāna tvena sphuṭa tayā avabhāsanam idam iti evam ākāram yeṣām teṣām yat etat bahis ātmanā kalpita māyīya śūnyādi śarīra anta pramātṛ pṛthak bhāvena hetunā bhinnānām tatas māyā pramātuḥ vicchinnānām avabhāsanam tat parama artha pramātari śuddha cit maye antar sthitavatām tena saha aikātmyam anujjhitavatām eva ghaṭate pramāṇena upapadyate tena anujjhita saṃvid abhedasya bhāvasya kalpita pramātṛ apekṣayā bhedena prakāśanam bhagavataḥ jñāna śaktiḥ iti uktam bhavati 
ĪPrVV_1,5.2^1	 pramāṇena upapadyate iti uktam tat pramāṇam darśayati prāk iva arthaḥ aprakāśaḥ syāt prakāśa ātma tayā vinā na ca prakāśaḥ bhinnaḥ syāt ātma arthasya prakāśa tā arthaḥ nīla ādiḥ tasya nīla ādi rūpa tā eva yadi prakāśam ānatā na punar sā aparā kācid artha śarīra uttīrṇā prakāśa ātma tā tarhi yathā sarvān prati nīlam eva tad saṃbhāvanayā bhaṇyate na kaṃcid vā prati vastutas vā sva ātmani eva tat nīlam parasya para niṣṭhatvā anupapatteḥ sva ātmani vā na nīlam na anīlam prakāśa anugraheṇa vinā vyavasthāna ayogāt 
ĪPrVV_1,5.2^2	 tathā prakāśamānatā api asya sarvān prati na kaṃcid vā prati api tu sva ātmani eva sva ātmani api vā na syāt iti andhatā jagataḥ atha indriya āloka ādi kṣaṇa vargāt prakāśa rūpaḥ asau nīlakṣaṇaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ eva jātaḥ evam api saḥ eva prasaṅgaḥ prakaṭa tā vāde api ayam eva doṣaḥ sarvathā artha śarīra viśrāntaḥ ced prakāśaḥ mama avabhāsate iti pramātṛ lagna tayā prakāśa sthitiḥ durupapādāḥ pramātā hi tadānīm indriya ādi mayaḥ artha rūpa prakāśasya kāraṇam bhavet bījam iva aṅkurasya na ca aṅkuraḥ bīja apekṣaḥ aṅkura ātmā tatas yadi na prakāśa ātmā sa syāt prāk iva jñāna udayāt pūrvam yathā asau= aprakāśaḥ tathā jñāna udaye api syāt 
ĪPrVV_1,5.2^3	 nanu jñānam artha prakāśa rūpam eva tat katham jñānasya udayānudayayoḥ arthasya tulya tā syāt syāt etat yadi upapadyet yāvatā arthāt bhinnam yat jñānam prakāśa rūpam tat arthasya saṃbandhi tayā katham syāt yadi tāvat arthaḥ prakāśate iti evaṃbhūtam jñānasya svarūpam tat artha jñānayoḥ abhedaḥ eva āyātaḥ artha svabhāvasya jñāna tvena ukta tvāt artha svabhāva tve ca sati prakāśasya artha ātma tāyām uktam dūṣaṇam atha artham prakāśayati iti jñānasya sva rūpam tarhi prakāśamānam artham karoti jñānam iti āpatite punar api saḥ eva doṣaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.2^4	 kṛta pratānaḥ ca ayam prakṛti arthaṇī artha vivekaḥ mayā eva bheda vidāraṇe iti tatas eva anveṣyaḥ tasmāt bhinnaḥ prakāśaḥ arthasya saṃbandhī bhavati iti saṃbhāvanā eva na asti tat ca idam upapattyā āyātam arthasya svarūpam prakāśamānatā prakāśa abhinna tvam iti prakāśaḥ ca yadi ghaṭe anyaḥ paṭe anyaḥ tadā anusaṃdhānasya ayogaḥ dvayoḥ prakāśayoḥ sva ātma mātra paryavasānāt iti vitatya upapāditam naśyet jana sthitiḥ iti atra tasmāt ekaḥ eva prakāśaḥ etat eva āvṛttyā darśitam na ca prakāśaḥ bhinnaḥ syāt iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.3^1	 vyatiriktasya jñānasya artha prakāśa rūpa tām abhyupagamya api bādhaka antaram āha bhinne prakāśe ca abhinne saṃkaraḥ viṣayasya tat prakāśa ātmā prakāśyaḥ arthaḥ na aprakāśaḥ ca siddhyati yadi arthāt anyaḥ eva jñāna ātmā prakāśaḥ atas eva bhinnaḥ arthataḥ tarhi sva ātmani tasya prakāśa mātra rūpa tvāt abhedaḥ eva tathā hi nīlasya prakāśaḥ pītasya prakāśaḥ iti yaḥ nīla aṃśaḥ pīta aṃśaḥ ca sa na tāvat jñānasya sva rūpam bheda vāda tyāga āpatteḥ atha viṣayaḥ tat eva idam vicāryate iha prakāśa balāt nīla pītayoḥ bhedaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ yena eva ca prakāśena nīlaḥ nīlaḥ eva iti upagamyate tena eva ca prakāśena pītaḥ pītaḥ iti katham saṃgacchatām nīlena janitaḥ pītena janitaḥ tena vā saha samāna sāmagrīkaḥ ityādi yat ucyate tat siddhe nīla pītayoḥ bhede syāt saḥ eva vicāryaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.3^2	 atha nīla ākāraḥ asau tat yadi pratibimba balāt tad dvitīya bimba anavabhāsāt ayuktam atha abhedaḥ tarhi tyaktaḥ bheda vādaḥ tathā karaṇa tā ādi vāde śikhara stha jñānam bahutara nīlā ādi janyam ekatra paṭu anyatra mandam iti katham bhedaḥ prakāśa śarīrasya abhedāt tathābhūte ca anyatara darśana udbhūte api saṃskāre balāt eva aśeṣa smaraṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti bhūyān saṅkaraḥ syāt etat arthaḥ eva astu kim anena doṣa āpādakena prakāśena iti atra āha aprakāśasya prasiddhiḥ eva na kācid sva ātmani hi nīlam yadi pūtam na kiṃcid vā tat kim duṣyet atas eva grantha kṛtā eva anyatra uktam evam ātmani asat kalpāḥ prakāśasya eva santi amī jaḍāḥ prakāśaḥ eva asti sva ātmanaḥ sva para ātmabhiḥ iti tat yadi prakāśaḥ tadā bhavati arthaḥ prakāśaḥ ca asau katham yadi prakāśa tā eva ghaṭasya vapuḥ sā eva paṭasya ityādi viśva vapuḥ prakāśaḥ siddhaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.4–5^1	 ekasya eva prakāśasya evaṃbhūta krama ākrama kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādi vicitra vaiśvarūpya pradarśana sāmarthya rūpam aiśvaryam iti etāvat paryavasāyayitavyam tat ca evam paryavasyati yadi prakāśasya vicitra bhāve hetu antaram apākṛtam tatra prakāśasya avicitrasya krameṇa vicitra tā kāraṇam pratibimba ātmakam tad pratibimba sajātīyam yat tat eva nīla ādi rūpam bāhyam tat ca yadi api anumeyam tathā api idam nīlam iti pratyakṣeṇa adhyavasāyāt adhyavasāya prāṇita tvāt ca pramāṇa sthiteḥ pratyakṣa vyapadeśyam bhaviṣyati bāhya artha vāda ukathitam iti hetu antaram anumīyamāna bāhya rūpam āśaṅkyamāna tvena darśayati tad tad ākasmika ābhāsaḥ bāhyam ced anumāpayet na hi abhinnasya bodhasya vicitra ābhāsa hetu tāḥ na vāsanā prabodhaḥ atra vicitraḥ hetu tām iyāt tasya api tad prabodhasya vaicitrye kim nibandhanam
