ĪPrVV_1,5.4–5^2	 iha bodhaḥ tāvat abhinnaḥ prakāśa mātram eva hi asya parama arthaḥ prakāśa adhikam yadi nīlasya rūpam tarhi tat aprakāśa rūpam iti na prakāśeta atha tathā prakāśa tvam eva asya rūpam pīta prakāśaḥ katham syāt atha api kramika nīla pīta ādi prakāśa rūpam eva tasya sva rūpam nīla ādi ābhāsa śūnyaḥ aham iti prakāśaḥ svāpa ādi avasthāsu na syāt tasmāt prakāśaḥ prakāśaḥ eva aṇu mātram api na rūpa antaram asya asti iti abhinnaḥ bodhaḥ tasya ca abhinnasya kadācid nīla ābhāsa tā kadācid pīta ābhāsa tā iti ye vicitra ābhāsāḥ tatra kāraṇa tvam hi yasymāt naḥ upapannam hetau abhinne kārya bhedasya asaṃbhavāt tasmāt sa sa vicitra nīla pīta ādi rūpaḥ ākāsmikaḥ ajñāta pratyakṣa siddha hetukaḥ san bāhyam vijñāna gata pratibimba ātmaka sva svabhāva saṃpādakam aucityāt nija rūpa sadṛśam krama upanipatat rūpa bahutara bheda ātmakam jñānāt sarvathā pṛthak bhūtam anumāpayati iti saṃbhāvayate bāhya artha vādī 
ĪPrVV_1,5.6^1	 na ca asya idam saṃbhāvanā mātram api tu niścaya paryavasāyi eva bhavati tathā hi vijñāna vādinā yaḥ hetuḥ vaicitrye vāsanā prabodha lakṣaṇaḥ uktaḥ sa naḥ upapadyate smṛti janakaḥ saṃskāraḥ vāsanāḥ iti tāvat prasiddham iha tu anubhava vaicitrya hetuḥ paryeṣaṇīyaḥ vartate astu vā nīla ādi ābhāsa saṃpādana sāmarthya rūpā jñānasya yogyatā ātmikā śaktiḥ vāsanā tasyāḥ ca sva kārya saṃpādana unmukhyam prabodhaḥ tatas bodheṣu ābhāsa vaicitryam iti tatra api tu brūmaḥ iha yadya api ābhāsānām jñāna antarvartinām apāramārthika tvam saṃvṛti sattvam ucyeta api tathā api yat eṣām tat vastu sadeva aṅgīkāryam avastunaḥ sarva sāmarthya virahita alakṣaṇasya kārya saṃpādana prāṇita sāmārtthya ātmaka svabhāva anupapatteḥ evaṃsthite yāḥ etāḥ vāsanāḥ ābhāsa kāraṇa tvena iṣyante tāsām bodhāt yadi bhinnam rūpam tat ca parama artha sat tat ayam śabda antara pracchannaḥ bāhya arthavāda prakāraḥ eva 
ĪPrVV_1,5.6^2	 atha saṃvṛtisat tarhi tena rūpeṇa kāraṇa tā anupapattiḥ tathā yena rūpeṇa āsām pāramārthika tā tena kāraṇa tā tat tarhi jñāna mātram tat ca abhinnam iti nīla ādi ābhāsa rūpasya kārya bhedasya asiddhiḥ evam vāsanānām abicitra tve tad prabodhaḥ vicitraḥ iti kā pratyāśā bhavantu vā vāsanāḥ bhinnāḥ tathā api bodha mātra atiriktasya deśa kāla bhāva ādeḥ prabodhaka abhimatasya vicitrasya kāraṇasya abhāvāt prabodhaḥ avicitraḥ iti ekaḥ eva prabodhaḥ iti samam eva nīla ādi vaicitryam bhāseta atha sva saṃtāna vartīni jñāna antarāṇi vicitrāṇi prabodha kāraṇāni iti tat asat sukha duḥkha nīka pīla ādi pūrva apara ādi deśa kāla bhedasya vijñāna mātra rūpa tve vijñānasya ca prakāśa mātra pramā artha tāyām svarūpa bheda asaṃbhave tathā bodha vailakṣaṇya anupapatteḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.6^3	 para pramātṛ rūpeṣu bodha antariṣu saṃtāna antara śabda vācyeṣu api tulyaḥ ayam availakṣaṇya prakāraḥ tatra api parakīya abhimatasya kṛśa sthūla ādeḥ kāyasya śvāsa praśvāsa ādeḥ prāṇasya sukha duḥkha ādeḥ dhī guṇasya anumātṛ abhimata saṃbinmātra rūpa abhede paratvam kasya bhavet iti na vidmaḥ bodhasya tad niṣṭhasya iti ced saḥ api pramāṇena yadi na siddhaḥ tat asat eva siddhaḥ api prameya tayā ced tat jaḍaḥ eva tathā api ca kāya ādi vat eva jñāna mātra svabhāvaḥ sva saṃvid mātra rūpa tve param prati asya asiddheḥ nanu vyāhāra ādi kriyā sva ātmani icchayā vyāhareyam iti evaṃrūpayā hetu bhāvena vyāptā dṛṣṭā tat caitra kāye api tayā tad hetukayā bhāvyam na ca mad saṃtati patitā samīhāḥ asti iti sva saṃvedanena niścitam tatas ca para samīhā siddhyati tat eva saṃtāna antaram iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.6^4	 atra ucyate iha anumātuḥ vyāhāra ābhāsaḥ dvidhā bhavati vyāpti grahaṇa kāle aviccheda prāṇaḥ aham vyāharāmi iti evaṃrūpaḥ anumāna avasare ca vyāharati ayam iti viccheda jīvitaḥ iti anyasya vyāptiḥ gṛhītāḥ anyaḥ ca ābhāsaḥ katham idānīm hetuḥ syāt vyāharati iti ābhāsasya hetuḥ aviditaḥ eva iti katham tatas hetoḥ samīhāḥ anumīyeta kim ca vyāharati ayam iti yaḥ pramātṛ antare anumātṛ saṃmate vicchinna tayā avabhāsaḥ saḥ anumeya saṃmatāyāḥ paramīhāyāḥ katham kāryaḥ syāt tasyāḥ hi vyāharāmi iti ābhāsaḥ kāryaḥ yaḥ asau aviccheda jīvitaḥ na ca aviccheda mayasya viccheda mayaḥ kāryam iti yuktam tathābhūta kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇa upāya abhāvāt na hi sva ātmani yaḥ ayam avicchinna ābhāsaḥ sa paratra vicchinnam vyāharati iti evaṃrūpam ābhāsam janayati iti kenacid pramāṇena siddham para siddhi pūrvaka tvāt asya arthasya para pramātṛ siddhaḥ ca evaṃbhūta artha adhīna tvena itaretara āśrayāt 
ĪPrVV_1,5.6^5	 na ca avaśyan avicchinnāt vicchinnena bhāvyam iti niyamaḥ asti vyavhicārāt na ca vicchinnaḥ api ābhāsaḥ upadyatām iti tad anusaṃdhānāt tad utpattiḥ niyatā tad sadbhāve api asya anutpatteḥ tad abhāve ca utpatteḥ vicchinnaḥ ābhāsaḥ paratra utpadyatām iti yā samīhā tayā saha pratraḥ utpannasya vicchinna ābhāsasya kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇam eva parāsiddhau na yuktaḥ iti vyāpteḥ eva asiddhiḥ pramātṛ antarāṇi ca yadi bhinnāni tadā tad niṣṭhānām avabhāsānām bhedaḥ eva jñānāt avyatiriktam ca iti nyāyāt tatas ca eka ābhāsa niṣṭhatva abhāvāt eka ābhāsa viśrāntaḥ saṃbhūya pramātḥṇām vyavahāraḥ na syāt iti anyosaṃbhavaḥ yat prameyam bodhāt bhinnam bhavati iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.6^6	 saha upalambha niyama ādeḥ anaikāntika tvāt nīla pīta ādinā api prameya rāśinā kim apakṛtam yena asya sva rūpa viśrāntiḥ na sahyate tasmāt pramātṛ antarāṇām api asiddhiḥ eva siddhau vā sarva pramātṛ antargatāḥ ābhāsā ekaikatra paratra ābhāsa vaicitrya hetum vāsanā udvodha vaicitryam janayeyuḥ niyame hetu antara abhāvāt iti tathā api na nīla ādi vaicitrya siddhiḥ evam vāsanānām tad udbodha hetūnām ca vicitrāṇām anupapattiḥ eva tatas ca sthitam etat abhinnaḥ bodhaḥ tasya ākasmikā ābhāsa bheda hetutva anupapatteḥ bāhyaḥ arthaḥ a numeyaḥ saṃbhāvyate iti yadi bāhya artha vādinā ucyate iti śloka dvaya arthaḥ ced śabdaḥ śloka dvaya vākya artha śaṅkā ādyotakaḥ evam āśaṅkyamāna tvena para saṃbhāvanā dṛḍhā darśitāḥ adhunā tu enām saṃbhāvanām śithilayitum tāvat āha syāt etad avabhāseṣu teṣu eva avasite sati vyavahāre kim anyena bāhyena anupapattinā syāt etat iti pūrva ukta saṃbhāvanā abhyupagame yadā vyākhyāyate tadā kim tu iti vākya śeṣeṇa tad śaithilya viṣayam saṃbhāvanā antaram śeṣa ślokena darśayate iti vyākhyeyam 
ĪPrVV_1,5.6^7	 yadi tu adhyāhāraḥ na sahyate tadā syāt etat iti idam api saṃbhāvanā antaram syāt yat anena ślokena ucyate iti eka vākyatayā yojyam anayā api kaṣṭa kalpanayā bāhyān arthān prasādhayatā bhavatā taiḥ na kiṃcid kartavyam ābhāsaiḥ eva taiḥ bhavatā abhyupagataiḥ vyavahāra siddheḥ na hi nitya anumeyena kaścid vyavahāraḥ iti kim bāhyena yatra sādhakam ca na asti pramāṇam bādhakam ca prakāśāt bhede anumeya tayā api prakāśana abhāvaḥ iti tāvat mukhyam abhyuścaya bādhakaḥ tu avayavinaḥ vṛtti anupapattiḥ samavāya asiddhiḥ kampā kampa āvaraṇān āvaraṇa raktā rakta diś bhāga bheda ādi viruddha dharma yogaḥ aṇu saṃcaya bāhya vāde api saṃcayasya anyasya abhāve paramāṇavaḥ eva te ca yadi saṃyujyante nirantara tayā tat avaśyam diś bhāga bhedaḥ evana akṣe ṣaṭsu dikṣu saṃcīyamāneṣu ṣaṭsu aṇuṣu madhyamasya paramāṇoḥ yatra eva dhāmni ekaḥ lagnaḥ tatra eva yadi aparaḥ tat eka paramāṇu mātra tā 
ĪPrVV_1,5.6^8	 atha anyatra ekaḥ anyatar aparaḥ tat avaśyam bhāga bheda āpattiḥ iti bhāgaḥ eva san tasya api eṣā eva saraṇiḥ iti na kiṃcid avaśiṣyate bāhyam tattvataḥ na ca etat vācyam mūrtānām eka deśa tva ayogāt saṃyoge bhinna deśa tva avyāvṛtteḥ tat niṣṭam dvi aṇukam nāma kārya dravyam aṇu parimāṇam tebhyaḥ tribhyaḥ mahat kāryam iti avayavī vādaḥ hi ayam sa ca pūrvam eva apabādhitaḥ yat ca avyāpya vṛtti tvam saṃyogasya ucyate tad niraṃśe katham saṃgacchatām sva āśraye hi yadi asau samavaiti kim anyāt asya avaśiṣyate yat na vyāpnuyāt iti abhyuścaya bādhakam ca idam iti na atra asmābhiḥ bharaḥ kṛtaḥ vistareṇa ca prajñā alaṅkāre darśitam ācārya śaṅkara nandanena 
ĪPrVV_1,5.7^1	 nanu bādhakam nāma pramāṇa siddhe vastuni na kiṃcid kartum samartham tena eva dṛḍhena pramāṇena bādhaka abhimatasya bādhitasya apramāṇa tva saṃpādanāt darśitam ca iha sādhakam pramāṇam kārya hetuḥ tad tad ākasmika ābhāsaḥ iti kārikayā iti āśaṅkyaḥ āha cit ātmā eva hi devaḥ antar sthitam icchā vaśāt bahis yogī iva nirupādānam artha jātam prakāśayet iha tāvat svapna smaraṇa manaḥ rājya saṃkalpa ādiṣu nīla ādi ābhāsa vaicitryam bāhya samarpa kahtu vyatirekeṇa eva nirbhāsate iti yadi api asti saṃbhavaḥ tathā api tad ābhāsa vaicitryam asthaiḥ yāt sarva pramātra sādha araṇyāt pūrva anubhava saṃskāra jatu asaṃbhāvanāt avastu iti śaṅkyeta yat punar idam yoginām icchā mātreṇa purasena ādi vaicitrya nirmāṇam dṛṣṭam tatra upādānam prasiddha mṛd kāṣṭha śukra śoṇita ādi vaicitrya mayam na saṃbhavati eva na hi evam vaktum śakyam sarva gatāḥ paramāṇavaḥ yogi icchayā jhaṭiti saṃghaṭitāḥ kāryam ārapsyante iti yat etat loka prasiddha kāraṇa bhāva anatikrama siddhaye nirūpyate 
ĪPrVV_1,5.7^2	 na ca etat prasiddham pramāṇubhyaḥ eva sthūlam ghaṭa ādi jāyate iti kim tu kapāla ādi vyavadhānena tathā api niyata sahakāri samavalambanam kara caraṇa ādi vyāpāre viśiṣṭa deśa kāla dharma ādhipati ayogaḥ śikṣā abhyāsa prakarṣaḥ iti iyati ca āṃśrīyamāṇe yogī kumbham nirmimāṇaḥ kumbhakāra prasiddha sanasta sāmagrī sanarjana puraḥsaraṃghaṭam ghaṭayan kumbhakāraḥ eva syāt tasmāt prasiddha kāraṇa ullaṅghane kim asaṃcetyamāna paramāṇu ādi upādāna kāraṇa antara cintayā iti tatra yogi saṃvidaḥ eva sā tādṛśī śaktiḥ yat ābhāsa vaicitrya rūpam artha jātam prakāśayati iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.7^3	 tat asti saṃbhavaḥ yat saṃvid eva abhyupagata svātantryāḥ apratīdhāta lakṣaṇāt icchā viśeṣa vaśāt saṃvidaḥ anidhika ātma tāyāḥ anapāyāt antar sthitam eva sat bhāva jātam idam iti evam prāṇa buddhi deha ādeḥ vitīrṇa kiyat mātra saṃvidūpāt svātantryam kim na abhyupagamyate sva saṃvedana siddham kim iti hetu antara paryeṣaṇa aprayāsena khidyate eva kāreṇa idam āha sarveṇa tāvat vādinā viṣaya vyavasthāpanam saṃvid rūpam anapahnavanīyam ādi siddham hi tat iti uktam tasya ca svātantryam eva deva śabda nirdiṣṭam cit rūpa tvam iti kim apara kāraṇa anveṣaṇa vyasani tayā hi yasmāt evam prakāśayati devaḥ iti saṃbhāvyate tasmāt kim bāhyena anupapattinā iti pūrveṇa saṃbandhaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.8^1	 nanu evam ubhayathā api saṃbhāvanā anumānam unmiṣati tatra kim makura pratibimbita ghaṭa ādi dṛṣṭāntena jñāna pratibimba tā ābhāsa vaicitrye vijñāna darpaṇa atiriktam tatas eva bāhya abhimatam hetum kalpayema kim vā yogi dṛṣṭāntena saṃvid svātantryam eva hetu bhāvena brūyāma tat idam sāṃśayikam vartate iti āśaṅkya bāhya artha anumāna saṃbhāvanām sūtra dvayena apākartum āha anumāna manābhāta pūrve na eva iṣṭam indriyam ābhātam eva bīja ādeḥ ābhāsāt hetu vastunaḥ na kevalam anantara śloka nirdiṣṭābhiḥ yuktabhiḥ pratyakṣeṇa bāhyaḥ arthaḥ na bhāsate iyat eva hi pratyakṣam tat ca nīlam bhāti iti sva prakāśa saṃvid rūpam na adhikam kiṃcid iti yāvat anumānena api na asya bāhya asya siddhiḥ iti api śabdasya abhiprāyaḥ tatra anumānam atra na eva pravartitum utsahate pravṛttam api na prakṛta siddhim ādavyāt iti anena sūtra dvayena upadarśyate tatra anumānam vikalpaḥ sarvaḥ ca ayam vikalpaḥ anubhava mūlaḥ iti prasiddham tena yat sarvathā anābhāta pūrvam ananubhūta caram tatra anumānam anumiti vyāpāraḥ vikalpa ātmā na eva kenacid vādinā iṣyate 
ĪPrVV_1,5.8^2	 nanu bhavatu pratyakṣatas dṛṣṭe anumāne saṃkathā iyam sāmānyatas dṛṣṭe tu kim vakṣyasi yathā artha upalabdhyā indriya anumāne ucyate tatra api vikalpena yathā saḥ arthaḥ spṛśyate tathā anumeyaḥ iti sthitiḥ vikalpaḥ ca naḥ indriya ādikam artham kenacid saṃniveśa viśeṣa ādinā viśeṣa ātmanā spṛśati api tu kiṃcid upalabdheḥ kāraṇam iti amunā svabhāvena sa ca svabhāvaḥ kāraṇa tā lakṣaṇaḥ pratyakṣa gṛhītaḥ eva tathā ca bījāt aṅkuraḥ tantubhyaḥ paṭaḥ ityādau kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pratyakṣa anupalambha balena tāvat niśceyaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.8^3	 tatra ca pratyakṣam pratyābhāsam prāmāṇyam bhajate vimarśa lakṣaṇasya pramiti vyāpārasya ekaika śabda vācye arthe pravṛtteḥ tad anusāri tvāt ca pramāṇasya iti vakṣyate eka abhidhāna viṣaye mitiḥ vastuni abādhitāḥ iti ābhāsa mātram ca sāmānyam iti niḥ eṣuate anupalambhaḥ api anya upalambha rūpaḥ ābhāsa mātra viśrāntaḥ eva iti kāraṇa ābhāsaḥ viśeṣa śūnyaḥ parigṛhītaḥ eva bījāt aṅkuraḥ iti pratītau yat yasya niyamam anuvidhatte avyatiriktam tat tasya kāryam iti pratighaṭam mṛttikā ādi rūpa hetu tadvat mātrasya āmāsāt 
ĪPrVV_1,5.9^1	 ābhāsaḥ punar ābhāsat bāhyasya āsīt kathaṃcana arthasya na eva tena asya siddhiḥ na api anumānataḥ ābhāsāt bāhyaḥ punar nābhāsa rūpaḥ sa ca ābhāsate iti vipratiṣiddham anābhāse ca na asti vikalpa rūpasya anumānasya vyāpāraḥ grāma gṛha ādeḥ tu yat bāhyam tat agrāma ādi rūpam naḥ ucyate pratyekam vāṭānūpa kuṇya tula ādeḥ bāhya tva prasaṅgāt api tu tad saṃnikaṭam tasmāt grāma bāhyam ābhāsa bāhyam iti ca śabda sāmya mātram etat na vastu sāmyam evam ye vikalpe vastu naḥ ābhāti iti manyante teṣām api tāvat anumāna vikalpaḥ na bāhye upapannaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.9^2	 asmābhiḥ tu upapāditam adhyavasāyasya api ābhāsamāna viṣaya tvam bhrānti tve ca avasāyasya iti sūtre tena anumāna vikalpa ātmanā api prakāśena yadi anāviṣṭaḥ nīla ādiḥ arthaḥ tat na anumitaḥ eva syāt atha āviṣṭaḥ eva tarhi prāk iva arthaḥ aprakāśaḥ syāt iti nyāyena prakāśa mātra svabhāvaḥ eva na bāhyaḥ tena bāhye sādhye yat kiṃcid pramāṇam ānīyate tad abāhya tām eva pratyuta sādhayati iti viruddham eva atas eva āha kathaṃcanaḥ iti kena api prakāreṇa pratyakṣa ātmanā anumeya ātmanā vā ābhāsanam ābhāsaḥ bāhyasya anābhāsasya na kadācid abhūt iti tasmāt siddham cit ātmā eva hi devaḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.10^1	 nanu antar sthitam bahis prakāśayet iti uktam tat antar sthita tvam upapādanīyam iti āśaṅkyaḥ āha svāminaḥ ca ātma saṃsthasya bhāva jātasya bhāsanam asti eva na vinā tasmāt icchā āmarśaḥ pravartate bahīrūpatayā ābhāsane api ahantā rūpa tā na truṭyati pramātra aikātmyam āntaryam iti hi vakṣyate tat ca sadā eva prakāśasya pramātṛ tvāt tad ātma tayā ca vinā aprakāśamānasya avastu tvāt kim tu tatra aham iti ucite parāmarśe yaḥ ayam idantā parāmarśaḥ sā eva bāhya tā tat ca iha antar sthita tvam aham iti etāvatā cit samucitena eva bapuṣā parāmarśanam eva tat ca iha nīla ādīnām asti eva na tu na asti iti yadi hi na syāt kumbha kṛtaḥ ghaṭam karavāṇi iti yaḥ uttara kriyām apekṣya icchā śabda vācyaḥ parāmarśaḥ eṣaṇīyena sa parāmṛśyena aniyantritaḥ ced tatas paṭa icchā api sā na kasmāt iti saṃkīryeran vyavahārāḥ atha tatra api ca eṣaṇīyaḥ tadānīm eva nirmitaḥ san tathā jātaḥ tarhi tat nirmāṇam cit ātmani vinā icchayā na upapannam iti tiṣṭhāsoḥ evam icchā eva hetu tā iti atra varṇayiṣyate 
ĪPrVV_1,5.10^2	 tat ca icchā antaram api viṣaya niyantritam na vā iti vikalpe anavasthā viṣaya niyantritam ced syāt ātma tā eva jātāḥ na ced ghaṭe paṭa icchā syāt atha tatra api tadānīm eva iti kṛtvā anavasthā tasmāt sarvaḥ ayam bhāva rāśiḥ cit ātmani aham iti eva vapuṣā satata avabhāsura vapuḥ aiśvarya rūpāt ca svātantrya lakṣaṇāt svāmi bhāvāt vicitreṇa vapuṣā krama ākrama ādinā saṃvid enam bahis karoti pramātṛ prathana pūrvakam tatra api kvacid ābhāse pramātḥn ekīkaroti nitamba nī nṛttaḥ iva prekṣakān tāvati hi teṣām ābhāse aikyam 
ĪPrVV_1,5.10^3	 śarīra prāṇa buddhi sukha ādi ābhāsa aṃśeṣu tu bhedasya avigalanāt na sarvathā aikyam atas eva pratikṣaṇam pramātṛ saṃyojana viyojana vaicitryeṇa parameśvaraḥ viśvam sṛṣṭi saṃhāra ādinā prapañcayati tad uktam ācāryeṇa sadā sṛṣṭi vinodāya sadā sthiti sukha asine sadā tribhuvana āhāra tṛptāya bhavate namaḥ ityādi śrī bhaṭṭa nārāyaṇena apimuhur muhur aviśrāntaḥ trailokyam kalpanā śataiḥ kalpayan= api kaḥ api ekaḥ nirvikalpaḥ jayati ajaḥ iti tasmāt sthitam antar sthitam bhāva jātam tena vinā tad viṣayasya parāmarśa ayogāt iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.11^1	 nanu parāmarśaḥ nāma vikalpaḥ sa ca avikalpa śuddha saṃvid vapuṣi bhagavati katham syāt iti āśaṅkya āha svabhāvam avabhāsasya vimarśam viduḥ anyathā prakāśaḥ artha uparaktaḥ api sphaṭika ādi jaḍa upamaḥ iha avabhāvasya prakāśasya anavabhāsasya ca aprakāśasya ghaṭa ādeḥ paraspara parihāreṇa dvayoḥ sva ātmani ced vyavasthānam tat ghaṭa paṭayoḥ iva idam jaḍam idam jaḍam iti durupapādam vailakṣaṇyam atha avabhāsaḥ yatas arthasya saṃbamdhī tatas na jaḍaḥ tarhi saṃbandha mātreṇa mṛd api ghaṭasya iti ajaḍā syāt atha na sva saṃbandha mātram api tu avabhāsaḥ arthasya prakāśaḥ tarhi artha ātmanā sa prakāśaḥ iti samāpatitam na ca anya ātmanā anyasya prakāśaḥ upapannaḥ atha anya svabhāvaḥ api ghaṭaḥ avabhāsasya kāraṇam tarhi avabhāsaḥ api ghaṭasya kāraṇam iti ghaṭaḥ api ajaḍaḥ syāt atha anyena satā api ghaṭena yatas avabhāsasya pratibimba rūpā cchāyā dattā tām asau adabhāsaḥ bibhrat ghaṭasya iti ucyate tatas ca ajaḍaḥ tarhi sphaṭika salilam akurādiḥ api evaṃbhūtaḥ eva iti ajaḍaḥ eva syāt 
ĪPrVV_1,5.11^2	 atha tathābhūtam api ātmānam tam ca ghaṭa ādikam sphaṭika ādiḥ na parāmraṣṭum samarthaḥ iti jat aḥ tathā aparāmarśanam eva ajāḍya jīvitam antar bahiṣkaraṇa svātantrya rūpam svābhāvikam avabhāsasya sva ātma viśrānti lakṣaṇam ananya mukha prekṣi tvam nāma aham evam prakāśa ātmā prakāśe iti hi vimarśa udaye sva saṃvid eva pramātṛ prameya pramāṇa ādi kṛtārtham abhimanyate na tu atiriktam kāṅkṣati sphaṭika ādi hi gṛhīta pratibimbam api tathā abhāvena siddhau pramātṛ antaram apekṣate iti nirvimarśa tvāt jaḍam sarvatra vastutas vimarśa ātmaka pramātṛ svabhāva tādātmya ahaṃpara āmarśa viśrānteḥ ajaḍa tvam eva pūrva apara koṭyoḥ yat uktam idam iti asya vicchinna vimarśasya kṛtārtha tā yā sva svarūpe viśrāntiḥ vimarśaḥ saḥ aham iti ayam iti madhya avasthā eva tu idantā vimṛśyamāna ūrvā para koṭiḥ vimūḍhānām māyā padam saṃsāraḥ iti vimarśaḥ eva pradhānam bhagavataḥ iti sthitam 
ĪPrVV_1,5.12^1	 na kevalam saṃvid tattvasya asmābhiḥ eva vimarśa prādhānyam uktam yāvat āgama antaraiḥ api iti darśayati ātmātaḥ eva caitanyam cit kriyā citikartṛ tā tātparyeṇa uditaḥ tena jaḍāt sa hi vilakṣaṇaḥ yatas vimarśaḥ eva pradhānam ātmanaḥ rūpam amum eva hetum prayojana rūpam uddiśya ātmā dharmi svabhāvaḥ dravya bhūtaḥ api caitantyam iti dharma vācinā śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyam āśritya uditaḥ kathitaḥ bhagavatā śiva sūtra iṣu caitanyam ātmā iti paṭhitam caitanyam iti hi dharma vācakopa lakṣaṇam citi śaktiḥ apariṇāminī tad dṛśeḥ kaivalyam draṣṭā dṛśi mātraḥ ityādau api hi dharma śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyam ātmanaḥ darśitam guruṇā anantena dravyam hi tat ucyate yat viśrāntaḥ padārtha vargaḥ sarvaḥ bhāti ca arthyate ca artha kriyāyai tat yadi na tat sakalaḥ ayam tattva bhūta bhāva bhuvana saṃbhāraḥ saṃvidi viśrāntaḥ tathā bhavati iti saḥ eva guṇa karma ādi dharma āśraya bhūta padārtha antara svabhāvaḥ tām eva mukhya dravya svarūpam āśrayate iti sā eva dravyam 
ĪPrVV_1,5.12^2	 tat ananta dharma rāśi viśrama bhitti bhūtāyāḥ tasyāḥ saḥ eva dharmaḥ caitanyam iti kartṛ kṛt antāt utpannena bhāva pratyayena saṃbandha abhidhāyinā api prādhānyena darśitaḥ tathā hi saṃbandha viśrāntasya pratīteḥ dravyta rūpasya ca saṃbandhinaḥ prakṛtyā ukta tvāt citi kriyā rūpam dhramam saṃbaddham avagamayatā ṣyañā niṣkṛṣṭa aṃśaḥ pratyāyitaḥ bhavati citi kriyā ca cittau kartṛ tā svātaṃtryam saṃyojana viyojana anusaṃdhāna ādi rūpam ātma mātra tāyām eva jaḍa vat aviśrānta tvam aparicchinna prakāśa sāra tvam ananya mukha prekṣi tvam iti tat eva anātma rūpāt jaḍāt saṃyojana viyojana ādi svātaṃtri avikalāt vailakṣaṇya ādāyi iti tat evam paratvena pradhāna tayā abhisaṃdhāya ātmā cetanaḥ iti vaktavye dharma antara adharīkaraṇāya vimarśa dharma uddhurīkaraṇāya ca ātmā caitanyam iti uktam cit kriyā citi kartṛ tātāt paryeṇaḥ iti samāsaḥ ardha yuj pāda viśrāntiḥ iti hi kāvye samayaḥ na śāstre yadi vā cit kriyā ātmā ucitaḥ citikartṛ tā ca iti pṛthak eva evam tu na kvacid paṭhitam 
ĪPrVV_1,5.13^1	 nanu yathā prakāśaḥ aprakāśaḥ ca iti ybhayam api sva ātmani tatas ca prakāśaḥ iti ukte jaḍāt na vailakṣaṇyam uditam syāt tadvat vimarśaḥ api avimarśaḥ api ca sva ātmani iti tena api katham vailakṣaṇyam jaḍa ajaḍayoḥ iti āśaṅkya āha citiḥ pratyavamarśa ātmā parā vāc svarasa uditā svātantryam etat mukhyam tat aiśvaryam paramātmanaḥ cetayati iti atra yā citiḥ citi kriyā tasyāḥ pratyavamarśaḥ sva ātma camatkāra lakṣaṇaḥ ātmā svabhāvaḥ tathā hi ghaṭena sva ātmani na camatkriyate sva ātmā na parāmṛśyate na sva ātmani tena prakāśyate na aparicchinna tayā bhāsyate tatas ca ca iti atas iti ucyate caitreṇa tu sva ātmani aham iti saṃrambha udyoya ullāsa vibhūti yogāt camatkriyate sva ātmā parāmṛśyate sva ātmani eva prakāśyate idam iti yaḥ paricchedaḥ etāvat rūpa tayā tad vilakṣaṇī bhāvena nīla pīta sukha duḥkha tad śūnyatā ādi asaṃkhyā avabhāsa yogena avabhāsyate tatas caitreṇa cetyate iti ucyate evam ca vimarśaḥ sva ātmani avimarśaḥ api sva ātmani iti asiddam etat 
ĪPrVV_1,5.13^2	 vimarśaḥ hi sarvaṃsahaḥ param api ātmīkaroti ātmānam ca parīkaroti ubhayam ekīkaroti ekīkṛtam dvayam api nyagbhāvayati iti evaṃsvabhāvaḥ pratyavamarśāḥ ca āntara abhilāpa ātmaka śabdana svabhāvaḥ tat ca śabdanam saṅketa nirapekṣam eva avicchinna camatkāra ātmakam antar mukha śiraḥ nirdeśa prakhyam akāra ādi māyīyasa aṅketika śabda jīvita bhūta nīlam idaṃcaitraḥ aham ityādi pratyavamarśa antara bhitti bhūta tvāt pūrṇa tvāt parā vakti viśvam abhilapati pratyavamarśena iti ca vāc atas eva sā svarasena cit rūpa tayā sva ātma viśrānti vapuṣā uditā sadāna stamitāḥ nityāḥ aham iti eva 
ĪPrVV_1,5.13^3	 etat eva paramātmanaḥ mukhyam svātantryam aiśvaryam īśitṛ tvam ananya apekṣi tvam ucyate parāparam tu idaṃbhāva rūpasya pratyavamarśasya akhyāti prāṇasya udbodha mātre api ahaṃbhāvaḥ eva viśrānteḥ śrī sadāśiva ādi bhūmau paśyantī daśāyām aparam tu idaṃbhāvasya eva nirūḍhau māyā garbha adhikṛtānām eva viṣṇu viriñca indra ādīnām tat tu teṣām parameśvara prasāda jam eva iti anya nirapekṣa tā eva paramārthataḥ ānandaḥ aiśvaryam svātanryam caitanyam tasmāt yuktam uktam tena jaḍāt sa hi vilakṣaṇaḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.14^1	 pradhāna āgameṣu api etat pradarśitam eva iti nirūpayati sā sphurat tā mahāsattā deśa kāla āviśeṣinī sā eṣā sāratayā proktāḥ hṛdayam parameṣṭhinaḥ iha ghaṭaḥ kasmāt asti sva puṣpam kasmāt na asti iti uktaḥ iti vaktāraḥ bhavanti ghaṭaḥ hi sphurati mama na tu itarat iti tat etat ghaṭa tvam eva yadi sphurat tvam sphuraṇa saṃbandhaḥ tat sarvadā sarvasya sphuret na kasyacid vā tasmāt mama sphurati iti kaḥ arthaḥ madīyam sphuraṇam spandanam ādiṣṭam iti spandanañca kiñcid calanam eṣā eva ca kiñcid rūpa tā yat acalam api calam ābhāsate iti prakāśa svarūpam hi manāk api na atiricyate atiricyate iva iti tat acalam eva ābhāsa bheda yuktam iva ca bhāti tatas uktam ātmā eva sarva bhāveṣu sphurat nirvṛta cit vapuḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.14^2	 aniruddha icchā prasaraḥ prasarat dṛkkriyaḥ śivaḥ iti yathā ati kruddhaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ vā kim karomi iti vā mṛśan dhāvan vā yat padam gacchet tatra spandaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ iti spanda tattva viviktaye iti guṇa ādi spanda niḥṣyandāḥ iti ca loke api vividha vaicitrya yogena spandavat tvam sattā ca bhavana kartṛ tā sarva kriyāṣu svātantryam sā ca sva puṣpa ādikam api vyāpnoti iti mahatī deśa kālau nīla ādi vat sā eva sṛjati iti tābhyām viśeṣaṇīyāḥ na bhavati yat kila yena tulya kakṣya tayā bhāti tat tasya viśeṣaṇam kaṭakaḥ iva caitrasya na ca deśa kālau vimarśena tulya kakṣyau bhātaḥ tayoḥ idantayā tasya ca ahantayā prakāśe tulya kakṣya tva anupapatteḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.14^3	 evam deśa kāla asparśāt vibhu tvam nitya tvam ca sakala deśa kāla sparśaḥ a pi tad nirmāṇa yogāt iti tatas api vyāpaka tva nitya tve tat uktam mahāsattā mahādevī viśva jīvanam ucyate iti sāram iti yat atuccham rūpam tat iyam eva vimarśa śaktiḥ grāhya grāhakāṇām yat prakāśa ātmakam rūpam tasya api aprakāśa vailakṣaṇya ākṣepikā iyam eva iti śrī sāraśāstre api nirūpitam yat sāram asya jagataḥ sā śaktiḥ mālinī parā iti sā eṣā iti śakti pratyabhijñānam darśitam hṛdayam ca nāma pratiṣṭhā sthānam ucyate tat ca ukta nītyā jaḍānām cetanam tasya api prakāśāt prakatvam tasya api vimarśa śaktiḥ iti viśvasya parame pade tiṣṭhataḥ viśrāntasya tasya idam eva hṛdayam vimarśa rūpam para mantra ātmakam yatra tatra abhidhīyate 
ĪPrVV_1,5.14^4	 sarvasya hi mantraḥ eva hṛdayam mantraḥ ca vimarśana ātmā vimarśanam ca parāvāc śakti mayam tatas eva uktam na taiḥ vinā bhavet śabdaḥ na arthaḥ na api citeḥ gatiḥ iti tatra tāvat samāpannā mātṛ bhāvam ityādi ca iti āgameṣu tatrabhavat bhartṛ hariṇā api na saḥ asti pratyayaḥ loke yaḥ śabda anugamāt ṛte anuviddham iva jñānam sarvam śabdena gamyate vāc rūpa tā ced utkrāmet avabodhasya śāśvatī na prakāśaḥ prakāśeta sā hi pratyavamarśinī iti sā eṣā saṃsāriṇām saṃjñā bahis antar ca vartate yat utkrāntau visaṃjñaḥ ayam dṛśyate kāṣṭha kuṅya vat ityādi ca tat etena viduḥ iti etat nirvāhitam bauddhaiḥ api adhyavasāya apekṣam prakāśasya prāmāṇyam vadadbhiḥ upagata prāyaḥ eva ayam arthaḥ abhilāpa ātmaka tvāt adhyavasāyasya iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.15–16^1	 nanu asaṃkhya śakti śreṇa uśobhita vapuṣi parama śive vimarśa śaktiḥ eva iyam itthaṃkāram abhiṣicyate kasmāt iti āśaṅkya āha ātmānam atas eva ayam jñeyīkuryāt pṛthak sthiti jñeyam na tu tad aunmukhyāt khaṇḍī eta asya svatantra tā svātantrya amukta ātmānam svātantryāt advaya ātmanaḥ prabhuḥ īśa ādi saṃkalpaiḥ nirmāya vyavahārayet sarvāḥ śaktoḥ kartṛ tva śaktiḥ aiśvarya ātmā samākṣipati sā ca vimarśa rūpāḥ iti yuktam asyāḥ eva prādhānyam iti tātparyeṇa uttaram uktam śabda arthasya ayam prakāśa ātmā parameśvaraḥ sva ātmānam jñātṛ eka rūpa tvāt ajñeyam api jñeyīkaroti iti yat saṃbhāvyate kāraṇa antarasya anupapatteḥ darśita tvāt dṛḍhena saṃbhāvanā anumānena tat atas eva vimarśa śakti lakṣaṇāt kartṛ tvāt hetoḥ bhavati yatas hi ayam ātmānam parāmṛśati tatas viśva nirbhara tvāt tathā nīla ādi tvena cakāsti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.15–16^2	 nanu eṣā eva kutas saṃbhāvanā ātmānam jñeyīkaroti iti āha pṛthak prakāśāt bahis bhūtā sthitiḥ yasya tādṛś jñeyam na eva bhavati tuḥ avadhāreṇa tatra ca uktāḥ yuktayaḥ abhyuccaya yuktim api āha yadi vyatiriktam jñeyam syāt tat jñātṛ rūpasya ātmanaḥ yat etat jñeya viṣayam aunmukhyam sva saṃvedana siddham dṛśyate tat na asya syāt tena vyatirikta viṣaya aunmukhyena anya adhīna tvam nāma pāratantryam asya ānīyate pāratantryam ca svātantryasya viruddham svātantryam eva ca ananya mukha prekṣi tvam ātmanaḥ sva rūpam iti vyatirikta unmukhaḥ ātmā anātmā eva syāt anātmā ca jaḍaḥ jñeyam prati naḥ unmukhībhavati iti prasaṅgaḥ tatas prasaṅga viparyayāt idam āyātam avyatirikta unmukhaḥ svatantraḥ san ātmānam eva jñeyīkaroti iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.17^1	 na ca kevalam nīla ādi rūpam eva jñeyam yāvat atyakta kartṛ svabhāvam svātantryeṇa aparityaktam eva santam ātmānam nirmāya vyavahāreṇa dhyāna upāsana arcana upadeśa ādinā yojayati iti yat saṃbhāvyate tat api atas eva iti saṃbandhaḥ nanu svātantrya yuktam ca nirmīyate ca iti viruddham idam atra āha advaya ātmanaḥ saṃvid eka rūpasya svātantryāt hetoḥ idam na na yujyate yat kila māyā pade ati durghaṭam pratibhāti tad saṃpādane yat apratihatam svātantryam tat eva punar svātantrya śabdena darśitam atas eva iti anena tu vimarśa śakti rūpam iti apunaruktam atha vai atas eva svātantryāt iti sāmānādhikaraṇyena śloka dvayena saṃbandhanīyam udāharaṇam atra arthe darśayati nīla ādi nirmāṇa vat asya svatrantra nirmāṇasya aprasiddha tvāt īśvaraḥ bhagavān ātmā nityaḥ vibhuḥ svatantraḥ iti evamādau hi pramātuḥ pūjayituḥ dhyātuḥ vā apṛthak bhūtam tat prameyam pūjyam dhyeyam ca bhāti iti tat tāvat nirmitam na ca anīśvaram 
ĪPrVV_1,5.17^2	 evam hi īśvaraḥ iti anīśvaraḥ iti saṃkalpa dhyāna ādeḥ tulya tvam syāt na ca evam phala bhedasya upalabdheḥ iti tasmāt svātantrya śūnyatā ābhāsanena svātantrya yukta tā ābhāsanena ca yat idam ubhayam jñeyam ātma rūpam eva parameśvaraḥ bhāsayati tat vimarśa śakti balāt eva iti sā eva pradhānam iti nanu prakāśa balāt bhāva vyavasthā sa ca prakāśaḥ vimarśa sāraḥ iti vimarśa abhede tat eva tat iti vaktum yuktam īśvaraḥ ātmā ityādi saṃkalpeṣu ca nirmitasya idantayā parāmarśaḥ svātantryam tu ahaṃparāmarśa rūpam iti nirmitasya tad rūpa tva abhāve katham svātantrya āmukta tvam iti tat etat parihartum āha na āhanta ādi parāmarśa bhedāt asya ānayata ātmanaḥ ahaṃmṛśya tayā aiva asya sṛṣteḥ tiṅvācya karma vat svarūpe bhāva pratyayaḥ ādi grahaṇāt ātma īśvara ādi parāmarśaḥ tiṅgrahaṇam kriyā vāci pratyaya upalakṣaṇam karma grahaṇam asattva bhūta śakti rūpa upalakṣaṇam 
ĪPrVV_1,5.17^3	 tat ayam arthaḥ aham iti evam svarūpaḥ yaḥ parāmarśaḥ yaḥ ca īśvaraḥ pramātā ātmā śivaḥ ityādiḥ ananta prakāraḥ parāmarśaḥ tasya yadi api bhedaḥ anyonya rūpa tā tathā api tad bhedāt hetoḥ asya ātmanaḥ nirmātṛ rūpasya ahaṃparāmarśa mayasya nirmeya rūpasya ca īśvara ādi parāmarśa āspadasya yaḥ bhedaḥ śaṅkitaḥ sa na yuktaḥ yatas īśvaraḥ iti api yaḥ parāmarśaḥ saḥ īśana śīle jñātṛ tva kartṛ tva tattve viśrānyati jñātṛ tva ādi ca jñāna ādau svātantryam ananya mukha prekṣi tvam avicchinna jñāna yogaḥ avicchedaḥ ca jānāmi karomi iti asmad artha viśrāntiḥ iti asya īśvarasya ātmanaḥ sṛṣṭeḥ sṛjyamānasya ahaṃvimarśanīya tvam eva sṛṣṭeḥ iti vā hetau pañcamī asya īśvarasya yatas īśvara ādi saṃkalpeṣu api ahaṃpara āmarśana yogyasya eva sṛṣṭiḥ arhe kṛtyaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.17^4	 yathā kriyā kāraka samuccaya vikalpa ādi śaktayaḥ yathāsvam tiṅtṛtīya ādi cava ādi prayoga avaseya parāmarśa parama arthāḥ pākaḥ kartā samuccayaḥ vikalpaḥ ityādi śabdaiḥ abhidhīyamānāḥ sattva bhāvam āpāditāḥ api pacati caitreṇa ca vā iti evaṃrūpe mūla parāmarśe viśrāmyanti anyathā tu tāḥ pratītāḥ na eva bhaveyuḥ tadvat atra api etat uktam bhavati parāmarśe nāma viśrānti sthānam tat ca pāryantikam eva pāramārthikam tat ca aham iti evaṃrūpam eva madhya viśrānti padam tu yat vṛkṣa mūla sthānīyam grāma gamane tasya tad apekṣayā sṛṣṭa tvam ucyate iti kaḥ virodhaḥ anena nīla ādeḥ api idam nīlam iti madhya parāmarśe api mūla parāmarśe aham iti eva viśrānteḥ ātma maya tvam upapāditam eva nīlam idam vedmi iti api hi aham prakāśe iti iyat tattvam yathā uktam idam iti asya ityādi mūḍhaḥ tu nīla ādi vimarśāt eva artha kriyā ādi paritoṣa abhimānī iti nīla ādeḥ svātantrya nirmukta tvam uktam ātma ādau tu tad mūla parāmarśa viśrāntim antareṇa pratīti parisamāptim artha kriyām ca mūḍhaḥ api na abhimanyate iti tasya nirmitau api anujjhita svātantryam uktam 
ĪPrVV_1,5.18^1	 nanu evam viśva parāmarśanām aham iti eva viśuddha eka parāmarśa viśrāntiḥ eva tattvam tat katham idam ucyate jñāna smṛti ādikāḥ asya śaktayaḥ iti jñānasya ca saṃśaya nirṇaya ādi bhedaḥ nīla ādīnām ca vaicitryam iti āśaṅkāyām parihāram āha māyā śaktyā vibhoḥ sā eva bhinna saṃvedya gocarā kathitā jñāna saṃkalpa adhyavasāya ādi nāmabhiḥ anupapannam avabhāsanam māyā iti ucyate tatas ca bhinnam prakāśāt sarvam avabhāsa jātam māyā tatra ca cit tattvasya eva svātantryam māyā śaktiḥ tayā bhinnam yat saṃvedyam pramātuḥ ca anyonyataḥ ca māyā śaktyā bhinnena pramātuḥ anyonyataḥ vedyāt ca karaṇa vargeṇa yat saṃvedyam saḥ eva gocaraḥ viśrānti padam yasyāḥ tādṛśī satī sā eva pratyavamarśa ātmā citiḥ parāvāc rūpāḥ jñānam iti saṃkalpaḥ iti adhyavasāyaḥ iti ca ucyate ādi grahaṇāt saṃśayaḥ smṛtiḥ ityādi 
ĪPrVV_1,5.18^2	 tathā hi indtriyeṇa sphuṭa grāhiṇā bāhyena viṣayeṇa sphuṭena ca niyantritam saṃvid tattvam tat jñānam manasā viṣayeṇa ca apshuṭena saṃkalpaḥ buddhyā viṣayeṇa ca viṣaya tva paryanta bhājāḥ adhyavasāyaḥ niścayaḥ viṣayasya ca yat bhinna tvam bahis antaḥkaraṇānām ca tad prakāśa abhedāt anupapannam cit tattvena bhāsyate iti bhede yatas viśrāntiḥ na tu bhedasya abhede īśvara sadāśiva ādi vat tatas jñāna saṃkalpa ādayaḥ bhinnāḥ tasya apradhvasta sva svabhāva abhedasya saṃvid tattvasya anusaṃdhātuḥ śaktayaḥ iti uktāḥ saṃśaya ādayaḥ ca bhinnā nīla ādi vaicitryam ca iti sarvam akhaṇḍitam 
ĪPrVV_1,5.19^1	 nanu pratyavamarśa ātma tvam citi śakteḥ saṅkalpa smaraṇa ādi śaktiṣu sacikalpa ātmikāsu bhavatu yā tu nirvikalpa rūpā sākṣātkaraṇa lakṣaṇāḥ anubahu aśaktiḥ tatra katham pratyabamarśaḥ hi abhilāpa viśeṣa yojana āmayaḥ abhilāpa viśeṣa yojanā ca saṅketa smaraṇam apekṣate tat ca saṃskāra prabodham saḥ api tādṛśdṛśam iti evam prathama samaye katham abhilāpa yogaḥ iti parasya vyāmoham apohitum āha sākṣātkārakṣaṇe api asti vimarśaḥ katham anyathā dhāvana ādi upapadyeta pratisaṃdhāna varjitam iha tāvat caitanyasya ātma bhūtaḥ aṅguli nirdeśa ādi prakhyaḥ abhilāpa yogaḥ anyathā bālasya prathamam vyavahāre dṛśyamāne vyutpattiḥ eva na syāt nirvikalpaka jñāna paraṃparayā hi tam śabdam śṛṇoti tatas tam artham puras paśyati punar tat viviktam bhū talam paśyati iti ghaṭam ānaya nayaḥ iti vyavahārāt katham asya ayam arthaḥ iti hṛdi parisphuret idam ghaṭaḥ iti idam ānayaḥ iti idam nayaḥ iti iti yojana aprāṇaḥ hi ayam arthaḥ yojanā ca vikalpa vyāpāraḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,5.19^2	 atra bālā asya prāc janma anubhūta saṅketa smṛteḥ evam tathā api saṅketa kāle sa śabdaḥ viṣaya tvena idaṃbhāvena pratyavamṛśyamāna tvāt bhedāt pracyutya nirbhāsamānaḥ vijñāna śarīre viśrāntaḥ san vācakaḥ iti bhavati tat vijñānasya savarūpam ced bhāti tat abhilāpa mayam eva iti yathā viṣayasya sukha rūpa tva abhāve api jñānam sukha ātmakam bhāti tathā mā bhūt abhilāpa ātmā rūpa ādiḥ viṣayaḥ tathā api vijñānam tad ātmakam avabhāsiṣyate atra tu darśane viṣayasya api vimarśa maya tvāt abhilāpa maya tvam eva vastutas staimitya ādi avasthā api yadi na parāmarśa mayī tarhi asyām vikalpa ātmaka pramātṛ vyāpāra anulāsāt saṃbhavaḥ śapatha parama arthaḥ eva smaraṇam ca na syāt rūpa viṣaya adhyavasāyī hi yadi vikalpaḥ udiyāt kim anyat sarva cintā saṃharaṇena staimityam nāma na syāt iti tatra api asti antar parāmarśaḥ sakalena ca śabda grāmeṇa śabdanam hi sahante vastūni tatra ca niyata śabda yojanam kriyate 
ĪPrVV_1,5.19^3	 tathā hi bālasya puras puṇḍe sahajaḥ yaḥ parāmarśaḥ aham iti avicchedena idam iti vicchedena vā tad pṛṣṭhe eva gauraḥ iti gauḥ iti vā śabdaḥ āropyate saḥ api abhyāsāt pramātṛ mayaḥ bhavati tad pṛṣṭhe ca anyaḥ śuklaḥ iti anyat balīvardaḥ iti iti evam saṅketa tattvam tasmāt asti sākṣātkāre pratyavamarśaḥ api śabdasya ayam āśayaḥ iha sākṣātkāraḥ vastutas paśyāmi iti evaṃbhūta vikalpana vyāpāra paryante eva vikalpaḥ hi pratyakṣasya vyāpāraḥ iti paraḥ api manyate na ca vyapāraḥ tadvataḥ bhinnaḥ yuktaḥ tad svarūpa bhūtaḥ hi saḥ bhavatu vā kṣaṇa mātra svabhāvaḥ sākṣātkāraḥ tatra api asti vimarśaḥ avaśyam ca etat katham anyathā iti yadi sa na syāt tat eka abhisaṃdhānena javāt gacchan tvaritam ca varkṣān paṭhan drutam ca mantra pustakam vācayan na abhimatam eva gacchet uccārayet vācayet vā 
ĪPrVV_1,5.19^4	 tathā hi tasmin deśe jñānam ācikramiṣā ākramaṇam ākrānta tā jñānam prayojana antara anusaṃdhānam tityakṣā deśa antara anusaṃdhiḥ tatra api ācikramiṣā ityādinā yojana viyojana rūpeṇa pratyavamarśena vinā abhimata deśa avāptiḥ katham bhavet evam tvarita udgrahaṇa vācana ādau mantavyam tatra viśe atas sthāna karaṇa ākramaṇa ādi yogaḥ atra ca yatas paścāt bhāvi sthūla vikalpa kalpanā na saṃvedyate tatas eva tvarita tvam iti sūkṣmeṇa pratyavamarśena saṃvartita śabda bhāvanā mayena bhāvyam eva saṃvartitā hi śabda bhāvanā prasāraṇena vivartyamānā sthūlaḥ vikalpaḥ yathā idam iti asya prasāraṇā ghaṭaḥ śkle ityādiḥ tasya api pṛthu budhnā udara ākāraḥ śukla tva jāti yukta guṇa samavāyī ityādiḥ dhāvu gati śuddhau iti pāṭhāt dhāviḥ tvarita gatau sva śakti vaśāt vartate iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.20^1	 bhavatu evam sūkṣmaḥ vimarśaḥ prakāśa śarīra āveśī yatra tu sthūla tvena vikalpa rūpa tā sphuṭāḥ tatra śabdaḥ nīla ādi vat eva pṛthak pratibhāsate nīlam idam iti sa katham prakāśa svarūpāt apṛthak bhūtaḥ syāt śabda ātmā ca vimarśaḥ sa ca atra māyā ātmakam bheda pade api prakāśa apṛthak bhūtaḥ bhavadbhiḥ iṣṭaḥ tat etat katham pratipattavyam iti āśaṅkya āha ghaṭaḥ ayam iti adhyavasā nāma rūpa ati rekiṇī pareśa śaktiḥ ātmā iva bhāsate na tu idantayā kena etat uktam ghaṭaḥ iti yaḥ sthūlaḥ śabdaḥ sa prakāśa jīvita svabhāvaḥ vimarśaḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,5.20^2	 saḥ api hi sthūlaḥ śabdaḥ arthavat pṛthak bhūtaḥ eva bhāti tau nāmaka rūpa lakṣaṇau śabda arthau eka rūpa tayā saḥ ayam iti evaṃrūpa tvena parāmṛśantī adhyavasā yā sā parameśvara śaktiḥ vimarśa rūpāḥ ātma vat eva aham iti anavacchinna tvena bhāti na tu kadācid idantayā vicchinna tvena bhāti vicchinna tvena avabhāse para pratiṣṭha tvāt punar vimarśa antareṇa bhāvyam tatra api evam iti anavasthātaḥ nīlasya prakāśanam eva na syāt pratiṣṭhā lābha abhāvāt tasmāt sarve eva vimarśaḥ prakāśāt avicchinnaḥ eva iti adhyavasāḥ iti ātaḥ ca upasarge iti aṅantaḥ striyām 
ĪPrVV_1,5.21^1	 nanu evam sarvasya eva jñāna kalāpasya aham iti eva pratiṣṭhāne vedya bhūmi sparśaḥ na asti vedya bhuvi ca deśa kāla yogaḥ na tu vedaka aṃśe deśa kāla yoga abhāve ca yat idam jñānām deśa apekṣayā pramātṛ ādi aṃśa apekṣayā ca sa krama tvam lakṣyate tat katham syāt krama abhāve ca eka tvam eva vastutas bhavet tatas ca jñāna smṛti ādibhiḥ tadvān parameśvaraḥ iti yat uktam tat katham nirvahet iti āśaṅkām śamayan pūrva uktam upasaṃharati kevalam bhinna samvedya deśa kāla anurodhataḥ jñāna smṛti avasāya ādi sa kramam pratibhāsate 
ĪPrVV_1,5.21^2	 satyam evam akramam eva saṃvid tattvam kintu sva śakti vaśāt bhinna tvena bhāsitāni yāni vedyāni teṣām mūrti bheda kṛtaḥ yaḥ dūrādūrava etatyauvaitatyādiḥ deśaḥ kriyā bheda kṛtaḥ ca yaḥ cira śīghra krama ādi rūpaḥ kālaḥ tau anurudhya chāyā mātreṇa abalambya jñāna smaraṇa adhyavasāyānām sva aṃśāḥ iva bhānti niraṃśānām api tad bhāsamāna aṃśa kṛtaḥ ca sa krama tva avabhāsaḥ paraspara apekṣayā sva aṃśa apekṣayā ca yadi api kāla kramaḥ eva sphuṭaḥ vijñāneṣu bhāti na deśa kramaḥ tathā api vimūḍhasya parvata saṃvedanam vitatam iva vadara saṃvedanam ca sūkṣmam iva bhāti iti deśa kramaḥ api darśitaḥ tena vedya gata krama svīkāra ābhāsāt sa krama tvam ābhāsamānam api na apāramārthikam ābhāsamānasya para artha tvāt tatas ca yuktam uktam jñāna ādayaḥ asya bhagavataḥ śaktayaḥ iti māyā śaktyā vibhoḥ iti ślokena svarūpa vaicitryam jñānām darśitam anena tu deśa kāla vaicitryam iti viśeṣaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,6.0	 sva ātma abheda dhanān bhāvān= tad apohana ṭaṅkataḥ vhindanyaḥ sva icchayā citra rūpa kṛtam stumaḥ śivaḥ evam smṛti śaktiḥ jñānaśaktiḥ ca nirūpitā atha tad ubhaya anuprāhiṇī apohana śaktiḥ vitatya śloka ekā daśakena aham pratyavam arśaḥ yaḥ prakāśa ātmā ityādinā siddhe sarvasya jīvataḥ iti antena nirṇīyate tatra ślokena pratyavamarśe avikalpaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti sūcyate tatas ślokena śuddhe ahaṃpratyavamarśe apohana vyāpāra asaṃbhavaḥ ucyate tatas sva dṛṣṭau= eva tad upapattiḥ iti ślokena tatas api dvayena aśuddhasya aham iti avamarśasya vikalpa rūpa tā tatas ślokena anusaṃdhānasva api vikalpa rūpa tā evaṃrūpa anusaṃdhāna ādi rūpam eva parameśvarasya sraṣṭṭa tvam iti ślokena tatas prakṛte cit ātmani artha avabhāsasya sattā upasaṃhiyate ślokena tatas dvayena tasma eva artha avabhāsasya anubhava smaraṇa ādau vaicitryam ucyate tat uktiḥ ca prakṛtāyām īśvara rūpasva ātma pratyabhijñāyām upayujyate iti ślokena iti āhnikasya tātparya arthaḥ atha grantha arthaḥ vyākhyāyate 
ĪPrVV_1,6.1^1	 uktim idam savabhāvam avabhāsasya vimarśam iti tatra vimarśaḥ abhilāpa ātmanā śabdena yojitaḥ eva tad yojana akṛtam ca vikalpa rūpa tvam śuddhe api parameśvare prāptam na ca etat iṣṭam tasya saṃsāra pade mā atha ātmani upapatteḥ iti āśaṅkya āha ahaṃpratyavamarśaḥ yaḥ prakāśa ātmā api vāc vapuḥ na asau vikalpaḥ sa hi uktaḥ dvayākṣepī viniścayaḥ prakāśasya śuddha saṃvid rūpasya deha ādi saṃsparśaiḥ anāvilībhūtasya yaḥ ātmā jīvita bhūtaḥ sāra svabhāvaḥ viccheda śūnyaḥ a ntarabhyupagama kalpaḥ ananya mukha prekṣi tva rūpa svātantrya viśrānti rūpaḥ aham iti pratyavamarśaḥ asau vikalpaḥ na bhavati 
ĪPrVV_1,6.1^2	 vikalpa tva āśaṅkāyām bījam darśayati vāc vapuḥ api iti viṣaya rūpāt śrotra grāhyāt śabdāt anyaḥ eva antaravabhāsamānaḥ saṃvid rūpa āveśī śabdana ātma abhilāpaḥ vāc iti anena uktaḥ vakti artham svādhyāsena saḥ ayam iti abhisaṃdhānena yadi vāc vapuḥ kasmāt na vikalpaḥ āha na hi asya vikalpa lakṣaṇam asti tathā hi vividhā kalpanā vividha tvena ca śaṅkitasya kalpaḥ anvavyavacchedanam vikalpaḥ vividha tvam ca bahnau= anagni saṃbhāvanā samāropa nirāse asati bhavat dvayam vahni avahni rūpam samākṣipati tena vikalpe avaśyam tat ca niścetavyam atat ca apohitavyam bhavati 
ĪPrVV_1,6.2^1	 tathā cabhinnayoḥ avabhāsaḥ hi syāt ghaṭā ghaṭayoḥ dvayoḥ prakāśasya iva na anyasya bhedinaḥ tu avabhāsanam ghaṭe hi dṛṣṭe ghaṭa sthānaḥ eva aghaṭe api yogya deśa abhimata sthāna ākramaṇa śīlaḥ vijñāna janakaḥ sva kāraṇa upanītaḥ saṃbhāvyate paṭa ādi svabhāvaḥ atas ghaṭāghaṭayoḥ dvayoḥ avabhāva sasya saṃbhāvanāt samāropaḥ sa avakāśaḥ bhavati aghaṭasya satya ārope niṣedhana lakṣaṇa upohana vyāpāraḥ iti tad anuprāṇitā vikalpa rūpa tā ghaṭaḥ iti etasya niścayasya liṅ saṃbhāvanāyām 
ĪPrVV_1,6.2^2	 yaḥ tu ayam prakāśaḥ nāma tasya sthāne yaḥ saṃbhāvyate sa tāvat aprakāśa rūpaḥ na bhavati tulya kakṣasya hi saṃbhāvanam bhavati na ca yat prakāśena kartavyam tad aprakāśasya kadācid dṛṣṭam saṃbhāvanā āropaṇa ādi balāt eva ca asya aprakāśa rūpa tvam vighaṭeta atas prakāśa tulyasya anyasya aprakāśa rūpasya bhedinaḥ tad tulya kakṣyasya apohana ātmaka bhedana vyāpārāsāhiṣṇoḥ avabhāsanam eva na asti tad abhāve kasya apoṣṭhanam avabhāsa saṃbhave api prakāśa rūpa tvam eva na ca prakāśasya sva rūpa deśa kāla bhedaḥ yena dvitīyaḥ prakāśaḥ ekasmāt apohyeta iti hi iti yasmāt evam tatas dvaya abhāvāt poha asaṃbhave vikalpa rūpatva abhāvāt cit mātre parāmarśa ātmani aham iti pratyavamarśaḥ eva na tu vikalpaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,6.3^1	 nanu ghaṭe pariniṣthita rūpe dṛṣṭe tad darśanam upajīvatā vikalpena katham aghaṭasya niṣedhanam kriyate na hi aghaṭasya kenacid nāma api gṛhītam aghaṭa vāsanā api ghaṭe dṛṣṭe kathaṃkāram prabudhyatām satyam evam śākyaḥ paryanuyojyaḥ na tu vayam yatas tad atad pratibhā bhājā mātrā eva ātad vyapohanāt tad niścayana muktaḥ hi vikalpaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti ayam iha pramātā nāma pramāṇāt atiriktaḥ pramāsu svatantraḥ saṃyojana viyojana ādi ādhāna vaśāt kartā darśitaḥ tasya ca pramātuḥ antar sarva artha avabhāsaḥ cit mātra śarīraḥ api tad sāmāna adhikaraṇya vṛttiḥ api darpaṇa nagara nyāyena asti iti api uktam 
ĪPrVV_1,6.3^2	 evam ca tad pratibhām ghaṭa ābhāsam atad pratibhām ca aghaṭa ābhāsam pramātā bhajate sevate tāvat tad avikalpa daśāyām cit svabhāvaḥ asau ghaṭaḥ cidvat eva viśva śarīraḥ pūrṇaḥ na ca tena kaścid vyavahāraḥ tat māyā vyāpāram ukkāsayan pūrṇam api khaṇḍayati bhāvam tena aghaṭasya ātmanaḥ paṭa ādeḥ ca apohanam kriyate niṣedhana rūpam tat eva vyapohanam āśritya tasma ghaṭasya niścayanam ucyate ghaṭaḥ eva iti eva arthasya saṃbhāvyamāna apara vastu niṣedha rūpa tvāt eṣaḥ eva paritas chedāt takṣaṇa kalpāt paricchedaḥ hi iti yatas evam tasmāt yuktam dvayākṣepī vikalpaḥ iti pūrva śloka ultena vastu dvayena hetū krameṇa uktau yasmāt evam vikalpaḥ tatas aham iti śuddhaḥ vimarśaḥ na vikalpaḥ iti śloka traye mahā vākya arthaḥ śākyaiḥ api pramātuḥ eva ayam vyāpāraḥ uktaḥ ekaḥ pratyavamarśa ākhyaḥ iti atra prapattā iti svayam iti ca vadadbhiḥ sa tu etaiḥ katham samarthyaḥ iti āḥ tām etat 
ĪPrVV_1,6.4–5^1	 nanu evam aham iti api pratyavamarśe anahaṃrūpasya ghaṭa ādeḥ pratiyoginaḥ a pohanīyasya apohe vikalpa rūpa tā katham na syāt iti āśayena āha cit tattvam māyayā hitvā bhinnaḥ eva avabhāti yaḥ dehe buddhau= atha prāṇe kalpite nabhasi iva vā pramātṛ tvena aham iti vimarśaḥ anya vyapohanāt vikalpaḥ eva sa para pratiyogi avabhāsa jaḥ aham iti avamarśaḥ dvidhā śuddhaḥ māyīyaḥ ca tatra śuddhaḥ yaḥ saṃvid mātre viśva abhinne viśva= chāyā ācchurita at chā ātmani vā aśuddhaḥ tu vedya rūpe śarīra ādau tatra śuddhe ahaṃpratyavamarśe pratiyogī na kaścid apohitavyaḥ saṃbhavati ghaṭa ādeḥ api prakāśa sāra tvena apratiyogi tvena anapohya tvāt iti apohya abhāve katham tatra vikalpa rūpa tā aśuddhaḥ tu vedya rūpe śarīra ādau anyasmāt deha ādeḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ ca vyavacchedena bhavan vikalpaḥ eva iti vākya arthaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,6.4–5^2	 akṣara arthaḥ tu cit tattvam prakāśa mātra rūpam hitvā sat api apahastanayāḥ apradhānīkṛtya bhinne dehāt au= aham eva deha ādiḥ nīla ādau prameye pramātā iti abhimānena yaḥ aham sthūlaḥ ityādi vimarśaḥ sa vikalpaḥ eva na tu śuddham pratyavamarśa mātram atra hetuḥ paraḥ dvitīyaḥ deha ādiḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ ca yaḥ pratiyogī tulya kakṣyaḥ anyonya parihārāt ca viruddhaḥ tasya yaḥ avabhāsaḥ samāropaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ tasmāt yatas asau= atat niṣedha anuprāṇitaḥ a ham iti avamarśaḥ jātaḥ aham sthūlaḥ na kṛśaḥ na ghaṭa ādiḥ iti śuddha prakāśa rūpasya apahastana eva deha ādeḥ bheda hetuḥ tad apahastane tu parameśvarasya sva ātma pracchādana icchā rūpā abheda aprakāśanam bhrānti rūpam prati svātantrya rūpāḥ māyā śaktiḥ hetuḥ cit rūpasya ca apahastanam deha ādeḥ eva atyakta vedya bhāvasya bhinnasya eva upapatti śūnya tayā eva pramātṛ tva abhimānaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,6.4–5^3	 tathā ca deha abhimāna bhūmikāyām sthitāḥ cārvākāḥ caitanya viśiṣṭaḥ kāyaḥ puruṣaḥ iti kāyam eva prādhānyena āhuḥ strī bāla mūrkhāṇām tathā abhimānāt tatas api viveka yuktāḥ pākaja utpatti pariṇāma ādi balāt asthiram śarīram manvānāḥ prāṇa śakti samadhiṣṭhānena ca vinā vikāra śata āveśam śarīrasya paśyantaḥ bubhukṣā pipāsā yoga yogyam prāṇam eva ātmānam kecana śruti anta vidaḥ manyante tatas api samadhika viveka bhājaḥ prāṇasya api anitya tvāt anusaṃdhāna yogya tām apaśyantaḥ jñāna sukha ādi āśraya bhūtām buddhim eva kāṇāda prabhṛtayaḥ ātmānam āhuḥ apare tasyāḥ api yogidśāyām vedya bhāvāt apara tvam manyamānāḥ asaṃvedya parva rūpam yat na kiṃcid rūpam sakala vedya rāśi vinirmuktam śūnya tvāt nabhaḥ tulyam na tu mahābhūta ākāśa svabhāvam tat pramātṛ tattvam śūnya brahma vādinaḥ sāṃkhya prabhṛtayaḥ āhuḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,6.4–5^4	 tasmin= api vedye śunyā antaram tatra api śūnya antram iti yāvat bhedaḥ tāvat kalpanā na truṭyati iti tad artham āha kalpite iti na ca anavasthā parama artha prakāśa balena yatas sarvasya prakāśaḥ na tu deha ādi vaśāt tayā tu abhimāna mātram dehaḥ pramātā iti saṅkoca mātra rūpam cit tattvam śūnyam bhū talam yathā ghaṭa abhāvaḥ saṅkoca upari vedya aṃśa= chāyā ācchuritam tu cit tattvam eva buddhi prāṇa deha ādi iti amī eva bhūmikā viśeṣāḥ uttarottaram āroha tām yoginām jāgrat āditayā piṇḍa sthādi tayā ca āgameṣu bhaṇyante apahastanam ca vyākhyāsyateḥ kalā udvalitam etat ca cit tattvam kartṛ tām ayam acit rūpasya śūnya ādeḥ mitam guṇa tayā sthitam iti tat sthitam aśuddhaḥ aham iti avamarśaḥ vikalpaḥ eva 
ĪPrVV_1,6.6^1	 dvividhaḥ api ca ayam aham pratyayaḥ dvidhā anubhava mātra rūpaḥ ca anusaṃdhāna ātmā ca śiva ātmani aham iti sadāśiva ātmani aham idam iti śuddhaḥ dvidhā aśuddhaḥ api aham sthūlaḥ iti yaḥ aham sthūlaḥ abhavam saḥ aham kṛśa bālaḥ yuvā sthaviraḥ saḥ eva aham iti ca aśuddhaḥ dvividhaḥ tatra śuddhe vikalpa rūpa tvam apratiṣṭham eva iti uktam aśuddhe tu anubhava rūpe vikalpa tvam upapāditam aśuddhe api tu anusaṃdhāna ātmaka tayā abhedasya prasphuraṇāt kaścid avikalpaka tvam śaṅketa tasya vyāmoham vyapohitum āha kādācid ka avabhāse yā pūrva ābhāsa ādi yojanā saṃskārāt kalpanā proktā sā api bhinna avabhāsini dehe ityādi vartate kādācid kaḥ kadācid bhavaḥ niyata deśa kāla ākāraḥ avabhāsaḥ yasya deha ādeḥ sva lakṣaṇa rūpasya tatra yā pūrva ābhāsena bāla ādi śarīra avabhāsena yojanāḥ yaḥ aham bālaḥ saḥ eva adya yuvā iti anusaṃdhānam ādi grahaṇāt uttareṇa bhāvinā ābhāsena saha yojanā sthaviraḥ bhavitāsmi iti sā yojanā sarvā kalpanā vikalpaḥ eva na tu śuddhaḥ pratyavamarśaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,6.6^2	 atra deha ādeḥ viśeṣaṇam hetu tva āśayena yatas bhinna tā avabhāsi tvam eva deha ādeḥ tadānīm api avichinnam yadi hi tasya deha ādeḥ sarvatas pūrṇa tvam avaccheda hīna tvam paśyan anusaṃdhānam aham idam iti vidadhyāt tat iyam sadāśiva bhūḥ kena vikalpāt pada tvena bhaṇyeta yāvatā avicchinne eva saḥ anusaṃdhiḥ bhinnepi katham anusaṃdhānam iti ced āha saṃskārāt prāktana anubhava kṛta vāsanā prabodha ja smṛti vaśāt iti yāvat prāṇe bala abala vaśāt anusaṃdhiḥ buddhau jñāna sukha ādi tāratamyāt śūnye vaitatya avaitatya yogāt ayam api vikalpaḥ eva evam saḥ eva ayam ghaṭaḥ iti ghaṭa ādi anusaṃdhāne api vikalpa tvam mantavyam kintu etāsu anusaṃdhāna bhūmiṣu vidyā śaktiḥ ādhikyena acira dyuti vat dīpyate iti tāsām para pada pariśīlana prathama kalpa abhyupāya tvam abhyupāgaman guravaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,6.7^1	 na ca deha ādīnām pūrva pūrva pramātṛ vedya tā yena pramātuḥ aprakāśe prameyam na bhāti tad prakāśaḥ ca na pūrva prakāśam vinā saḥ api na pramātṛ antara prakāśam vinā iti anavasthā syāt api tu śuddha prakāśaḥ eva viśvasya prakāśaḥ iti nirūpayan ukta yuktyā sadā eva sṛṣṭi ādi śakti aviyogaḥ bhagavataḥ uktaḥ bhavati iti darśayati tat evam vyavahāre api prabhuḥ deha ādim āviśan bhāntam eva antarartha ogham icchayā bhāsayet bahis yat pūrvam darśitam dehe buddhau ityādi tat evam upapadyate katham yadi vyavahāre māyā pade deha prāṇa ādim api prabhuḥ eva prakāśa parama arthaḥ icchayā māyā śakti rūpayā āviśan deha prāṇa ādi prādhānyena svarūpam pradarśayan antar saṃbinmātre bhāntam aham iti evaṃrūpam artha ogham icchayā eva bahis idam iti bhāsayati tatas etat upapadyate anyathā tu anavasthā syāt hetau liṅ api śabdaḥ eva śabdaḥ ca bhinna kramau yat etāvat uktam tat iti tasmāt hetoḥ evam jātam vakṣyamāṇa rūpam kiṃtat 
ĪPrVV_1,6.7^2	 yat kila prabhuḥ parasparam vyavahāra kāle kraya vikraya prekṣā vyākhya ādau caitra maitra ādi saṃbandhinaḥ deha prāṇa ādīn ekatayā tāvati vyavahāre āviśan antar bhāntam eva anujjhita antar prakāśam eva santam bahis eka ābhāsa tayā bhāsayati iti saṃbhāvyate iti etat jātam iti saṃbhāvanāyām liṅ tena tena pramātrā saha asmin kāle aikyam sṛjyate anyena pramātrā aikyam saṃhriyate ghaṭa ādi mātra rūpe sthitiḥ kriyate pūrṇa svarūpa nimīlanāt tirobhāvaḥ ādhīyate tāvatī ābhāse aikya avabhāsa pūrṇa tva vitaraṇāt anugrahaḥ kriyate tena na kevalam mahā sṛṣṭiṣu mahā sthitiṣu mahāpralayeṣu prakopa tirodhāneṣu dīkṣā jñāna ādi anugraheṣu bhagavataḥ krṭya pañcaka yogaḥ yāvat satatam eva vyavahārepi yat uktam sadā sṛṣṭi vinodāya sadā sthiti sukha asine sadā tribhuvana āhāra tṛptāya svāmine namaḥ iti pratikṣaṇam aviśrāntaḥ trailokyam kalpanā śataiḥ kalpayan= api kaḥ api ekaḥ nirvikalpaḥ jayati ajaḥ ityādi ca tathā  prākāmyam ātmani yadā prakaṭīkaroṣi vyaktoḥ iti ca 
ĪPrVV_1,6.8	 iha antarartha abhāva bhāsaḥ sthitaḥ eva tat kim tatra kāraṇa antara cintayā iti prakṛtam prameyam tad siddhaye upapattiḥ uktā tena vinā icchā rūpaḥ pratyavamarśaḥ na syāt iti tad prasaṅgāt pratyavamarśa vikalpa ādi svarūpam upapāditam iti śiṣyāṇām dhiyam samādhātum prakṛtam prameyam upapādayan upasaṃharati evam smṛtau vikalpe vā api apohana parāyaṇe jñāne vā api antarābhāsaḥ sthitaḥ eva iti niścitam prakāśa ātmā parameśvaraḥ eva yatas deha ādi pramātṛ tā abhimāna daśāyām api vastutas pramātā evam iti atas hetoḥ idam siddham bhavati smaraṇe apohana jīvite ca vikalpe anubhava jñāne ca antara ābhāsaḥ prakāśa viśrāntaḥ sthitaḥ eva na atra saṃśayaḥ kaścid yadi hi deha ādiḥ eva parama artha pramātā syāt tat śarīrasya prāṇasya dhiyaḥ śūnyasya vā antar ghaṭa ādi iti na kiṃcid etat ghaṭa ādi parihāreṇa deha ādeḥ sthita tvāt parama artha prakāśaḥ tu sarvaṃsahaḥ iti tatra antar viśvam iti anāyāsa siddham etat 
ĪPrVV_1,6.9^1	 nanu antara ābhāsa vargasya bahis ābhāsanam yadi sarvatra asti kaḥ tarhi smaraṇa ādau ābhāsa bhedaḥ na ca asau na saṃvedyate sphuṭa tā sphuṭa tā ādi prasphuraṇasya anapahnavanīya tvāt iti āśaṅkya āha kiṃtu naisargikaḥ jñāne bahis ābhāsana ātmani pūrva anubhava rūpaḥ tu sthitaḥ sa smaraṇa ādiṣu anubhava jñānasya idam nīlam iti antar avabhāsam vahirābhāsayataḥ sva antarbhāva ābhāsaḥ naisargika nisṛṣṭeḥ svātantryāt āyātaḥ na tu smaraṇa ādeḥ iva anya jñāna kṛta vāsanā ādi balāt 
ĪPrVV_1,6.9^2	 smaraṇe utprekṣaṇe pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvini adhyavasāye ca yaḥ antar nīla ādi avabhāsaḥ bāhya tayā adhyavasāyitavyaḥ na asau sva ātmoyaḥ api tu pūrva anubhava saṃskāra jaḥ asau tatra saṃskāraḥ nāma anubhavasya kāla antare api anuvartamāna tā atas asau= anuvartamānaḥ anubhavaḥ yatas nīla ādi ābhāsa saṃbhinnaḥ tatas tad tādātmya āpannam smaraṇa ādi api tathā nirbhāsate tatas eva smaraṇa kāla asaṃbhavī ābhāsaḥ tad anubhava pūrva kāla kalita eva iti svayam smaraṇa ādeḥ nirviṣaya tvam gṛhīta grāhi tvam ca uddhoṣyate etat eva asphuṭa tvam iti siddhaḥ anubhava smaraṇa ādau ābhāsa bhedaḥ antara ābhāsa vargasya bahis ābhāsanam anya avyavadhānena sphuṭa tā vyavadhānena tu tātkālika tva abhāvāt asphuṭa tā iti 
ĪPrVV_1,6.10	 nanu anubhava jñānāt aindriyakāt anyat sarvam jñānam vyavadhānena bahis ābhāsana rūpam prāptam iti āśaṅkya pravibhāgam āha sa naisargikaḥ eva asti vikalpe svaira cāriṇi yathā abhimata saṃsthāna ābhāsanāt buddhi gocare yaḥ pratyakṣa vyāpāram anupajīvan vyākṣepa sāra tayā manorājya saṅkalpa ādi vikalpaḥ sa svaram kṛtvā sva preraṇena prapreraṇa nairapekṣyeṇa svātantryeṇa carati udeti vyayate ca tatra yaḥ bahis ābhāsaḥ nīla ādeḥ antara ābhāsa mayasya sa naisargikaḥ eva tathā hi aparidṛṣṭa pūrvam api śvetam daśana śataka lota kara yugala yuktam dantinam antar pramātṛ bhūmau sthitam bahis antaḥkaraṇa bhūmau svacchadhī darpaṇa ātmikāyām sa vikalpaḥ tātkālikam eva bhāsayati 
ĪPrVV_1,7.1^1	 asmāt ca antara ābhāsa saṃbhava samarthana prasaṅga āgatāt ābhāsa bheda vicārāt śāstre yat prayoanam mukhya tayā abhisaṃhitam sva ātmani īśvara pratyabhijñāna rūpam tad adhikaraṇa siddhāntanītyāḥ anāyāsa siddham iti darśayati atas eva yathā abhīṣṭa samullekha avabhāsanāt jñāna kriye sphuṭe eva siddhe sarvasya jīvataḥ pratibhāti ghaṭaḥ iti yadi api viṣaya upaśliṣṭam eva pratibhānam bhāti tathā api na tad viṣayasya svakam vapuḥ api tu saṃvedanam eva tat tathā cakāsti mām prati bhāti iti pramātṛ lagna tvāt tathā ca veda tam eva bhāntam anu bhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti śatrā avirata sphuraṇa tvam karma pravacanīyena tadīya svātantrya upakalpita nirmāṇa kriyā janitaḥ vedya vedaka bhāva rūpaḥ lakṣaṇa ātmā saṃbandhaḥ dyotitaḥ kevalam viṣaya ullekhana balāt bahis krama avabhāsaḥ samarthitaḥ sa sa krama yaugapadyādi vicitra rūpaḥ yaḥ padārthānām vakṣyamāṇa īśvara svātantrya rūpa deśa kāla śakti upakalpitaḥ kramaḥ deśa kāla paripāṭī tena rūṣitā pratibimba kalpa tayā uparaktāḥ yā pratibhā uktā kevalam bhinna saṃvedya 
ĪPrVV_1,7.1^2	 ityādinā eṣā iti ca sarvasya sva kāśa rūpāḥ paramārthataḥ ca antarmukha tvena prakāśa mātra parama artha tayā bheda abhāvāt akramā sā eva maheśvaraḥ avidyamānaḥ antar paricchedaḥ deśataḥ kālataḥ svarūpataḥ ca yasyāḥ cittaḥ saṃvidaḥ tat eva rūpam yasya iti atas eva bahirmukha prakāśa ātmaka vijñāna svabhāvasya pramāṇa vargasya yaḥ antar pratyābhāsam idam idam iti ananta kalpaḥ vikalpa mayaḥ vimarśa ātmā pramāsam ūhaḥ tatra saṃyojana viyojana viśrama ādi rūpa aneka prakāra svātantrya paripūrṇaḥ śuddha ahaṃpratyavamarśa mayaḥ pramātā sa bhaṇyate atas ca bahis ghaṭa prakāśaḥ ayam ghaṭaḥ iti antar vikalpaḥ svīkṛta pūrvarūpaḥ aham iti tad ubhaya viśrānti sthānam iti iyat pūrṇam prakāśasya sva rūpam 
ĪPrVV_1,7.2	 atra eva upapattim pradarśayitum anvayam tāvat āha tad tad vibhinna saṃvitti mukhaiḥ eka pramātari pratitiṣṭhatsu bhāveṣu jñātā iyam upapadyate saṃvid niṣṭhā hi viṣaya vyavasthitayaḥ iti yat ucyate tat na bhinna rūpa prakā ātmaka saṃvid mātra viśrāntyā siddhyati api tu tāḥ tāḥ vibhinnāḥ saṃvidaḥ niścaya rūpāḥ pramā ātmānaḥ yāḥ tāni eva mukhāni dvārāṇi upāyāḥ mārgāḥ taiḥ mukhaiḥ nadī srotaḥ sthānīyaiḥ yadi amī bhāvāḥ nīla sukha ādayaḥ uhyamānā ekasmin aham iti pramātṛ rūpe mahā saṃvid samudre pratitiṣṭhanti ābhimukhyena viśrāntim bhajante tatas eṣu parasparam samanvaya rūpam tat jñātā iyam tat upapattyā ghaṭate jñātīnām bhāvaḥ tad śabda pravṛtti nimittam parasparam jānīyuḥ iti karma ca anyonya yogakṣema udvahana ātmakam jñātā iyam tat ca samanvaya abhiprāyeṇa iha darśitam na jaḍānām svatas samanvayaḥ kadācid api iti pratipādayitum 
ĪPrVV_1,7.3	 tathā ca vyatireka mukhena etat eva āha deśa kāla krama juṣām arthānām sva samāpinām sakṛt ābhāsa sādhyaḥ asau= anyathā kaḥ samanvayaḥ arthānām jaḍānām tad jñānām tad vikalpānām tad niścayānām ca deśa kramam kāla kramam ca atyajatām sva samāpinām sva rūpa mātra pratiṣṭhānām kaḥ samanvayaḥ na kaścid iti arthaḥ yatas hi asau samanvayaḥ sakṛt ābhāsena deśa kāla ākāra miśrīkaraṇa ātmanā yojana ābhāsena sādhayitum śakyaḥ na anyathā na hi pṛthak pṛthak parikṣīṇeṣu srotaḥsu tad uhyamānāḥ tṛṇa ulapa ādayaḥ samanvayam kaṃcid yānti iti aneka tvena deśa kāla ādi bhedaḥ iti āśayena sakṛt śabdaḥ tat niṣedha tātparyeṇa prayuktaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,7.5	 tatra kaḥ asau samanvayaḥ iti āśaṅkya bahutara vyāpakam kārya kāraṇa bhāvam tāvat darśayati pratyakṣa anupalambhānām tad tad bhinna aṃśa pātinām kārya kāraṇa tā siddhi hetu ta eka pramātṛ jāḥ iha anubhūtaḥ viṣayaḥ prakāśate smṛtau tatra viṣayasya asau smṛtiḥ na nūtanaḥ prakāśaḥ api tu asya sa prakāśaḥ prācyaḥ anubhavaḥ eva sa ca anubhavaḥ jñāna rūpa tvena jñeya rūpa tva abhāvāt na jñāna antara saṃvedyaḥ api tu sva prakāśaḥ sa ca smṛti kāle yadi asan tat katham prakāśatām bhavatu vā asau tathā api smṛtiḥ syāt tasmāt etat evam upapadyate yat eva smṛti sva saṃvedanam tat eva anubhavasya sva saṃvedanam na tu aparam sva saṃvedana vyatiriktam pratyakṣam anumāna ādikam vā tatra kramate tatas ca tāvat kāla api avichinnam ekam yat sva saṃvedanam tat eva pramātṛt tvam iti siddham anyatra anubhavitari smartā anyaḥ naḥ upapadyate iti anayā chāyayā smṛtyā pramātṛ siddhiḥ pūrvam uktāḥ idānīm tu sva saṃvedana ekībhāvena bhaṅgi antareṇa iti viśeṣaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,7.6^1	 nanu anubhava atirikte api arthe santu vikalpāḥ pramāṇam aprāmāṇyam hi bādha balāt bhavati bādha abhāve tat katham syāt iti āśaṅkya saḥ api ayam bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ satya asatya pravibhā janayā viśveṣām vyavahārāṇām jīvita bhūtaḥ naḥ ekena pramātṛ tattvena vinā ghaṭataḥ iti vitatya darśayati bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ api sva ātma niṣṭhā virodhinām jñānānām udiyāt eka pramātṛ pariniṣṭhiteḥ bādha abhāve prāmāṇyam iti etad artham avaśya samarthyaḥ yaḥ bādha vyavahāraḥ saḥ api katham iti api śabdasya arthaḥ iha śuktyā tāvat rajatasya na kācid bādhā nāma kriyamāṇā dṛśyate śukti jñānena rajata jñānam bādhyate iti api na yuktam svasmin viṣaye ātmani ca svarūpe dvayoḥ jñānayoḥ pariniṣṭhitayoḥ viśr 
ĪPrVV_1,7.6^2	 antayoḥ anyonyam virodhasya abhāvāt atha ayam paraspara parihāraḥ eva virodhaḥ tarhi sarveṣām jñānānām virodhāt bādhya bādhaka bhāvasya sva ātmani pariniṣṭhā eva na labhyā iti sutarām vighaṭeta satya itara pravibhāgaḥ nañapi atra tantreṇa vyākhyeyaḥ etat uktam bhavati yadi jñānam svayam naśyati tadā kim jñāna antareṇa asya kṛtam na hi tena tad kāle asaṃbhava tā tasya viṣaya apahāraḥ kartum śakyaḥ na rājatam iti api jñānam svam rajata abhāvam viṣayīkurvat na viṣayam apaharet rajata jñānasya 
ĪPrVV_1,7.6^3	 atha api jñāna antareṇa nāśyate iti api pakṣaḥ tatra api sarveṣām jñānām iyam eva saraṇiḥ iti kiṃcid eva bādhyam iti katham syāt yadā tu rajata jñānam śukti jñānam ca ekatra sva saṃvedane viśrānyataḥ tadā etat upapadyate tathā hi ekatra api pramātṛ tattve viśrāmyatām jñānānām na eka prakārā eva viśrāntiḥ api tu vicitra tayā eva sā saṃvedyate tathā hi nīlam iti utpalam iti jñāne pramātari viśrāmyantī paraspara uparāga ābhāsena viśrāmyataḥ ghaṭaḥ iti paṭaḥ iti parasparānāḥ keṣeṇa śuktikāḥ iti na rajatam iti vā jñānam rajatam iti jñānasya unmūlanam tadīya vimarśa ātmaka pramā rūpa vyāpāra anuvartana vidhvaṃsam kurvat pramātari pratiṣṭhām bhajate evam kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādau viśrānti vaicitryam prameya asaṃbhavi pramātrā svātantryeṇa nirmitam tatas eva asya pramāsvatantra tā dāyi vācyam evam ekatra pramātari pūrva jñānasya parivarjanena yatas niścitā sthitiḥ iti bādhya bādhaka vyavahāraḥ upapannaḥ nīla ādi vat kila tān api vyavahārān saḥ eva parameśvaraḥ svātantryāt ābhāsayati tat te api satyāḥ eva iti 
ĪPrVV_1,7.7	 atra parakīyam matam āśaṅkate dūṣayiṣyāmi iti vivikta bhū tala jñānam ghaṭa abhāvam atiḥ yathā tathā ced śuktikā jñānam rūpya jñāna apramātva vid iha śuktikā jñānam sva ātmānam saṃvidat sva ātma abhinnam pramāṇa tvam budhyate tad paricchinatti iti nyāyāt tad paricchedana āntarīyakaḥ ca anya vyavacchedaḥ iti aśukti jñāna rūpasya rajata jñānasya apramāṇa tva vedanam tat eva ucyate yat etat śuktikā saṃvedanā bhinna pramāṇa tva vedanam na ca etat apūrvam yat vastu antara jñānam eva vastu antara abhāva jñānam iti śuddha bhū bhāga grahaṇam eva hi ghaṭa abhāva grahaṇam iti prasiddham etat evam apramāṇa tva saṃvedanam eva rajata jñānasya bādhya tvam ucyate atas ca bādhya bādhaka tvam evam siddham iti ced asmābhiḥ ucyate tat kim pramātra aikyena iti 
ĪPrVV_1,7.8	 atra prasaṅgāt abhāva vyavahārasya siddhau tattvam upapādayiṣyan dṛṣṭāntam eva tāvat para darśane dūṣayati na evam śuddha sthala jñānāt siddhyet tasya aghaṭa ātmanā na tu upalabdhi yogyasya api atra abhāvaḥ ghaṭa ātmanaḥ yaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ uktaḥ saḥ eva na kutas iti ced ucyate iha bhū talam na ghaṭaḥ iti tādātmyena abhāvaḥ vyavahartavyaḥ kadācid kadācid vyatirekeṇa iha bhū tale ghaṭaḥ naḥ iti tatra śuddha bhū tala jñānāt ādyaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ sidhyati yatra dṛśya tvam naḥ upayogi upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ api hi yasya na asti piśāca ādeḥ svabhāva balāt yasya vā śabda ādeḥ tad gāhaka śrotra ādi sāmagrī sākalyasya tatra eka jñāna saṃsargi vaḥ tu antara pratipatti abhāvena aniścayāt tasya api tādātmyena ayam abhāvaḥ gṛhyate bhū talam na piśācaḥ na śabdaḥ iti yatra tu dṛśya tvam viśeṣaṇam avaśyam apayogi tatra vyatirekeṇa abhāve vyavahartavye naḥ eṣaḥ abhyupāyaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,7.9	 kutas iti ced atiaprasaṅgāt iti brūmaḥ tam eva darśayati viviktam bhū talam śaśvat bhāvānām sva ātma niṣṭhiteḥ tat katham jātu tat jñānam bhinnasya abhāva sādhanam vidyamāne api ghaṭe bhū talam śuddham eva na hi bhāvāḥ miśrībhavanti tatas ca tadā api śuddha bhū tala jñānam asti iti sati api ghaṭe katham abhāvaḥ vyatirekeṇa na vyavahriyate atra bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti tat jñānam iti vivikta bhū tala bhāga jñānam jātu iti kasyāṃcid eva daśāyām ghaṭa asaṃnidhāna rūpāyām bhinnasya ghaṭasya abhāvam sādhayati na tu sarvadā iti kena prakāreṇa bhavet etena atra bhū tale piśācaḥ na asti iti api syāt iti āpatitam mantavyam 
ĪPrVV_1,7.10^1	 nanu evam vyatireka abhāva niṣṭhaḥ vyavahāraḥ loke tāvat avigītaḥ asyāṃcid eva daśāyām dṛṣṭaḥ tatra kā gatiḥ iti āśaṅkya cirantanaiḥ aparidṛṣṭam tad siddhi prakāram darśayati kim tu āloka cayaḥ andhasya sparśaḥ vā uṣṇa ādikaḥ mṛduḥ tatra asti sādhayet tasya sva jñānam aghaṭa ātma tām iha bhāvaḥ eva bhāva antarasya abhāvaḥ iti vyavahartavyaḥ iti ayam tāvat aparityājyaḥ prātītikaḥ panthāḥ tatra bhāvasya bhāva antareṇa yaḥ ādhārya ādhāra bhāvaḥ saḥ eva bhāva tad abhāvayoḥ tatas ca bhū tale ghaṭa vyatiriktam vastu antaram śilā ādikam āloka puñja ādikam vā yat cākṣuṣe jñāne bhāti tat eva vyavahriyate bhū tale ghaṭa abhāvaḥ bhū tale ghaṭaḥ na asti iti vā yatra api na asti cakṣuḥ vyāpāraḥ netra nimīlana saṃtama sādau tatra api bhū tale ghaṭa ucita kaṭhina sparśa viviktam mṛdum uṣṇam śītam anuṣṇa aśītam vā gṛhṇan tam eva atra ghaṭa abhāvaḥ iti vyavaharati vāyu sparśasya sarvagasya avaśyaṃbhāvāt iti vākya arthaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,7.10^2	 padārthaḥ tu kim tu iti svam ata upakṣepāya sva pratibhā praśna parāmarśaḥ kim punar atra nyāyyam iti tatra āha tatra bhū tale āloka cayaḥ tāvat asti jñeyaḥ andhasya uṣṇa ādikaḥ sparśaḥ asti tasya āloka cayasya sparśasya vā yat sva jñānam anya ghaṭa ādi viviktena svena rūpeṇa jñānam tat kartṛ tasya āloka ādeḥ aghaṭa rūpa tām ghaṭa abhāva rūpa tām tatra bhū tale sādhayati iti śakyaḥ a yam arthaḥ śaki lij ca iti liṅ āntara prāṇa spandana janita sūkṣma śabda ākarṇanāt ca śrotra ādi sākalyam saṃbhavāyamānaḥ tam eva śabdam eka jñāna saṃsargiṇam śṛṇvan śabda antaram niṣedhayati naḥ iha anyaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,7.10^3	 tad sūkṣma śabda abhāvam api sūkṣmatama antar nāda avahita śrotraḥ vedayate rasa gandha sparśa abhāvaḥ api danta udaka rasam tri puṭikā gandham kāyīyam ca sparśam saṃvedayamānena eva rasa abhāvaḥ vedyaḥ na hi eka jñāna saṃsarga yogya vastu antara upalambhena vinā upalabdhi kāraṇa sākalya niścayaḥ asti iti ekāntaḥ eṣaḥ acira pravṛtta tad tad viṣaya anubhava kalpitasya tadā eva dhvaṃsānāśaṅkanāt karaṇasya kāraṇa sākalya niścayaḥ kim eka jñāna saṃsargi tayā iti ced na tattva bhāva upalipsuḥ hi prayatnena tat tad indriya adhiṣṭhānam vyāpārayan= eva lakṣyate 
ĪPrVV_1,7.11^1	 nanu evam adṛśya asya api piśāca ādeḥ niṣedha vyavahāraḥ vyatirekeṇa api prāpnoti sa hi āloka puñjaḥ yathā ghaṭāt anyaḥ tadvat piśāca ādeḥ api tat etat āśaṅkya āha piśācaḥ syāt anālokaḥ api āloka abhyantare yathā adṛśyaḥ bhū talasya antar na niṣedhyaḥ sa sarvathā ālokapuñjaḥ yadi api piśācāt vyatiriktaḥ yadi api ca ālokaḥ asti apiśāca ātmā iti etāvat siddhyati tathā api atra piśācaḥ na asti iti etat aśakyam adhyavasātum ghaṭaḥ hi ālokapūra madhye api asaṃbhāvyaḥ ghaṭa saṃnidhau tatra ālokapūrā samarpaṇāt atas ca siddhi ati idam atra ghaṭaḥ na asti iti piśācaḥ tu tādṛś svabhāvaḥ yaḥ bhū tala madhye āloka madhye api vā bhavan bhū talasya ālokasya vā tām nibiḍa tām na vihanti tatas ca āloka madhye tasya saṃbhāvanāt katham vyatirekeṇa niṣedha vyavahāraḥ evam rūpa madhye rasa ādeḥ saṃbhāvanāt tasya api aniṣedhaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,7.11^2	 yadi api anālokaḥ ālokāt anyaḥ piśācaḥ tathā api asau bhū talasya antar madhye adṛśyaḥ bhavati iti saṃbhāvyate yathā tadvat eva ālokasya abhyantarepi saḥ asti iti saṃbhāvyate eva tatas ca yadi api ālokaḥ tatas anyaḥ iti anena pathā niṣiddhaḥ piśācaḥ tathā api sarva prakāreṇa na niṣiddhaḥ iti tad abhāva nibandhanāḥ katham tatra vyavahārāḥ pravartantām iti śloka arthaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,7.12	 evam prasaṅgāt abhāva vyavahārasya tattvam upadarśya prakṛte yojayati evam rūpya vidā bhāva rūpā śukti matiḥ bhavet na tu ādya rajata jñapteḥ syāt aprāmāṇya vedikā yathā ālokaḥ ghaṭa abhāvaḥ iti āloke gṛhīte prāk gṛhītasya ghaṭasya na kiṃcid āyātam tathā eva śukti jñānam rūpya jñāna abhāvaḥ iti iyat saṃbhāvyate yathā ghaṭa jñānam ghaṭa jñāna prāmāṇya saṃvid paṭa jñāna abhāvaḥ paṭa jñāna abhāva prāmāṇya saṃvid iyatā ca na pūrva pravṛttam paṭa jñānam apramāṇībhavati eṣā hi tasya ghaṭa jñānasya svarūpa cintā sarvāḥ na jñāna antarasya ādyasya kim api atas jātam evam śuktiḥ iyam iti na rajatam idam iti ca jñānam eva sva ātmanā prakāśatām aham śuktau rajata abhāve ca pramāṇam na tu rajate iti tāvatā tu prāktanasya rajata jñānasya na kiṃcid vṛttam iti tad viṣayīkṛtam rajatam katham asatyam syāt 
ĪPrVV_1,7.13^1	 nanu idam iti anena tat eva parāmṛśyate yatra rajata jñānam abhūt tatra eva idānīm na rajatam iti śuktiḥ iti ca jñānam pramāṇa bhūtam jātam tat atas anumīyate tat prācyam rajata jñānam apramāṇam iti na hi etat saṃbhavati viruddha viṣaya dvaya avagāhi jñāna dvayam pramāṇam ekatra viṣayībhavati iti tat ayam ānumānikaḥ bādha vyavahāraḥ bhaviṣyati iti āśaṅkya āha dharmya siddheḥ api bhavet bādhāḥ na eva anumānataḥ sva saṃvedana siddhā tu yuktā sa eka pramātṛ jāḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,7.13^2	 na kevalam sva saṃvedanāt na siddhyati bādhā yāvat anumānataḥ api na siddhyati dharmiṇaḥ asiddheḥ api śabdāt hetoḥ vyāpteḥ ca apiḥ ubhayatra neyaḥ iha dharmiṇi siddhe siddhena hetunā smaryamāṇa vyāptikena sādhya dharma ayoga vyavacchedaḥ anumāna vyāpāraḥ iha ca prācye rūpya jñāne dharmiṇi aprāmāṇyam sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ tatra śuktikā jñānam vā na rajatam iti jñānam vā tad jñāna viṣayī kārya tvam vā viṣaya gatam hetūkriyeta na ca etat yuktam tad kāle prācya rūpya bodhasya dharmiṇaḥ abhāvāt na ca api tasya śukti jñāna ādayaḥ dharmāḥ na ca apakṣa dharmāt sādhya siddhiḥ atas smaryamāṇam tad dharmi syāt iti api asat 
ĪPrVV_1,7.13^3	 atha śuktiḥ na rajata jñānasya viṣayaḥ iti sādhyate śuktikā jñāna viṣaya tvāt iti tat yadi idānīm tadā siddha sādhanam atha pūrvam tadā tad pūrva sva saṃvedanena bādhya viṣaya tā kena ca evam vyāptiḥ gṛhītā yatra idānīm anyat jñānam tatra pūrvam anyat na bhavati iti anumā anantareṇa iti ced ananvasthā etena etat pratyuktam ekasmin viṣaye katham jñāna dvayam syāt iti kaḥ hi eka viṣaya tām tayoḥ jñānayoḥ jānīyāt te hi tāvat sva ātmani sva viṣaye ca viśrāmyate iti uktam iti anumānataḥ api na bādhā na ca tathābhūtam api vyavadhānam atra pratītau saṃvedyate sva saṃvedana siddha tayā jhaṭiti bhāsanāt atas eva etat api aśakyam vaktum mā bhūt bādhā nāma iti evam para pakṣe anupapattim pradarśya sva pakṣe eka pramātṛ pariniṣṭhiteḥ udiyāt bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ iti vākyena pratijñātam nigamayati yuktā sā ekasmāt pramātuḥ yadi jāyeta iti saḥ eva hi tathā nirmātā iti vyākhyātam eva sthite ca evam yadi vyavahāra siddhaye anyathā anupapattiḥ api ucyate tat ucyatām kāmam adhunā sarvam siddhyati iti 
ĪPrVV_1,7.14^1	 na kevalam ete kārya kāraṇa bhāva smaraṇa bādhā vyavahārāḥ sakala loka yātrā sāmānya vyavahāra bhūtāḥ eka pramātṛ pratiṣṭhāḥ yāvat avāntara vyavahārāḥ api ye kraya vikraya ādayaḥ sa malāḥ upadeśya upadeśa bhāva ādayaḥ ca nirmalāḥ tepi eka pramātṛ niṣṭhāḥ eva bhavanti vyavahārāḥ hi sarve samanvaya prāṇāḥ iti upasaṃhāra krameṇa darśayati ittham atyartha bhinna artha avabhāsa khacite vibhau sa malaḥ vimalaḥ vā api vyavahāraḥ anubhūyate 
ĪPrVV_1,7.14^2	 tad tad vibhinnaḥ iti śloka dvaya uktena anena upapatti prakāreṇa anvaya vyatireka ātmanā tathā śloka antaraiḥ uktena vyavahāra udāharaṇa prakāreṇa idam api mantavyam yat vibhau deśa kālān avacchinne atas eva atyartha bhinnaiḥ māyā balāt bheda eka prāṇitaiḥ nīla sukha ādi ābhāsaiḥ pratibimba kalpaiḥ anatirikta tayā vartamānaiḥ khacite svarūpānanyathā bhāvena uparakte viśrāntaḥ sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ anubhūyate anubhavaḥ eva atra dṛḍhatamam pramāṇam iti yāvat anubhūyate ca sa upadeśaiḥ avadhāna paraiḥ yena eṣām yā eva saṃsāra daśāsaṃmatā vyavahāra daśā sā eva pramātṛ tattva prakhyā ātmikā śiva bhūmiḥ yat uktam  saṃbandhe sāvadhāna tā iti apratyabhijñāta ātma parama arthānām sa malaḥ vyavahāraḥ anyeṣām saḥ eva nirmalaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,8.0^1	 sva saṃvedana saṃsiddha vyavahāra vaśena yaḥ nityam maheśvaraḥ siddhaḥ siddhānām tam stumaḥ śivam evam jñāna smaraṇa apohanāni vyutpādya eṣām ekam āśrayam vinā vyavahāraḥ na yuktaḥ iti nirūpitam etāvatā na ced antar kṛtā iti atra yat uktam ekaḥ iti tat parighaṭitam antara ābhāsa samarthanena antar kṛta ananta viśva rūpaḥ iti api nirūpitam yat atra eva maheśvaraḥ iti uktam tat māheśvaryam svātantrya rūpam upapādayitavyam tat ca jñāna viṣayam kriyā viṣayam ca iti ubhaya prakāram tatra yatas bhagavān jñātā kartā ca yadi api ca prakāśa vimarśa ātmakam cit eka ghanam ekam eva saṃvid rūpam tathā api vyutpādanāya tad parighaṭitaḥ eva ayam vibhāgaḥ tena jñāna ātmaka kriyā viṣayam svātantryam yadi api kriyāśakti rūpam tathā api tat jñāna adhikāraḥ eva nirṇetavyam tad viṣaya tvāt evam ca jñātṛ śabda arthaḥ prakṛtitaḥ pratyayataḥ ca saṃpūrṇa tayā nirṇītaḥ bhavati 
ĪPrVV_1,8.0^2	 tatra jñānam nāma svayaṃbhedita ābhāsa bheda upāśraya niyantraṇa asaṃkucitam aham iti saṃvedanam tatra ābhāseṣu yat svātantryam tat eva jñāna śakti viṣayam svātantryam saṃpadyate iti tātkālikā akṣasāmakṣya ityādinā śuddhe jñāna kriye yatas iti antena śloka ekā daśakena tat nirūpyate tatra abhāsa antara apekṣī ca ābhāsaḥ anyathā vā iti ślokena uktvā saḥ eva ābhāsaḥ ekaḥ iti śloka antareṇa ucyate artha kriyā ābhāsaḥ api tathā eva ābhāsa niyate iti śloka dvayena uktvā kasmin ābhāse sā artha kriyāḥ iti punar śloka dvayena ābhāsa antara vicitrita ābhāsa bhitti sthānīyam āntara tvam iti ślokena tatas bāhya tvam svarūpataḥ vibhāgataśva iti śloka yugmena tatas ślokena jñāna ādi śakti āśrayasya ekasya upasaṃhāraḥ śloka antareṇa maheśvara tvam upasaṃharatā bhāvinaḥ kriyā adhikārasya upakṣepaḥ iti saṅkṣepa arthaḥ āhnikasya atha śloka arthaḥ nirūpyate 
ĪPrVV_1,8.1	 nanu yadi parameśvara niṣṭhatayā eva samastaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ tat asya sphuṭa tva asphuṭa tva prāya prasiddha vaicitrya anupapattiḥ yena kila ayam anuprāṇitaḥ saḥ ekaḥ eva bhagavān na ca tad vyatirekeṇa vyavahārasya nijam kiṃcana tattvam utpaśyāmaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha tātkālikā kṣasā makṣya sāpekṣāḥ kevalam kvacid ābhāsāḥ anyathā anyatra tu andhā andhatama sa ādiṣu kevalam etāvatā ābhāsānām bhedaḥ na punar artha avabhāsasya sva ātma gataḥ kvacid api bhedaḥ iti śloka dvayasya saṃmelitasya saṃbandhaḥ yasmin= eva kāle saḥ ābhāsaḥ ābhāti tad kāle eva bhavati yat akṣa sāmakṣyam bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvam nāma ābhāsā antaram paśyāmi iti evaṃrūpam tad sāpekṣāḥ tad vyāmiśrāḥ kvacid ābhāsāḥ bhavanti yatra sphuṭa tā vyavahāraḥ andha viṣayaḥ andhakāra stha pramātṛ viṣayaḥ punar yaḥ anyaḥ vyavahāra usphuṭa tāmayaḥ tatra te ābhāsā anyathā tathā hi jāti andhasya bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tva lakṣaṇam ābhāsa antaram na eva asti dṛṣṭavataḥ tu andhībhūtasya saṃtamasa shtitasya ca tātkālikam tat na asti api tu prāktanam eva bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvam anusaṃdhatte 
ĪPrVV_1,8.2	 viśeṣaḥ artha avabhāsasya sattāyām na punar kvacid vikalpeṣu bhavet bhāvi bhavat bhūta artha gāmiṣu tasmāt artha avabhāsasya keṣucid api vikalpeṣu sattāyām svarūpe viśeṣaḥ asti iti saṃbhāvanā na kartavyā te hi vikalpāḥ bhāvi vaḥ tu gāminaḥ vā bhaviṣyan= iṣṭhāḥ vā bhavantu avrtamāna niṣṭhā vai atīta vastu viśrāntāḥ vā etat uktam bhavati nīlam idam paśyāmi saṅkalpayāmi utprekṣe smarāmi karomi vacmi ityādau nīla ābhāsaḥ asau svarūpataḥ anūna adhikaḥ evam paśyāmi iti api yaḥ pīta ādiṣu te punar ābhāsāḥ svātantryeṇa yadā bhagavatā saṃyojyante viyojyante ca tadā ayam sphuṭa tva ādiḥ vyavahāraḥ nīlam iti ābhāsasya utprekṣe iti ādi a ābhāsa antara vyavacchedanena paśyāmi iti ābhāsa vyāmiśraṇāyām sphuṭa tā vyavahāraḥ evam traikālika vyavahāra vaicitrya upapattiḥ parameśvara svarūpa antarbhūta tve punar ābhāsānām na kutaścid vyavacchedaḥ na kenacid vyāmiśraṇāḥ iti 
ĪPrVV_1,8.3	 nanu etat nīla ādiṣu upapadyatām yatra bāhya indriya vyāpāraḥ asti sukha ādau tu tad abhāvāt katham vaicitryam iti āśaṅkya āha sukha ādiṣu ca saukhya ādi hetuṣu api ca vastuṣu avabhāsasya sadbhāve api atīta tvāt tathā sthitiḥ sukhe sraj candana ādike ca tad kāraṇe duḥkhe ahikaṇṭaka ādau ca tad hetau atīte anāgate vā yadi api ābhāsaḥ saḥ eva tathā api atītam idam anāgatam idam iti ābhāsā antareṇa yatas vyāmiśraṇāḥ anubhavāmi iti ābhāsāt ca yatas vyavacchedaḥ tena vidyamāneṣu api teṣu tasya pramātuḥ tena prakāreṇa sthitiḥ na bhavati yathā pūrvan abhūt aham adhunā sukhaḥ duḥkhī iti samarjita tad tad nimita sāmagrīkaḥ vā iti 
ĪPrVV_1,8.4	 gāḍham ullikhyamāne tu vikalpena sukha ādike tathā sthitiḥ tathā eva syāt sphuṭam asya upalakṣaṇāt yadā tu vikalpena tāni vastūni bāḍham ullikhati tadā paunaḥpunya viśiṣṭa sukha tad hetu ullekhana abhidhāna kāraṇa ābhāsa anupraveśāt ābhāsa antara vyāmiśraṇa ātmanā tena eva asmad uktena prakāreṇa na punar anyena tathā iti sukhī aham iti ādikena sthitiḥ bhavati iti saṃbhāvyam ucitam etat yatas tadānīm sphuṭa tva ābhāsa miśram sukha ābhāsam upalakṣayati asau atīta grahaṇam bhāvinaḥ api upalakṣaṇam 
ĪPrVV_1,8.5^1	 nanu iyatā kim uktam bhavati bāhya rūpāḥ sraj a ādayaḥ sukha ādi hetavaḥ bāhya janitāḥ ca sukha ādayaḥ sukhyaham iti abhimāna hetavaḥ iti tatas ca bāhya tva abhāve tad janya tva abhāve ca na tathā uktam syāt tatra ca te eva na kecid tatas ca katham uktam artha avabhāsasya sattāyām na kvāpi viśeṣaḥ iti sattāyāḥ eva abhāvāt iti āśaṅkya āha bhāva abhāva avabhāsānām bāhyatā upādhiḥ iṣyate na ātmā sattā tatas teṣām āntarāṇām satām sadā 
ĪPrVV_1,8.5^2	 iha sukham asti mama duḥkham na asti mama iti ye bhāva ābhāsāḥ abhāva ābhāsāḥ ca teṣām bāhya tvam nāma ātmā svarūpam na bhavati na hi sukham iti asya svarūpam bāhyam iti vapuṣā bhāti sukhasya hi sukham eva sva rūpam kevalam bāhya tvam nāma abhāsa antaram īśvareṇa svātantrya balāt eva yadā tatra sukha ābhāse miśratayā bhāsyate tadā tat tasya upādhi rūpa tām uparañcaka tām viśeṣaṇa tvam gacchati tatas ca yathā nīla ābhāsa abhāve utpala ābhāsasya na kiṃcid vṛttam svarūpataḥ rāja ābhāsa abhāve vā puruṣa ābhāsasya tathā bāhya tva ābhāsa abhāve api sukha ābhāsasya duḥkha abhāva ābhāsasya kānta ābhāsasya ca na svarūpataḥ kācana mlānatā iti āntarāṇām sadā eva sthitiḥ eṣām 
ĪPrVV_1,8.6^1	 iha antaḥkaraṇe buddhi darpaṇa ātmani nīla ādīnām avabhāsānām āntara tvam api asti antaḥkaraṇam adhyebhava tvāt bāhya tvam api grāhyatā rūpam pramātuḥ vicchedena avabhāsāt bāhya tvam ca kevalam bāhya pratyakṣa tā atra ca avasthā dvaye api artha kriyām amī kurvanti eva antatas jñānam sva viṣayam yat punar pramātṛ tādātmya lakṣaṇam āntara tvam tatra amī katham na kāṃcid artha kriyām vidadhīran iti āśaṅkya āha āntara tvāt pramātṛ a aikye na eṣām bheda nibandhanāḥ artha kriyā api bāhya tve sā bhinna ābhāsa bhedataḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,8.6^2	 pramātra aikye iti tad nimittakam yat ānantara tvam tasmāt hetoḥ eṣām ābhāsānām artha kriyā na kācid asti sā hi artha kriyā bhede sati bhavati sa hi nīla ābhāsaḥ pīta ābhāsāt yatas bhidyate yatas ca pramātuḥ bhidyate tatas svena sādhyām bhinnam artha kriyām tasya pramātuḥ kuryāt na ca eṣa tadā bhede asti pramātra aikyāt sā hi artha kriyā ābhāsa bheda niyatā tathā ca kānta ābhāsasya bāhya tve api sati ābhāsā antarasya āliṅgana lakṣaṇasya vyapagame dūrībhavati iyam iti ca ābhāsa antarasya upagame anyā eva prāktana āhlāda viparītā dṛśyate artha kriyā atas ābhāsa bheda abhāvaḥ yatas pramātra aikya kṛte āntara tve tasmāt na artha kriyāḥ iti artha kriyā ābhāsaḥ api ca ābhāsā antaram eva iti artha kriyā kāritvam api na bhāvānām sattvam yena tad abhāve svarūpataḥ abhāvaḥ syāt 
ĪPrVV_1,8.7	 nanu ca bāhya ābhāsa vyatibhedana kāle āntara ābhāsaḥ virodhāt vicchinnaḥ iti katham idam uktam āntarāṇām yaḥ ābhāsaḥ sa sadā iti etat pariharati cit maya tve avabhāsānām antarā iva sthitiḥ sadā māyayā bhāsamānānām bāhya tvāt bahis api asau iha avabhāsānām sadā eva bāhya tā ābhāsa tada bhāvayoḥ api antarā iva pramātṛ prakāśaḥ eva sthitiḥ yatas ete cit mayāḥ anyathā na eva prakāśeran iti uktam yatas yadā tu māyā śaktyā viccheda avabhāsana svātantrya rūpayā bāhya tvam eṣām ābhāsyate tadā tat avalambya avabhāsamānānām asau sthitiḥ bahis api antar api na ayam antara ābhāsaḥ bāhya tvasya virodhaḥ pratyuta sarva ābhāsa bhitti bhūtaḥ asau tat katham virodhaḥ iti yuktam uktam sadā eva āntarāṇām sattā iti 
ĪPrVV_1,8.8	 nanu bāhya tve sati artha kriyā tat ca bāhya indriya gamya tvam na ca vikalpa ullikhitānām tat saṃbhavati tat katham amīṣām artha kriyā syāt dṛśyate ca vikalpa ullikhitaḥ piśāca ādiḥ trāsa ādi vidhāyī iti āśaṅkya āha vikalpe yaḥ ayam ullekhaḥ saḥ api bāhyaḥ pṛthak prathaḥ pramātṛ a aikātmyam āntaryam tatas bhedaḥ hi bāhya tā vimarśa viśeṣa rūpe vikalpa jñāne yaḥ ullikhyamānaḥ kāntā caura ādiḥ arthaḥ sa upi bāhyaḥ na kevalam bahis avalokyamānaḥ yasmāt saḥ api pramātuḥ sakāśāt pṛthak eva prathate ayam iti yat ca pramātari aham iti eva viśrānta tvam tat āntara tvam antar iti nikaṭam tat ca kiṃcid apekṣya apekṣaṇīyaḥ ca sarvatra pramātā eva apekṣaṇīya antaraa abhāve tatas ca pramātari nikaṭam tādātmya prāptam eva iti tatas yat bhinnam tat bāhyam eva iti yuktāḥ ullekhasya api artha kriyā 
ĪPrVV_1,8.9^1	 nanu kumbhakāra ādi vyāpāreṇa ghaṭa ādeḥ astu bāhya tvam antaḥkaraṇa gocarasya tu kim kṛtam tat iti āśaṅkyaḥ āha ullekhasya sukha ādeḥ ca prakāśaḥ bahis ātmanā icchātaḥ bhartuḥ adhyakṣa rūpaḥ akṣa ādi bhuvām yathā antar vikalpa pratibimba tasya nīla ādeḥ yaḥ bahis ātmanā pramātṛ vicchinnena svabhāvena prakāśaḥ sa bhartuḥ antarābhāsān bibhrataḥ bahis sṛṣṭim ca puṣṇataḥ īśvarasya eva icchayā yathā eva cakṣuḥ ādi viṣaya bhūtānām pratyakṣa jñāna śabda vācyaḥ bāhya ātmanā prakāśaḥ nīla ādīnām etat uktam bhavati kumbhakāra vyāpāraḥ nāma paramārthataḥ īśvara icchā eva tad abhāsita kāya spanda paryantā na punar anyaḥ kaścana saḥ tatas ca tathā īśvara icchayā prakāśāt avahiḥ bhūtā api nīla ādyā bāhya karaṇa gocarībhūtāḥ kalpitāt pramātuḥ vicchinna rūpa tvena bāhya tvena bhāsante tathā antaḥkaraṇa gocarībhūtāḥ api iti kaḥ viśeṣaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,8.9^2	 sukha duḥkha prāyāḥ tu bharata ādi ukta rūpāḥ sthāyi vī abhicāri rūpāḥ riti nirveda ādayaḥ antaḥkaraṇa eka gocarībhūtāḥ bahis ātmanā bhānti saṅkalpeṣu yadi api kṣetrajñasya eva svātantryam tathā api cit param ārtha tāyāḥ nyagbhāvayitum aśakya tvāt īśvarasya eva tat vastutas yathā uktam grantha kṛtā eva yadi api artha sthitiḥ prāṇa puryaṣṭaka niyantrite jīve niruddhā tatra api paramātmani sā sthitā tad ātmanā eva tasya syāt katham prāṇena yantraṇā iti yatra tu anicchoḥ eva kṣetrajñasya svarasa vāhi vyākṣepa sārā sāṅkalpikī sṛṣṭiḥ tatra sphuṭaḥ īśvarasya eva vyāpāraḥ tasmāt sa aṅkalpikānām api bahirbhāve parameśvaret chiava hetuḥ iti siddhāntaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,8.10	 adhunā pūrva uktam aikyam māheśvaryam ca nigamayati tad aikyena vinā na syāt saṃvidām loka paddhatiḥ prakāśa aikyāt tat eka tvam mātā ekaḥ saḥ iti sthitam yat etat pūrva uktena granthena upapāditam tat iti tasmāt hetoḥ saṃvidām jñānām aikyena vinā loka paddhatiḥ loka mārgaḥ sarvaḥ vyavahāraḥ na saṃbhavet saṃbhavati ca ayam tasmāt aikyam āsām na ca etat durghaṭam yatas viṣaya prakāśaḥ eva saṃvid ucyate kevalam viṣaya uparāga mahmnā bahirmukha tayā nīla prakāśaḥ anyaḥ pīta prakāśaḥ ca anyaḥ pramārthataḥ tu prakāśasya deśa kāla ākāra saṅkoca vaikalyāt eka tvam eva iti ekaḥ eva prakāśaḥ antar viśrāntaḥ saḥ eva ca pramātā ucyate iti sthitam idānīm upapattitaḥ 
ĪPrVV_1,8.11	 saḥ eva vimṛśat tvena niyatena maheśvaraḥ vimarśaḥ eva devasya śuddhe jñāna kriye yatas na ca asya asau prakāśa lakṣaṇaḥ sva ātmā nīla ādi uparāgaḥ ca parāmarśan śūnyaḥ eva āste sphaṭikramaḥ eḥ iva api tu sadā eva vimṛśyamāna rūpaḥ iti vimṛśat rūpa tvam anavacchinna vimarśatā ananya unmukha tvam ānanda eka ghana tvam tat eva asya māheśvaryam saḥ eva hi ahaṃbhāva ātmā vimarśaḥ devasya krīḍā ādi mayasya śuddhe pāramārthikyau jñāna kriye prakāśa rūpa tā jñānam tatra eva svātantrya ātmā vimarśaḥ kriyā vimarśaḥ ca antar kṛta prakāśaḥ iti vimarśaḥ eva para avasthāyām jñāna kriye parāpara avasthāyām tu bhagavat sadāśiva bhuvi idantā sāmāna adhikaraṇyā āpanna āhatā vimarśa svabhāve apara avasthāyām ca māyā pade idaṃbhāva prādhānyena vartamāne iti viśeṣaḥ sarvathā tu vimarśaḥ eva jñānam tena vinā hi jaḍa bhāvaḥ asya syāt iti uktam saḥ eva ca kriyāḥ iti bhāvinaḥ kriyā adhikārasya upakṣepam karoti
